# Theorem registry — canonical status

> Canonical, single-source-of-truth registry for every named
> theorem-style claim in the Context Zero / CoordPy programme.
> If this file disagrees with any other doc on the *status* of a
> claim, this file is right and the other file is stale.
>
> Status vocabulary (definitions in `docs/HOW_NOT_TO_OVERSTATE.md`):
>
> - **proved** — mathematical proof or proof-by-inspection.
> - **proved-conditional** — proof depends on a stated assumption.
> - **mechanically-checked** — runtime audit on every run; soundness by inspection.
> - **empirical** — measured on a published bench from a published seed.
> - **conjectural** — stated, falsifiable; not yet proved or systematically tested.
> - **retracted** — earlier reading withdrawn; replaced by a more honest reading.
>
> Last touched: post-W80 W81 P1-Blocker Attack (Deployable Substrate Gateway / Sequence-Conditioned Learned Consolidation / Learned Multi-Runtime Economics / Differentiable Memory Substrate / Adversarial Consensus & Repair) milestone added 2026-05-18; post-W79 W80 P0-Blocker Attack (Frontier-Quality Local Runtime / Runtime Instrumentation Contract / Second-Backend Parity Matrix / Living Capability Matrix / Live Local-Model Evaluation) milestone added 2026-05-18; post-W78 W79 Stronger Direct-Blocker-Attack / Replacement-Then-Restart-After-Long-Delay / Controlled-Runtime Substrate / OpenAI-Compatible-Façade / Learned-Consolidation Budget-Primary Two-Plane Multi-Agent Substrate Programme milestone added 2026-05-17; post-W77 W78 Stronger Less-Bounded Long-Horizon Reconstruction / Bounded-Window-Falsifier Budget-Primary Two-Plane Multi-Agent Substrate Programme milestone added 2026-05-17; (older milestones — see git log).

## W81 P1-Blocker Attack — Deployable Substrate Gateway / Sequence-Conditioned Learned Consolidation / Learned Multi-Runtime Economics / Differentiable Memory Substrate / Adversarial Consensus & Repair (W81-T-* and W81-L-*)

| Claim | One-line description | Status | Code/proof anchor |
| ----- | -------------------- | ------ | ------------------ |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-ROUTES | The W81 deployable substrate gateway V1 implements 7 OpenAI-shaped + substrate-side-channel routes and supports both programmatic dispatch and a real `http.server`-bound TCP listener | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/deployable_substrate_gateway_v1.py:W81_GATEWAY_ROUTES`, `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_serves_over_real_http_transport` |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-CONTENT-ADDRESSED | Identical request bodies through identical gateway configs produce identical request CIDs and identical response CIDs, even across independent gateway instances | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_content_addressing` |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-AUTH-SHIM | When `bearer_token` is set in `GatewayConfigV1`, requests missing the matching `Authorization: Bearer <token>` header are rejected with HTTP 401 on every protected route; `/healthz` remains unauthenticated by design | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_auth_rejects_missing_token` and siblings |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-SUBSTRATE-SIDE-CHANNEL-EXPLICIT | Substrate side-channel returns from `/v1/chat/completions` are opt-in (`substrate_options.return_side_channel`) and can be globally disabled at gateway-config time via `allow_substrate_side_channel=False` | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_substrate_side_channel_can_be_locked_down` |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-REPLAY-BYTE-IDENTICAL | The `/v1/substrate/replay` endpoint produces final-token logits whose max abs diff vs full-recompute is < 1e-8 on the in-repo NumPy controlled runtime | empirical | `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_substrate_replay_is_byte_identical` |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-CONFORMANCE-PASSES-12 | `/v1/substrate/conformance` runs the W80 instrumentation conformance suite on the gateway's controlled runtime; reports n_pass=12, n_fail=0 | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_substrate_conformance_passes_12_axes` |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-END-TO-END-BENCH | `run_gateway_end_to_end_bench_v1()` routes one chat completion + one substrate forward + one substrate replay + one conformance run through the gateway and produces a content-addressed end-to-end report | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/deployable_substrate_gateway_v1.py:run_gateway_end_to_end_bench_v1`, `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_end_to_end_bench` |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-OPENAI-SDK-COMPAT | The real `openai.OpenAI` Python SDK with `base_url` pointed at the gateway successfully round-trips `client.chat.completions.create(...)` and receives a strict-schema-valid response (logprobs is null, choices[].message.role is "assistant", object is "chat.completion") | empirical | `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_openai_sdk_round_trip` |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-SYSTEM-FINGERPRINT | The chat-completion response carries an OpenAI-shape `system_fingerprint` field deterministically derived from the runtime params CID; identical runtime params produce identical fingerprints | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_chat_completion_has_system_fingerprint` |
| W81-T-GATEWAY-V1-STREAM-HONEST | `stream=true` requests are answered with a single non-streaming JSON body carrying `streaming_supported=false` AND `stream_requested=true` so the caller knows their intent was received and explicitly not honored | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_deployable_substrate_gateway.py::test_w81_gateway_stream_true_returns_non_streaming_body` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-DETERMINISTIC | Identical seeds + data + hyperparams produce identical fitted-module CIDs in `train_sequence_conditioned_consolidation_module` | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_learned_consolidation_v2.py::test_w81_v2_training_deterministic_on_seed` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-CONVERGES | Training the V2 sequence-conditioned consolidation module on the synthetic temporal-integration dataset strictly reduces loss; `post_loss < pre_loss` and `converged=True` | empirical | `coordpy/learned_consolidation_v2.py:train_sequence_conditioned_consolidation_module`, `tests/test_w81_learned_consolidation_v2.py::test_w81_v2_training_reduces_loss` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-BEATS-RIDGE | On the W81 sequential reconstruction dataset, V2 strictly beats closed-form pointwise ridge regression | empirical | `tests/test_w81_learned_consolidation_v2.py::test_w81_v2_beats_ridge_on_sequential_task` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-BEATS-V1 | V2 sequence-conditioned recurrent model strictly beats W79's V1 pointwise two-layer nonlinear head on the same sequential reconstruction dataset | empirical | `tests/test_w81_learned_consolidation_v2.py::test_w81_v2_beats_v1_pointwise_head` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-BEATS-BOUNDED-WINDOW | V2 strictly beats a k=2 bounded-window ridge baseline that cannot see history past 2 timesteps | empirical | `tests/test_w81_learned_consolidation_v2.py::test_w81_v2_beats_bounded_window_baseline` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-PLUGS-INTO-LHR-V2 | V2 plugs into the W79 long-horizon-reconstruction carrier V2 via `attach_v2_to_long_horizon_carrier` / `build_v2_carrier_slots`; V2-populated `learned_slots` content-address against the V2 module CID and the carrier entries, with no schema change | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/learned_consolidation_v2.py:attach_v2_to_long_horizon_carrier`, `tests/test_w81_learned_consolidation_v2.py::test_w81_v2_plugs_into_long_horizon_reconstruction_carrier` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-CARRIER-SLOTS-DETERMINISTIC | Identical V2 module CIDs + identical carrier entries produce byte-identical slot CIDs when populated via `build_v2_carrier_slots` | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_learned_consolidation_v2.py::test_w81_v2_carrier_slots_deterministic` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-ECONOMICS-V1-ACTIONS | The W81 learned economics controller V1 supports exactly 5 canonical actions (`replay`, `runtime_recompute`, `transcript_recompute`, `promote_to_richer_substrate`, `abstain`) and a 7-dim feature schema | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/learned_economics_controller_v1.py:W81_ECONOMICS_ACTIONS`, `tests/test_w81_learned_economics_controller.py::test_w81_economics_actions_are_canonical` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-ECONOMICS-V1-BEATS-HEURISTIC | On the held-out W81 economics evaluation set, the trained learned controller's mean utility strictly exceeds the hand-built heuristic baseline's mean utility | empirical | `tests/test_w81_learned_economics_controller.py::test_w81_economics_learned_beats_heuristic_on_utility` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-ECONOMICS-V1-CLOSER-TO-OPTIMAL | The learned controller's optimality gap (vs the simulation's optimal action) is strictly smaller than the heuristic baseline's optimality gap | empirical | `tests/test_w81_learned_economics_controller.py::test_w81_economics_learned_closer_to_optimal_than_heuristic` |
| W81-T-LEARNED-ECONOMICS-V1-NO-COLLAPSE | The learned controller uses at least 3 of the 5 canonical actions on the eval set — i.e. it does not collapse onto a single action | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_learned_economics_controller.py::test_w81_economics_action_distribution_uses_all_actions` |
| W81-T-DIFFERENTIABLE-MEMORY-V1-SLOT-WRITES | The W81 differentiable memory substrate V1 writes to its K addressable slots during the forward pass; final-snapshot slot magnitudes are strictly non-trivial | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_differentiable_memory_substrate.py::test_w81_diffmem_slot_accumulation_nonzero` |
| W81-T-DIFFERENTIABLE-MEMORY-V1-BEATS-V2 | On the W81 delayed-recall task, V1 slot-based attention memory beats V2 single-state recurrent memory (V2 hidden_dim 8 ≪ V1 K*D_mem = 128) | empirical | `tests/test_w81_differentiable_memory_substrate.py::test_w81_diffmem_v1_beats_v2_on_content_addressed_recall` |
| W81-T-DIFFERENTIABLE-MEMORY-V1-BEATS-RIDGE | On the same delayed-recall task, V1 strictly beats closed-form pointwise ridge | empirical | `tests/test_w81_differentiable_memory_substrate.py::test_w81_diffmem_v1_beats_ridge_on_recall` |
| W81-T-DIFFERENTIABLE-MEMORY-V1-COMPRESSED-SNAPSHOT-CID | The final K-slot state is content-addressed via `compressed_snapshot_cid(X=...)`; identical inputs produce identical CIDs and different inputs produce different CIDs | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_differentiable_memory_substrate.py::test_w81_diffmem_compressed_snapshot_cid_stable` and sibling |
| W81-T-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-FOUR-DECISION-KINDS | V1 adversarial consensus has exactly 4 canonical decision kinds (`commit`, `abstain`, `escalate_to_richer_substrate`, `replay_from_trusted`) | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/adversarial_consensus_repair_v1.py:W81_DECISION_KINDS`, `tests/test_w81_adversarial_consensus_repair.py::test_w81_consensus_decision_kinds_are_canonical` |
| W81-T-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-DELAY-DECAY | A witness arriving `delay_halflife * k` timesteps late has approximately `2^-k` of the trust of an on-time witness with the same value | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_adversarial_consensus_repair.py::test_w81_consensus_delayed_witnesses_have_lower_trust` |
| W81-T-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-CORRUPTION-DETECTION | A single adversarial witness whose value is far from the cluster receives < 10% of the typical honest witness's trust score after the corruption penalty | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_adversarial_consensus_repair.py::test_w81_consensus_corruption_penalty_drops_adversary_trust` |
| W81-T-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-BEATS-NAIVE-BENCH | On the W81 adversarial bench (n=7 witnesses, f=2 adversarial, 80 seeds), V1's mean error strictly beats naive averaging AND V1 wins on ≥ 80% of seeds | empirical | `coordpy/adversarial_consensus_repair_v1.py:run_adversarial_consensus_bench_v1`, `tests/test_w81_adversarial_consensus_repair.py::test_w81_consensus_v1_strictly_beats_naive_on_bench` |
| W81-T-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-COMPETITIVE-WITH-MEDIAN | V1 beats the median estimator on ≥ 40% of seeds — i.e. V1 is competitive with the standard robust baseline AND adds explicit abstain / escalate / replay routing | empirical | `tests/test_w81_adversarial_consensus_repair.py::test_w81_consensus_v1_competitive_with_median` |
| W81-T-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-AUDIT-CHAIN-CONTENT-ADDRESSED | Identical witness sets + identical configs produce identical audit CIDs; different witness values produce different audit CIDs | mechanically-checked | `tests/test_w81_adversarial_consensus_repair.py::test_w81_consensus_decision_audit_chain_is_content_addressed` |
| W81-L-GATEWAY-V1-LOCAL-MODEL-ONLY-CAP | The gateway routes to `controlled_runtime_substrate_v1` (in-repo NumPy runtime); it does NOT pierce third-party hosted-model substrate | limitation | `coordpy/deployable_substrate_gateway_v1.py` |
| W81-L-GATEWAY-V1-AUTH-SIMPLE-CAP | The auth shim is a bearer-token equality check; it is NOT a full OAuth / signed-JWT story | limitation | `coordpy/deployable_substrate_gateway_v1.py:GatewayConfigV1` |
| W81-L-GATEWAY-V1-NO-STREAMING-CAP | V1 does NOT implement Server-Sent-Events streaming; `stream=true` requests are answered with a non-streaming JSON body carrying `streaming_supported=false` | limitation | `coordpy/deployable_substrate_gateway_v1.py:_handle_chat_completions` |
| W81-L-GATEWAY-V1-NO-TLS-CAP | V1 binds plain HTTP; TLS is out of V1 scope (deploy behind a reverse proxy for TLS) | limitation | `coordpy/deployable_substrate_gateway_v1.py:serve_forever` |
| W81-L-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-TINY-CAP | V2 uses hidden_dim 32 / memory_dim 16 / 60 train iters by default; not GPU-backed | limitation | `coordpy/learned_consolidation_v2.py` |
| W81-L-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-SYNTHETIC-CAP | V2 trains on synthetic temporal-integration sequences; live-runtime hidden-state coupling is W81 P1 #19 follow-on / not V2's job | limitation | `coordpy/learned_consolidation_v2.py` |
| W81-L-LEARNED-CONSOLIDATION-V2-RESEARCH-ONLY-CAP | V2 is explicit-import only; not on the stable public surface | limitation | `coordpy/learned_consolidation_v2.py` |
| W81-L-LEARNED-ECONOMICS-V1-SUPERVISED-CAP | V1 is supervised on a synthetic optimal-action dataset; not full policy-gradient RL on a live runtime | limitation | `coordpy/learned_economics_controller_v1.py` |
| W81-L-LEARNED-ECONOMICS-V1-SIMULATED-COSTS-CAP | V1's cost/quality model is the deterministic synthetic one declared in `EconomicsSimulationV1`; live-runtime cost/quality validation is W81 follow-on work | limitation | `coordpy/learned_economics_controller_v1.py:EconomicsSimulationV1` |
| W81-L-DIFFERENTIABLE-MEMORY-V1-TINY-CAP | V1 uses hidden_dim 24, memory_dim 16, K_slots 8, T 12 by default; NumPy CPU only | limitation | `coordpy/differentiable_memory_substrate_v1.py` |
| W81-L-DIFFERENTIABLE-MEMORY-V1-NOT-ON-MAIN-SCOREBOARD-CAP | V1 does NOT displace the W56..W79 synthetic-substrate wins; it is a new differentiable-memory line, not a replacement for the ridge-heavy outer controller | limitation | `coordpy/differentiable_memory_substrate_v1.py` |
| W81-L-DIFFERENTIABLE-MEMORY-V1-SYNTHETIC-CAP | V1's win is on the W81 synthetic delayed-recall task; no live local-model evidence yet | limitation | `coordpy/differentiable_memory_substrate_v1.py` |
| W81-L-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-SCALAR-EVIDENCE-CAP | V1 fuses scalar / fixed-shape vector evidence; structured-string consensus is out of V1 scope | limitation | `coordpy/adversarial_consensus_repair_v1.py` |
| W81-L-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-EMPIRICAL-BOUNDS-CAP | The adversarial-robustness claim is empirical (validated on the W81 bench family); it is not yet derived as a closed-form analytical theorem | limitation | `coordpy/adversarial_consensus_repair_v1.py` |
| W81-L-ADV-CONSENSUS-V1-NOT-ON-MAIN-SCOREBOARD-CAP | V1 does not replace the W56..W79 consensus controllers; it is a new line, not a drop-in upgrade | limitation | `coordpy/adversarial_consensus_repair_v1.py` |

## W80 P0-Blocker Attack — Frontier-Quality Local Runtime / Runtime Instrumentation Contract / Second-Backend Parity Matrix / Living Capability Matrix / Live Local-Model Evaluation (W80-T-* and W80-L-*)

| Claim | One-line description | Status | Code/proof anchor |
| ----- | -------------------- | ------ | ------------------ |
| W80-T-INSTRUMENTATION-CONTRACT-V1-AXES-COUNT | The W80 runtime instrumentation contract defines exactly 12 canonical axes partitioned into 5 read, 4 write, and 3 witness axes | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/runtime_instrumentation_v1.py:W80_INSTRUMENTATION_AXES_ALL`, `tests/test_w80_runtime_instrumentation.py::test_w80_instrumentation_contract_schema_versioned` |

| W80-T-CONTROLLED-RUNTIME-NUMPY-CONFORMS | The W79 in-repo NumPy controlled runtime adapts cleanly into the W80 contract; conformance suite reports 12 pass, 0 fail, 0 skip | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/runtime_instrumentation_v1.py:ControlledRuntimeInstrumentationAdapterV1`, `tests/test_w80_runtime_instrumentation.py::test_w80_controlled_runtime_adapter_passes_conformance` |
| W80-T-TRANSFORMERS-RUNTIME-V1-LOADS-DISTILGPT2 | The HF transformers runtime V1 loads `distilbert/distilgpt2` and exposes its canonical config (6 layers × 12 heads × hidden 768, head_dim 64) | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/transformers_runtime_v1.py:TransformersRuntimeV1`, `tests/test_w80_transformers_runtime.py::test_w80_transformers_runtime_loads_distilgpt2` |
| W80-T-TRANSFORMERS-RUNTIME-V1-DETERMINISTIC | The HF transformers runtime forward is deterministic on identical (model bytes, input bytes) in fp32 on CPU; trace CIDs match | empirical | `coordpy/transformers_runtime_v1.py:TransformersRuntimeV1.forward`, `tests/test_w80_transformers_runtime.py::test_w80_transformers_runtime_deterministic_forward` |

| W80-T-PARITY-MATRIX-V1-TWO-BACKENDS | The runtime parity matrix V1 includes two controlled backends (in-repo NumPy + HF transformers) and both pass conformance | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/runtime_parity_matrix_v1.py:build_runtime_parity_matrix_v1`, `tests/test_w80_parity_matrix.py::test_w80_parity_matrix_with_transformers_has_two_backends` |

| W80-T-CAPABILITY-MATRIX-V1-LIVING | Two consecutive builds of the capability matrix produce different refreshed_at_ns timestamps and different matrix CIDs while preserving the hosted-boundary V12 CID | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/capability_matrix_v1.py:build_capability_matrix_v1`, `tests/test_w80_capability_matrix.py::test_w80_capability_matrix_is_living` |

| W80-T-R201-32-H-BARS-ALL-PASS | R-201 ships 32 H-bars (H1400..H1431) covering the live-runtime conformance set + cross-backend mechanism deltas + task success / answer consistency / visible-token / recompute-cost honest metrics + substrate adapter V25 integration; all pass on `distilbert/distilgpt2` | empirical | `coordpy/r201_benchmark.py:run_r201`, `tests/test_w80_r201_live_local_model.py::test_w80_r201_all_pass_against_live_model` |

| W80-T-R201-TASK-SUCCESS-UNAMBIGUOUS | The live runtime produces a non-empty greedy completion whose final-position top-1 logit beats top-2 by >= 0.1 — i.e. unambiguous, not a near-tie | empirical | `tests/test_w80_r201_live_local_model.py::test_w80_r201_task_success_completion_unambiguous` |
| W80-T-R201-XBACK-REPLAY-DELTA | The replay-from-KV mechanism transfers across backends: the in-repo NumPy runtime achieves diff < 1e-8, the HF transformers runtime achieves diff < 5e-3 — both byte-identical at their respective precision targets | empirical | `tests/test_w80_r201_live_local_model.py::test_w80_r201_cross_backend_replay_delta` |
| W80-T-SUBSTRATE-ADAPTER-V25-EXTENDS-V24 | Substrate adapter V25 strictly extends V24 by adding the W80 HF transformers backend as a first-class entry inside the existing adapter line; V24 matrix CID is preserved for tamper-evident chaining | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/substrate_adapter_v25.py:probe_all_v25_adapters`, `tests/test_w80_substrate_adapter_v25.py::test_w80_substrate_adapter_v25_matrix_extends_v24` |
| W80-T-SUBSTRATE-ADAPTER-V25-HF-TIER | When transformers + torch are installed, the V25 HF backend hits the `controlled_runtime_substrate_v1` tier and exposes the seven W79 controlled-runtime axes via the V24 yes/no scheme | mechanically-checked | `coordpy/substrate_adapter_v25.py:probe_transformers_runtime_v1_adapter`, `tests/test_w80_substrate_adapter_v25.py::test_w80_substrate_adapter_v25_records_hf_when_available` |

| W80-L-TRANSFORMERS-V1-NOT-FRONTIER-MODEL-CAP | distilgpt2 is still NOT a frontier model. The load-bearing W80 claim is that the contract works on a real pretrained transformer, not that distilgpt2 is competitive at scale | limitation | `coordpy/transformers_runtime_v1.py` |

| W80-L-PARITY-MATRIX-V1-TRANSFORMERS-OPTIONAL-CAP | Building the matrix without transformers installed produces a one-runtime matrix + a "transformers unavailable" probe entry; CI stays deterministic | limitation | `coordpy/runtime_parity_matrix_v1.py` |
| W80-L-CAPABILITY-MATRIX-V1-LIVING-CAP | V1 *re-probes* on every build call; it is not a static snapshot. Refreshed-at timestamps make this explicit | limitation | `coordpy/capability_matrix_v1.py` |
| W80-L-CAPABILITY-MATRIX-V1-HOSTED-WALL-PRESERVED-CAP | The W79 frontier-blocked-axes set is forwarded unchanged | limitation | `coordpy/capability_matrix_v1.py` |

| W80-L-R201-LIVE-NOT-FRONTIER-CAP | distilgpt2 is not a frontier model — the load-bearing claim is the contract works on a real pretrained transformer | limitation | `coordpy/r201_benchmark.py` |

| **W62-L-NO-THIRD-PARTY-SUBSTRATE-COUPLING-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **Hosted backends (Ollama, OpenAI-compatible) remain text-only on the HTTP surface; W62 makes no claim of third-party transformer-internal access.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem (W56..W62 carry forward unchanged)** | `coordpy.substrate_adapter.probe_ollama_adapter` returns `text_only` tier on every observable Ollama backend; `probe_openai_compatible_adapter` ditto. |
| **W62-L-V7-NO-AUTOGRAD-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **W62 fits ONLY twelve closed-form linear ridge solves (seven from W61 + five new): cache controller V5 two-objective stacked; cache controller V5 trained-repair; cache controller V5 composite_v5; replay controller V3 per-regime head × 4 regimes; replay controller V3 hidden-vs-KV 3-class classifier. NO end-to-end backprop, NO autograd, NO GPU.** | **proved-by-inspection limitation theorem** | `fit_two_objective_ridge_v5`, `fit_corruption_repair_head_v5`, `fit_composite_v5`, `fit_replay_controller_v3_per_regime`, `fit_hidden_vs_kv_regime_classifier`. |
| **W62-L-NUMPY-CPU-V7-SUBSTRATE-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The V7 substrate is 9 layers / d_model=64 / byte-vocab / max_len=128 / untrained NumPy on CPU. NOT a frontier model.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `coordpy.tiny_substrate_v7.TinyV7SubstrateConfig` defaults. |
| **W62-L-V14-OUTER-NOT-TRAINED-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The V14 outer wrapper adds one carrier (replay-dominance EMA) but does NOT train the V13 outer GRU end-to-end.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `step_persistent_state_v14` only EMAs the new carrier. |
| **W62-L-ECC-V14-RATE-FLOOR-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **Structural rate ceiling log2(2^23) = 23 raw data bits per segment-tuple. 4096-bit/token target reproduces this cap as H170c.** | **mechanically-checked** | `probe_ecc_v14_rate_floor_falsifier`. |
| **W62-L-V14-LHR-SCORER-FIT-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The V14 four-layer scorer's first three layers (random+ReLU, random+tanh, random+tanh-2) are FROZEN; only the final ridge head is fit.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `fit_lhr_v14_four_layer_scorer`. |
| **W62-L-V6-PREFIX-DRIFT-CURVE-LINEAR-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The prefix V6 drift-curve predictor is a linear ridge on a 3-d segment-configuration feature stacked across K target steps; it does NOT model token-content-conditional drift.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `fit_prefix_drift_curve_predictor`. |
| **W62-L-V6-CACHE-CONTROLLER-NO-AUTOGRAD-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **Cache controller V5 fits three new heads via closed-form ridge: two-objective (n_features × 2), trained-repair (4-dim), composite_v5 (6-vector mixture). No autograd.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `fit_two_objective_ridge_v5` + `fit_corruption_repair_head_v5` + `fit_composite_v5`. |
| **W62-L-V3-REPLAY-NO-AUTOGRAD-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **Replay controller V3 fits 4 closed-form 6×4 ridge heads (one per regime) + a nearest-centroid regime gate + a 5×3 ridge hidden-vs-KV classifier. No autograd.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `fit_replay_controller_v3_per_regime` + `fit_hidden_vs_kv_regime_classifier`. |
| **W62-L-V6-HSB-NO-AUTOGRAD-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **HSB V6 three-target stack fit delegates to V5's worst-residual column reduction. No new gradient descent.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `fit_hsb_v6_three_target`. |
| **W62-L-V6-ATTN-NO-AUTOGRAD-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **V6 attention-steering is a two-stage clip (coarse L1-mass + fine per-(L,H,Q,K) KL); no autograd.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `steer_attention_and_measure_v6`. |
| **W62-L-MULTI-HOP-V12-SYNTHETIC-BACKENDS-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The 20 multi-hop backends are NAMED, not EXECUTED. V12 is a graph + trust arbiter, not a real multi-machine harness.** | **proved-by-inspection (carries forward from W61-L-MULTI-HOP-V11-CAP)** | `evaluate_dec_chain_len17_fidelity` body. |
| **W62-L-CRC-V10-FINGERPRINT-SYNTHETIC-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The 1024-bucket fingerprint is wrap-around XOR over the in-repo substrate cache, not third-party hosted cache state.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `kv_cache_fingerprint_1024`. |
| **W62-L-CONSENSUS-V8-REPAIR-STAGE-SYNTHETIC-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The trained_repair stage applies an additive repair correction; it does NOT un-corrupt the raw cached state.** | **proved-by-inspection** | `ConsensusFallbackControllerV8.decide_v8`. |
| W62-C-FRONTIER-SCALE-V7-SUBSTRATE-LIFT (conjecture) | If frontier-scale runtimes exposed compatible hooks (per-(layer, head, slot) cache-write ledger; per-layer logit-lens; per-(layer, head, position) attention-receive delta; per-(layer, head) replay-trust EMA) the W62 mechanism stack would scale-monotonically improve usefulness | conjectural | open question; W62 ships only the in-repo V7 runtime. |
| W62-C-PER-REGIME-REPLAY-DOMINANCE-GENERALISES (conjecture) | The per-regime ridge + nearest-centroid pattern generalises to richer regimes (transcript-replay, hidden-state corruption, attention-pattern compromise, multi-hop substrate transfer) | conjectural | W62 implements 4 regimes; the framework extends to more. |

V11 is a graph + trust arbiter, not a real multi-machine harness.** | **proved-by-inspection (carries forward from W60-L-MULTI-HOP-V10-CAP)** | `evaluate_dec_chain_len16_fidelity` body. |
| W61-C-FRONTIER-SCALE-SUBSTRATE-LIFT (conjecture) | If frontier-scale runtimes exposed compatible hooks (per-(layer, position, d_key) cache keys; per-(layer, head) hidden-write trace; per-(layer, position) replay-age; bilinear retrieval head fitting; trained replay thresholds) the W61 mechanism stack would scale-monotonically improve usefulness | conjectural | open question; W61 ships only the in-repo V6 runtime. |
| W61-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (conjecture) | The substrate-coupling pattern (V6 + V5 bridges + V4 cache + V2 replay + V5 attention + V6 hybrid) generalises to frontier transformer architectures with comparable internal surfaces | conjectural | carries forward W56..W60 line; W61 deepens the in-repo evidence but does not test on frontier models. |

## W58 Deep Cache-Reuse Substrate-Coupled Latent Operating System (W58-T-* and W58-L-* / W58-C-*)

| Claim | One-line description | Status | Code/proof anchor |
| ----- | -------------------- | ------ | ------------------ |

## Cross-role cohort-coherence multi-agent coordination (W7-1 .. W7-3) — SDK v3.8

| Claim                | Description                                                                                                                                                                         | Status                            | Anchor                                                                                                |
| -------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **W7-1 (SDK v3.8)**  | **FIFO unbeatability under low surplus: when the producer's emission stream satisfies ``|candidates(scenario)| ≤ K_role`` for every scenario in the bench, every fixed admission policy (FIFO, claim_priority, coverage_guided, cohort_coherence, learned) is permutation-equivalent to ``admit_all``; ``structure_gain`` over substrate FIFO is identically zero by construction.** Phase-53 default config (``mean_n_admitted_auditor < K_auditor=4`` in every regime) is the empirical anchor in the *positive* direction. | **proved-empirical**              | `docs/data/phase53_scale_vs_structure_K4_n5.json`; `phase53_scale_vs_structure.py`                    |
| **W7-1-aux (SDK v3.8)** | **Streaming cohort-coherence admission is unstable under candidate-arrival permutation: under a stream where the first auditor-routed candidate carries a foreign-service tag, ``CohortCoherenceAdmissionPolicy(fixed_plurality_tag=None)`` admits the foreign tag and rejects every subsequent gold-tag candidate, producing ``mean_n_admitted_auditor`` strictly less than the gold cohort size.** On Phase-54 default, streaming cohort ties FIFO at ``accuracy_full = 0.000`` across 10/10 scenarios. | **W7-2 (SDK v3.8)**  | **Cross-role cohort-coherence structural win under gold-plurality: when the candidate stream satisfies the gold-plurality property (gold service tag has strictly more auditor-routed candidates than any decoy service tag) AND ``|candidates| > K_auditor``, the buffered ``CohortCoherenceAdmissionPolicy`` (constructed via ``from_candidate_payloads``) achieves ``accuracy_full = 1.000`` while substrate FIFO, ``CapsuleFifoAdmissionPolicy``, ``ClaimPriorityAdmissionPolicy``, ``CoverageGuidedAdmissionPolicy``, and the streaming cohort variant all produce ``accuracy_full = 0.000``. | **W7-2-conditional (SDK v3.8)** | **W7-2 holds iff K_auditor is in the structure-win window: ``gold_count_min ≤ K_auditor < min(K_auditor+1, total_candidates)``. The Phase-54 budget sweep observes ``+0.400`` gap at K∈{2,3} (gold cohort partially fits) and ``+1.000`` gap at K∈{4,5,6,8} (gold cohort fully fits; foreign-service decoys filtered out by cohort regardless of K). | **W7-3 (SDK v3.8)**  | **Extraction floor (proved-negative): no per-role admission policy (FIFO, priority, coverage, learned, streaming or buffered cohort coherence) can recover a missing causal claim that the producer never emitted into the candidate stream. Proof: ``capsule_role_view.parents`` is constructed from ledger CIDs (Capsule Contract C5); a never-emitted claim has no CID; therefore no ROLE_VIEW can include it.** Empirical anchor: Phase-53 ``deadlock_pool_exhaustion`` 1/5 miss across all 5 admission strategies in every model regime; ``DEADLOCK_SUSPECTED`` is never emitted by 14B / 35B from role-local events. Implication: separates admission-fixable failures from extraction-fixable failures; the producer's claim coverage is a strict upper bound on every downstream admission strategy. | **proved-negative**               | Capsule Contract C5; `docs/data/phase53_scale_vs_structure_K4_n5.json` (failure_hist on `deadlock_pool_exhaustion`) |

## Bundle-aware team decoder (W10-Λ, W10-1..W10-4) — SDK v3.11

| Claim                | Description                                                                                                                                                                         | Status                            | Anchor                                                                                                |
| -------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **W10-Λ (SDK v3.11)** | **Service-blind admission structural limit on R-57: on the Phase-57 default bank (multi-service-gold + corroborated-decoy via non-causal claim_kinds), every admission policy in the SDK whose state is a function of the (role, tag) bipartite multiset alone — `FifoAdmissionPolicy`, `ClaimPriorityAdmissionPolicy`, `CoverageGuidedAdmissionPolicy`, `CohortCoherenceAdmissionPolicy` (W7-2), `CrossRoleCorroborationAdmissionPolicy` (W8), `MultiServiceCorroborationAdmissionPolicy` (W9) — achieves `accuracy_full = 0.000` and `accuracy_services = 0.000` under the decoder's set-equality `services_correct` check. The bipartite multiset for the corroborated decoy is observationally indistinguishable from at least one gold service's bipartite multiset; no service-blind policy can prefer one over the other.** | **proved-empirical (n=10) + structural sketch** | `docs/data/phase57_decoder_K8_n10.json::pooled` (every admission policy at 0.000); `docs/data/phase57_seed_sweep.json` (5/5 seeds reproduce); `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py` (each policy's state shape). |
| **W10-1 (SDK v3.11)** | **Bundle-aware decoder sufficiency: pairing the SDK v3.10 W9 admission policy (`top_k = 3`, `min_corroborated_roles = 2`) with `BundleAwareTeamDecoder(cck_filter=True, role_corroboration_floor=1, fallback_admitted_size_threshold=2)` achieves `accuracy_full = 1.000` on Phase-57 default (K_auditor=8, T_auditor=256, n_eval=10, bank_seed=11), stable across 5/5 alternate bank seeds (11, 17, 23, 29, 31). Headline gap = +1.000 vs every admission-only baseline, +1.000 vs SDK v3.10 W9. The first capsule-native multi-agent coordination method that crosses the admission/decoding split.** | **proved-empirical (n=50 saturated)** | `docs/data/phase57_decoder_K8_n10.json`; `docs/data/phase57_seed_sweep.json`; `Phase57DefaultConfigTests::test_bundle_decoder_strictly_beats_w9_at_K8` |
| **W10-2 (SDK v3.11)** | **CCK structural correctness (proved by inspection): for every `root_cause` label `R` in `CAUSAL_CLAIM_KINDS_PER_ROOT_CAUSE`, (a) `CCK[R]` is non-empty iff `R` is a specific-tier root_cause (data / storage / compute / edge / network); (b) `CCK[R]` is empty for `unknown` (no filter); (c) for the generic-tier root_causes `error_spike` and `latency_spike`, `CCK[R] = {ERROR_RATE_SPIKE, LATENCY_SPIKE}` (the bundle decoder is a no-op on generic-tier root_causes, by design — this is the named scope limit of W10-1).** | **proved (by inspection)**            | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::CAUSAL_CLAIM_KINDS_PER_ROOT_CAUSE`; `BundleAwareTeamDecoder.decode`. |
| **W10-3 (SDK v3.11)** | **Backward-compat with W7-2 / W8 / W9 on R-54 / R-55 / R-56 (proved-empirical n=10 each): the bundle-aware decoder paired with the corresponding admission policy (W7-2 buffered cohort on R-54, W8 corroboration on R-55, W9 multi-service on R-56) achieves the same `accuracy_full` (1.000) and the same `services` set as the prior best capsule strategy on every cell of every prior regime. The `fallback_admitted_size_threshold = 2` knob is the load-bearing piece: when admission has produced a small dominant set (size ≤ 2), the decoder trusts admission rather than re-filtering. Without the fallback, the decoder slips by 0.20 on Phase-56 `slow_query_web_db` scenarios where one gold service is mentioned only via non-CCK kinds.** | **proved-empirical (n=10 each)**      | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_BUNDLE_DECODER.md` § 3 backward-compat probe; `Phase57BackwardCompatTests::test_bundle_decoder_matches_w9_on_phase56`, `..._matches_w8_on_phase55`, `..._matches_w7_2_on_phase54`. |
| **W10-4 (SDK v3.11)** | **Decoy-CCK-promotion falsifier (proved-empirical n=10 saturated): on the Phase-57 falsifier bank where the decoy is also mentioned via at least one CCK-eligible claim_kind for the gold root_cause, the bundle decoder cannot exclude the decoy; `capsule_bundle_decoder` ties FIFO at `accuracy_full = 0.000` on 10/10 falsifier scenarios. The W10-1 win does NOT hold in this regime — by construction. Sharper observation: this is the structural limit of *any* CCK-style closed-vocabulary tier filter; a higher-resolution decoder (e.g. multi-round bundle reasoning, W10-C3) is needed.** | **proved-empirical (n=10 falsifier saturated)** | `docs/data/phase57_falsifier_K8_n10.json`; `Phase57FalsifierTests::test_bundle_decoder_ties_fifo_on_falsifier`. |

| **W11-2 (SDK v3.12)** | **Round-union monotonicity (proved structural): let `H_1, ..., H_n` be the per-round admitted bundles and `K(B)` the set of `claim_kinds` in `B`. Then `K(union) ⊇ K(H_i)` for every `i`, and the priority decoder's elected `root_cause` on `union` is at most as generic as on any individual `H_i` in the priority order. Adding more `claim_kinds` to the input of a priority-rule decoder can only move the elected label up the priority list, not down.** | **proved (by construction)**       | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::_decoded_root_cause`, `_DECODER_PRIORITY`; structural argument. |

The W11 decoder is a strict generalisation along the noise-corroboration axis only; on regimes where the decoy is NOT noise-corroborated or where admission already filters the dominant set to size ≤ 2, the inner W10 fallback path preserves the prior win.** | **proved-empirical (n=8 each)**    | `docs/data/phase58_cross_regime.json`; `Phase58CrossRegimeTests::test_R54_W7_2_preserved`, `..._R55_W8_preserved`, `..._R56_W9_preserved`, `..._R57_W10_preserved`. |
| **W11-4 (SDK v3.12)** | **Round-budget falsifier (proved-empirical n=8 saturated): on the Phase-58 falsifier bank where round-1 noise count is doubled, paired with `K_auditor=4`, the round-1 noise floods the per-round inbox and round-2's specific-tier claim's downstream effect on the union is structurally limited; `capsule_multi_round` ties FIFO at `accuracy_full = 0.000` on 8/8 falsifier scenarios. The W11-1 win does NOT hold in this regime — by construction. Sharper observation: this is the structural limit of *any* multi-round decoder that consumes per-round admitted sets; a smarter admission policy that prioritises specific-tier kinds is the natural next move.** | **proved-empirical (n=8 falsifier saturated)** | `docs/data/phase58_falsifier_K4_n8.json`; `Phase58FalsifierTests::test_falsifier_collapses_to_zero`. |

The bench property holds in 0/4 scenarios; normalisation has nothing to rescue (W13 stats: ``n_heuristic = 0``, ``n_exact > 0``, ``n_passthrough = 0``); W13 ties W12 ties multi_round at ``accuracy_full = 0.250``. The W13 advance is *not* observable on R-60-ollama because there is no drift to widen the closure of. The honest reading: synthetic→real-LLM transfer at the open-world axis is gated NOT primarily by normalisation but by *event-shape design + prompt-side discipline*; the synthetic noisy extractor mimics drift but does not mimic real-LLM epistemic filtering.** | **empirical-research (n=4 producer-side observation; 12 real Ollama calls; 0 failures; 49.4 s wall on Mac 1)** | `docs/data/phase60_real_ollama_qwen2_5_14b_n4.json::raw_responses_per_scenario`, `extractor_stats`; `vision_mvp/experiments/phase60_open_world_normalization.py::CapturingOllamaExtractor`. |

## Producer-side ambiguity preservation (W14-Λ-prompt, W14-Λ-real, W14-1..W14-4) — SDK v3.15

The bench property's ``round1_decoy_corroborated`` predicate requires ≥ 2 distinct producer roles to mention the decoy in round 1; under producer-side compression the auditor receives ≤ 1 distinct-role decoy mention; a never-emitted handoff has no CID (Capsule Contract C5); no role view can admit it (W7-3 extraction floor); no cross-round decoder can decode it. | **W17-2 (SDK v3.18)** | **Magnitude-hinted prompt determinism + threshold table soundness: (a) magnitude-hinted prompt rendering is byte-for-byte deterministic given ``(schema, events, round_idx, OperationalThreshold table)``; (b) with empty ``schema.magnitude_thresholds``, rendered prompt reduces to structured prompt with anti-relative-magnitude clause appended; (c) threshold table filters to round's allowed-set (round-2 diagnosis prompts do NOT carry round-1 observation thresholds); (d) :data:`INCIDENT_TRIAGE_DEFAULT_MAGNITUDE_THRESHOLDS` exposes the same numeric thresholds as the synthetic :class:`MagnitudeFilteringExtractor` (Phase-61 calibration anchors).** | **proved (by inspection) + mechanically-checked** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::_render_magnitude_hinted_prompt`, `OperationalThreshold`, `INCIDENT_TRIAGE_DEFAULT_MAGNITUDE_THRESHOLDS`; `MagnitudeHintedProtocolRenderingTests`; `IncidentTriageMagnitudeHintsTests`. |
| **W17-3 (SDK v3.18)** | **Backward compatibility (full programme regression): with ``mode = PRODUCER_PROMPT_NAIVE`` or ``mode = PRODUCER_PROMPT_STRUCTURED`` AND ``magnitude_hinted_schema = False``, the W17 surface reduces to the SDK v3.15 W14 anchor byte-for-byte. On the synthetic side, swapping ``mode = 'structured'`` for ``mode = 'magnitude_hinted'`` with ``magnitude_hinted_schema = True`` produces the same downstream answer because the synthetic ``MagnitudeFilteringExtractor`` does not consult prompt thresholds. R-58 / R-59 / R-60 / R-61 / R-62 / R-63 default + falsifier banks all preserved; **442/442 prior tests pass byte-for-byte**; 20 new tests cover the W17 surface.** | **proved-empirical (full programme-wide regression)** | `vision_mvp/tests/` (full suite; 442/442 + 20 new = 462/462); `W17BackwardCompatTests::test_synthetic_mag_hinted_matches_structured_on_r61`. |
| **W17-C-XMODEL (SDK v3.18; proved-conditional + empirical-research)** | **Cross-model live composition: the W17-1 win at qwen2.5:14b-32k transfers to qwen3.5:35b-MoE on the same fresh live R-64-LIVE-MAGHINT regime under the magnitude-hinted prompt with ``think = False``. On a fresh live ``qwen3.5:35b`` probe (n=8 × 24 producer calls; 0 failures; 92.0 s wall): bench property holds in 8/8 (W17 magnitude-hint extension transfers byte-for-byte on the bench-property axis); ``capsule_attention_aware = 0.750``; ``capsule_layered_fifo_packed = 0.000``; ``capsule_fifo = 0.000``; +0.750 strict gain over both substrate FIFO AND FIFO-packed-W14H-only baseline (well above the 0.50 strong-bar threshold). The 0.250 gap relative to the 14B anchor is on the ``accuracy_root_cause`` axis: the 35B emits a different specific-tier kind on one scenario than the 14B does (a model-side specific-kind judgment artifact, not a producer-protocol failure). The first proved-conditional cross-model real-LLM strict gain in the programme.** | **proved-conditional + empirical-research (n=8 × 24 producer calls; 0 endpoint failures; 92.0 s wall on Mac-1; ``think = False`` chat-template flag)** | `docs/data/phase64_live_maghint_qwen3_5_35b_n8.json`. |

## Conjectures (W3-C*)

| Claim   | Description                                                              | Status                                       |
| ------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------- |
| W3-C1   | General subsumption: every Phase-N bounded-context theorem subsumes      | conjectural                                  |
| W3-C2   | Capsule contract preserves all Phase-N substrate guarantees              | conjectural                                  |
| W3-C3   | Honest-falsification frontier (table-level invariants)                   | retracted by W3-15 cohort lift               |
| W3-C4 (legacy) | Earlier "decoder paradigm shift candidate at 0.400 / strict zero-shot" | **retracted** by W3-26 / W3-27       |
| **W3-C4 (new SDK v3.3)** | **PARSE_OUTCOME failure_kind distribution stable across LLM tags** | **superseded by W3-C6 (sharper synthetic reading)** |
| W3-C5 (legacy) | Relational-axis extension closes W3-16                              | conjectural                                  |
| **W3-C5 (new SDK v3.3)** | **Sub-intra-cell PROMPT/LLM_RESPONSE capsule slice closes the inner-loop boundary without breaking W3-34 spine equivalence** | **DISCHARGED by W3-42/W3-43/W3-44/W3-45 in SDK v3.4** |
| **W3-C6 (new SDK v3.4)** | **Synthetic-LLM cross-distribution PARSE_OUTCOME failure-kind TVD ≥ 0.5; strict→robust parser-mode shift on synthetic.unclosed = 1.000** | **empirical (reproducible from synthetic distribution library)** |
| W3-C6   | Plurality + auxiliary signal closes 0.200 priority-decoder ceiling       | partial — replaced by learned-decoder W3-19  |
| W3-C7 (strict) | Strict point-estimate Gate-1 ($\hat p \ge 0.400$) + zero-shot Gate-2 strict penalty ≤ 5pp | **retracted** by W3-26, W3-27   |
| W3-C8   | (deferred — relational decoder closes Gate 2 strictly)                   | conjectural                                  |
| W3-C9   | Refined paradigm-shift reading: $n=80$ point-estimate + zero-shot gap    | conjectural (candidate)                      |
| W3-C10  | Relational decoder level-ceiling                                                | conjectural                                  |
| **W4-C1 (SDK v3.5; SDK v3.7 conditional reading)** | **Learned per-role admission policy admits strictly fewer handoffs (12/12 seeds) and improves pooled team-decision accuracy on most train seeds (gap_full > 0 in 11/12 seeds, mean +0.054; gap_root_cause > 0 in 8/12 seeds, mean +0.032) over the strongest fixed admission baseline (coverage-guided) on the Phase-52 default config (K_auditor=8, noise=(0.10, 0.30, 0.05), PYTHONHASHSEED=0).** | **conditional**: empirical-positive on its anchor distribution (Phase-52 synthetic+noise default config, K=8, spurious=0.30 — unchanged from SDK v3.5); **falsified** at higher symbolic noise (spurious=0.50, disclosed in SDK v3.5); **falsified out-of-distribution on the Phase-53 real-LLM regime** (capsule_learned 0.400 vs fixed 0.800 on synthetic and qwen2.5:14b-32k, gap = -0.40; ties at qwen3.5:35b at 0.800/0.800; SDK v3.7, see `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_SCALE_VS_STRUCTURE.md` § 4.4) |
| **W4-C2 (SDK v3.5)** | **Cohort-lifted role view closes W4-3 on a sub-class of scenarios**           | **conjectural** (Phase 53 candidate; falsifier: a scenario whose causal-share floor exceeds a single COHORT's max_parents) |
| **W4-C3 (SDK v3.5)** | **The capsule-layer admission rule subsumes the Phase-36 AdaptiveSubscriptionTable route-edit primitive** | **conjectural** (open) |
| **W5-C1 (SDK v3.6)** | **Parser-boundary instability is a (model architecture × prompt-format) interaction, not a model-capacity artefact. Concretely, scaling 14.8B-dense → 36B-MoE under fixed prompt format on the bundled bank flips strict-mode parser failure rate from 0/10 to 10/10.** | **empirical-research** (n=10 saturation; falsifier = a bank where the larger model strict-parses ok > 50%) |
| **W5-C2 (SDK v3.6)** | **Robust-mode parser recovery (specifically ``recovery=closed_at_eos``) is the load-bearing safety net that makes the capsule-native runtime model-class-agnostic on the bundled prompt format. Cross-model TVD on robust = 0.000 in W5-1.** | **empirical-research** (n=10 saturation; falsifier = a model whose ``unclosed_new`` cannot be salvaged) |
| **W5-C3 (SDK v3.6)** | **The capsule-native runtime's closed-vocabulary ``PARSE_OUTCOME.failure_kind`` is a *minimum sufficient* typed witness of cross-model behaviour differences — strict-mode failure-kind TVD captures in one number what manual byte-level diff over N responses would surface.** | **conjectural** (research; falsifier = a model pair with identical strict-mode `failure_kind` distribution but materially different downstream test-pass rate) |
| **W6-C1 (SDK v3.7; FALSIFIED on Phase-53)** | **Drafted conjecture: ``structure_gain`` (capsule_learned − substrate, accuracy_full) is preserved or grows when the underlying LLM scales up. Falsifier: ``structure_gain[35B] ≤ 0`` with ``substrate ≥ capsule_learned − 0.05``.** | **falsified-empirical** on Phase-53 default: ``structure_gain[14B] = -0.4``; ``structure_gain[35B] = 0.0``. Honest revised reading: structure_gain is **non-positive at every regime tested**; scale narrows a *deficit* (not a surplus). |
| **W6-C2 (SDK v3.7; FALSIFIED on Phase-53)** | **Drafted conjecture: the per-role admission scorer trained on Phase-52 synthetic+noise data transfers usefully (capsule_learned > capsule_fifo) to real-LLM candidate streams. Falsifier: capsule_learned beats capsule_fifo by < 0.05 on average across all model regimes.** | **falsified-empirical** on Phase-53 default: capsule_learned − capsule_fifo = -0.40 / -0.40 / 0.00 across (synthetic, 14B, 35B); average gap = -0.267. The W4-C1 (SDK v3.5) advantage **does not transfer OOD** to the real-LLM regime on this bench. |
| **W6-C3 (SDK v3.7)** | **36B-MoE producer roles emit a different candidate-handoff distribution than 14.8B-dense producer roles on the same scenario bank under matched prompt and temperature; falsifier: per-role TVD between candidate-kind histograms < 0.10.** | **empirical-research (positive)** — TVD = 0.167 on the pooled (source_role × claim_kind) histogram across 5 scenarios; modest but above the 0.10 falsifier; cf. W5-1's parser-axis TVD = 1.000 (the multi-agent extractor axis is more model-class-stable than the parser axis on the same hardware). |
| **W6-C4 (SDK v3.7; new)** | **Substrate FIFO admission is competitive with every capsule admission policy (FIFO, priority, coverage, learned) in real-LLM-driven multi-agent benchmarks at sufficient per-role budget. Falsifier: a (model, scenario, K_auditor) configuration where ``substrate_acc[m, s] < min_capsule_acc[m, s] - 0.05``.** | **conjectural-empirical** — anchored by 0.000 gap at K_auditor=4 on Phase-53 default; falsifier search direction = lower K_auditor (1, 2, 3) where substrate FIFO must admit non-causal head-of-arrival emissions. |
| **W6-C5 (SDK v3.7; new)** | **Model scale narrows the OOD generalisation gap of the per-role admission scorer trained on synthetic noise: ``scale_gain[capsule_learned] > 0 ≥ scale_gain[every fixed capsule policy] = 0`` whenever the synthetic training distribution carries non-trivial noise (``spurious_prob ≥ 0.20``). Falsifier: a synthetic→real transfer where ``scale_gain[capsule_learned] ≤ 0``.** | **conjectural-empirical** — anchored by ``scale_gain[capsule_learned] = +0.400`` against ``scale_gain[fixed] = 0`` on Phase-53 default. |
| **W7-C1 (SDK v3.8; new)** | **Multi-service-gold extension: a cohort policy that admits the *top-2* plurality tags (rather than the strict plurality) strictly improves accuracy_full on multi-service-gold scenarios over single-plurality cohort. Falsifier: a multi-service Phase-55-style bench where top-2 cohort ties or loses to single-plurality cohort.** | **conjectural** (Phase-55 candidate; not yet measured). |
| **W7-C2 (SDK v3.8; new)** | **Bundle-aware decoder + cohort admission strictly outperforms cohort admission alone on benches with weak / partial service-tag coherence (e.g. some gold candidates lacking a service tag). Falsifier: a bench where the decoder modification provides ≤ +0.05 on accuracy_full over cohort_buffered alone.** | **conjectural** (decoder modification not yet shipped). |
| **W7-C3 (SDK v3.8; new)** | **The W7-2 structural win transfers to a real-LLM regime when the LLM is prompted with a multi-service event mix (foreign-service decoys come from the prompt, not from synthetic injection). Falsifier: a real-LLM run where buffered cohort coherence achieves ``cohort_buffered − fifo accuracy_full < 0.20`` after surplus is verified.** | **conjectural** (Phase-56 candidate; requires Mac-2 or wider real-LLM runs). |
| **W8-C1 (SDK v3.9; new)** | **Multi-service-gold extension: a corroboration policy that admits the *top-k* highest-scoring tags strictly improves accuracy_full on multi-service-gold scenarios over single-tag corroboration on a Phase-56-style bench. Falsifier: a multi-service bench where top-k corroboration ties or loses to single-tag corroboration.** | **conjectural** (Phase-56 candidate; not yet measured). |
| **W8-C2 (SDK v3.9; new)** | **The W8-1 strict-separation result transfers to a real-LLM regime when the LLM is prompted with a multi-service event mix that produces decoy raw plurality + gold cross-role corroboration in the LLM-extracted candidate stream. Falsifier: a real-LLM run where corroboration beats FIFO by < 0.20 on accuracy_full after both bench properties are verified.** | **conjectural** (Phase-56 candidate; SDK v3.9 confirms no-regression in low-surplus 14B regime, but the W8-1 conditional regime requires re-prompting). |
| **W8-C3 (SDK v3.9; new)** | **Bundle-aware decoder + corroboration admission strictly outperforms corroboration alone on benches where admission cannot fully filter foreign-service candidates (e.g. partial-coverage cases). Falsifier: a bench where the decoder modification provides ≤ +0.05 over admission-alone.** | **conjectural** (decoder modification not yet shipped; restates W7-C2 under W8 framing). |
| **W8-C1 (SDK v3.9; DISCHARGED by W9-1 in SDK v3.10)** | **Originally: a corroboration policy that admits the *top-k* highest-scoring tags strictly improves accuracy_full on multi-service-gold scenarios over single-tag corroboration on a Phase-56-style bench.** | **DISCHARGED-empirical** by W9-1 on Phase 56: top-K with argmax-by-role-count gate beats single-tag W8 by +1.000 stable across 5/5 bank seeds. |
| **W9-C1 (SDK v3.10; DISCHARGED by W10-1 in SDK v3.11)** | **Originally: bundle-aware decoder companion that filters service tags at decode time by the dominant (claim_kind, role) signature strictly improves accuracy_full on the Phase-56 falsifier regime where admission alone admits a decoy.** | **DISCHARGED-empirical** by W10-1 on the Phase-57 decoder-forcing regime: bundle-aware decoder paired with W9 admission (top_k=3) beats every service-blind admission policy by +1.000 stable across 5/5 bank seeds. The decoder-side axis is now the load-bearing axis of the SDK v3.11 milestone. |
| **W9-C2 (SDK v3.10; new)** | **Top-K extension to |gold_services| ≥ 3: the W9-1 strict-separation result generalises to multi-service incidents with ``|gold_services| = N ≥ 3`` when ``top_k = N``, provided every gold service is corroborated by ≥ 2 distinct producer roles AND every decoy is corroborated by ≤ 1. Falsifier: a Phase-57 bench (3-service gold) where W9 with ``top_k=3`` beats FIFO by < 0.50 on accuracy_full.** | **conjectural** (Phase-57 bench not yet built; the W9 policy already supports arbitrary top_k). |

| **W10-C1 (SDK v3.11; new)** | **CCK-table extension: the bundle-aware decoder approach generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits a closed-vocabulary tier mapping `claim_kind → tier` and `root_cause → tier`. | **W10-C2 (SDK v3.11; new)** | **Real-LLM transfer of W10-1: when the producer LLM emits a multi-service-gold + corroborated-decoy stream, pairing W9 admission with the bundle-aware decoder closes the W10-Λ gap on the LLM-extracted candidate stream. | **W10-C3 (SDK v3.11; PARTIALLY DISCHARGED by W11-1 in SDK v3.12)** | **Originally: multi-round bundle decoder closes W10-4 (decoy-CCK-promotion) on a sub-class of scenarios.** | **PARTIALLY DISCHARGED-empirical** by W11-1 on R-58 (a different sub-class — *delayed-causal-evidence* with noise-corroborated decoy — than W10-4's CCK-promoted decoy). | **W11-C1 (SDK v3.12; new)** | **The noise-decoy drop generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits a closed-vocabulary `generic-noise` claim_kind set. | **W11-C2 (SDK v3.12; PARTIALLY DISCHARGED by W12-1 in SDK v3.13)** | **Originally: real-LLM transfer of W11-1: when round-1 producers emit generic-tier observations and round-2 producers emit specific-tier diagnoses on the LLM-extracted candidate stream, multi_round closes the W11-Λ gap.** | **PARTIALLY DISCHARGED-empirical** by W12-Λ + W12-1: the *un-normalised* W11 decoder does NOT transfer (W12-Λ shows multi_round ties FIFO at 0.000 on Phase-59 default at ``synonym_prob=0.50``), but a *normalised* W11 decoder (W12-1) DOES transfer (+1.000 vs every un-normalised method, stable 5/5). The honest revised reading is: synthetic cross-round structure transfers to real-LLM regimes *only when an explicit normalisation layer absorbs the producer's kind / payload drift channel*. The original conjecture (W11 alone transfers) is **falsified-empirical**; the closure-conditional generalisation (W11 + closed-vocabulary normalisation transfers under bounded noise) is **W12-1**, proved-conditional + proved-empirical. |
| **W11-C3 (SDK v3.12; new)** | **Multi-step disambiguation: with three or more rounds and conflicting specific-tier evidence across rounds (e.g. round-2 emits DEADLOCK on gold_A, round-3 emits POOL_EXHAUSTION on gold_B), a contradiction-aware round-resolution rule (last-wins / weighted-confidence) strictly outperforms naive union. Falsifier: a 3-round bench where any contradiction-aware rule provides ≤ +0.05 over naive union on accuracy_full.** | **conjectural** (multi-step capsule chains not yet shipped). |
| **W12-C1 (SDK v3.13; new)** | **Cross-bench transfer of the W12 normalisation contract: the closed-vocabulary normalisation pattern generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits a closed-vocabulary closure of LLM kind variants. | **W12-C2 (SDK v3.13; new)** | **Real-Ollama (qwen2.5:14b-32k or qwen3.5:35b) producer transfer of W12-1: when the producer LLM is a real Ollama-served model on the Phase-53-style prompt, the same R-59 strong bar (gap robust − w11 ≥ 0.50, audit_ok preserved, no regression on R-53..R-58) holds. Falsifier: a real-Ollama run where the LLM emits drift outside :data:`CLAIM_KIND_SYNONYMS` on > 50% of causal claims (i.e. the synthetic noise channel is *narrower* than the real LLM's variant distribution), in which case W12-1 partially fails and the strong-bar advance is partial. The opt-in ``ollama`` LLM mode is the operator path; SDK v3.13 establishes the synthetic side of the transfer; the real-Ollama side is the next data point and the natural Mac-2-returns probe.** | **conjectural** (Phase-59 ``--llm-mode ollama`` candidate; requires Mac 1 or Mac 2 reachable + a willingness to accept synthetic-fallback contamination on HTTP failure). |
| **W12-C3 (SDK v3.13; PARTIALLY DISCHARGED by W13-1 in SDK v3.14)** | **Originally: an adaptive (learned or heuristic) synonym table closes more of the LLM-drift channel than the closed-vocabulary :data:`CLAIM_KIND_SYNONYMS`.** | **PARTIALLY DISCHARGED-empirical** by W13-1: a *heuristic* layered normaliser (exact + regex-predicate abstraction rules) strictly widens the closure on R-60-wide (every variant in :data:`HEURISTIC_RESCUABLE_OOV_KINDS` resolves to its named canonical, +1.000 vs W12). The *learned* normaliser variant remains conjectural (W13-C2). The closure boundary is structural, not the table contents (W13-4). |
| **W13-C1 (SDK v3.14; new)** | **Cross-bench transfer of the W13 closure-widening contract: the layered (exact + heuristic) normalisation pattern generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits a closed-vocabulary tier mapping AND a small set of regex predicates over kind text whose union covers ≥ 90 % of LLM kind drift on the family's prompt. Falsifier: a benchmark family (security-incident, robotics, compliance-review) where any size-bounded heuristic predicate set covers < 50 % of LLM drift on the calibrated prompt.** | **conjectural** (closed-vocabulary tier mapping + heuristic rule set for security-incident, robotics, or compliance-review families not yet shipped). |
| **W13-C2 (SDK v3.14; new)** | **Learned-normaliser closure: an embedding-distance-based or LLM-distilled normaliser strictly widens the W13 heuristic closure on R-60-cosmic. Specifically, a learned normaliser that maps OOV kinds to their nearest canonical via cosine distance over a small claim-kind embedding survives a higher ``cosmic_oov_prob`` than the regex-predicate set. Falsifier: a learned normaliser that does not strictly improve over the W13 heuristic table at ``cosmic_oov_prob ∈ {0.30, 0.50, 0.70}``. Honest scope: this is a closure-widening move, not a structural fix — the W13-4 closure boundary applies to any predicate-based normaliser; a learned normaliser only widens the closure but does not eliminate it (a maximally adversarial drift channel is still a finite-VC-dim adversary). | **conjectural** (no learned normaliser shipped; the heuristic table is the SDK v3.14 anchor). |
| **W13-C3 (SDK v3.14; new)** | **Real-Ollama transfer of W13-1 with a redesigned event stream: when the Phase-58 events are redesigned so the decoy and gold services have *comparable* magnitudes (so a real LLM at the 14B class does not filter the decoy as noise) AND the prompt instructs the LLM to emit one claim per distinct event, real Ollama qwen2.5:14b-32k does emit the R-58 delayed-causal-evidence shape AND does drift kinds with non-trivial probability (≥ 20 %); under this regime, the W13-1 strict bar (gap ≥ 0.50) is cleared on the real-LLM stream. Falsifier: a real-Ollama run on the redesigned events where W13 − W12 < 0.20 pooled accuracy_full. Honest scope: this is the natural fix for the W13-Λ-real observation — but it pushes the contribution back onto event-shape / prompt-side rather than on the normaliser per se.** | **conjectural** (Phase-60 v2 candidate; requires a redesigned event stream that elicits non-trivial drift from a 14B-class LLM). |
| **W13-C4 (SDK v3.14; new)** | **Abstention as a load-bearing signal: when the W13 normaliser is configured with ``abstain_on_unknown=True``, the priority decoder can use the abstention rate as an "I don't know" signal and trigger a fallback (e.g. a different admission policy, a request for additional rounds, an LLM rewrite call). On a regime where the OOV rate is non-trivial but bounded, an abstention-aware decoder strictly improves over a passthrough decoder. Falsifier: a regime where the abstention-aware decoder ties or loses to the passthrough decoder by ≥ 0.05 on accuracy_full.** | **conjectural** (the abstention sentinel is implemented; the abstention-aware decoder pathway is not yet wired). |
| **W13-C3 (SDK v3.14; PARTIALLY DISCHARGED by W14-1 + W14-Λ-real in SDK v3.15)** | **Originally: real-Ollama transfer of W13-1 with a redesigned event stream + a prompt that instructs the LLM to emit one claim per distinct event would clear the W13-1 strong bar (gap ≥ 0.50) on the real-LLM stream.** | **PARTIALLY DISCHARGED-empirical** by W14-1 + W14-Λ-real: the *combination* of comparable-magnitude events + structured producer protocol clears the strict-gain bar on real Ollama 14B (n=8, +0.500 vs FIFO at exactly the R-61-OLLAMA-A threshold), BUT the gain is on the **W11/W12/W13 cross-round pipeline as a whole** — not specifically on the W13 closure-widening, which is structurally invisible because the real LLM still emits canonical kinds. The honest revised reading: prompt-side discipline + comparable-magnitude events restore the bench property; W13's *normalisation* contribution remains dormant on this regime. The "specifically on W13" framing of the original W13-C3 is **falsified-empirical** in the negative direction (no kind drift to widen the closure of); the cross-round structural bar is cleared at +0.500 by the combined intervention (W14). |
| **W14-C1 (SDK v3.15; new)** | **Cross-bench transfer of the W14 protocol: the layered observation/diagnosis prompt schema generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits an observation/diagnosis tier partition over its closed-vocabulary claim kinds AND the events fit a multi-round delayed-causal-evidence shape. Falsifier: a benchmark family (security-incident, robotics, compliance-review) where observation and diagnosis cannot be cleanly partitioned, OR where the round-1/round-2 separation is structurally absent.** | **conjectural** (only the incident-triage schema ships; security-incident / robotics / compliance-review schemas not yet built). |
| **W14-C2 (SDK v3.15; new)** | **Model-side magnitude calibration: the 1/8 R-61-ollama-structured failure (LLM judged ``error_rate=0.15`` not to qualify as ``ERROR_RATE_SPIKE``) is closed by an explicit *magnitude hint* extension to the structured prompt — the tier banner enumerates the magnitude thresholds the LLM should treat as qualifying. Under the magnitude-hinted prompt, qwen2.5:14b on R-61 events achieves ``accuracy_full ≥ 0.875``. Falsifier: a magnitude-hinted run where the model still under-emits gold claims at the same rate.** | **conjectural** (the magnitude hint is not yet wired into the structured prompt rendering; the W14-Λ-real 7/8 result is the empirical anchor in the *positive* direction, the failure scenario is the candidate falsifier). |
| **W14-C3 (SDK v3.15; new)** | **Multi-round generalisation: the W14 protocol's observation/diagnosis split generalises to N ≥ 3 rounds with a *graded* tier hierarchy (observation → preliminary diagnosis → refined diagnosis). Under a 3-round bench with two specific-tier kinds emitted on different rounds (round 2 = preliminary; round 3 = refined), the structured protocol with N-tier banners strictly outperforms the 2-round protocol on accuracy_full. Falsifier: a 3-round bench where the N-tier protocol provides ≤ +0.05 over the 2-round protocol on accuracy_full.** | **conjectural** (multi-step capsule chains not yet shipped; restates W11-C3 under the W14 framing). |
| **W14-C4 (SDK v3.15; new)** | **Cross-model transfer: the W14-1 win at qwen2.5:14b-32k transfers to qwen3.5:35b-MoE (the prior W5-1 cross-model probe) and to non-Ollama backends (MLX-distributed). Specifically, the structured protocol's bench-property recovery on R-61-ollama-structured ≥ 75 % holds for both model classes. Falsifier: a 35B run where the bench property holds in < 50 % of scenarios under the structured prompt.** | **conjectural** (requires Mac 2 reachable + a willingness to consume the wall-time budget; the SDK v3.15 anchor is 14B only). |
| **W14-C5 (SDK v3.15; new)** | **Multi-hypothesis variant: an extension of the structured protocol that explicitly permits multi-hypothesis listings on ambiguous round-1 events ("if uncertain, list 2-3 candidate kinds comma-separated") strictly improves accuracy_full over the single-hypothesis variant on regimes where the LLM's per-event confidence is low. Falsifier: a regime where the multi-hypothesis variant ties or loses to the single-hypothesis variant by ≥ 0.05.** | **conjectural** (not yet wired; the W14 default is single-hypothesis per event). |
| **W15-C-real (SDK v3.16; new)** | **Real-LLM downstream-decoder transfer of W15-1: the W15 salience pack provides a strict accuracy gain over FIFO truncation when the cross-round bundle is fed to a real LLM (e.g. Mac-1 ``qwen2.5:14b-32k``) configured as a downstream re-decoder agent under a tight context window. Specifically, on R-62-tightbudget with the bundle re-decoded by the LLM under a context window equal to ``T_decoder``, the W15 method maintains ≥ 0.20 strict accuracy gain over FIFO truncation. Falsifier: a real-LLM downstream-decoder run where W15 − FIFO < 0.10 OR where the LLM's attention is sufficiently uniform that prompt-position ordering does not change correctness (the proxy attention metric does not transfer to the real model).** | **conjectural** (requires Mac 1 / Mac 2 reachable + an LLM downstream re-decoder pipeline; SDK v3.16 ships the synthetic side only). |
| **W15-C1 (SDK v3.16; new)** | **Cross-bench transfer of the W15 packing contract: the salience scoring pattern (tier + CCK + corroboration + magnitude + round) generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits a closed-vocabulary CCK + magnitude vocabulary. Falsifier: a benchmark family (security-incident, robotics, compliance-review) where no closed-vocabulary tier mapping or magnitude proxy exists; equivalently, where the salience score becomes uninformative (variance below the within-tag tie-break threshold).** | **conjectural** (only the incident-triage CCK + magnitude vocabulary ships; security-incident / robotics / compliance-review schemas not yet built). |
| **W15-C-LEARNED (SDK v3.16; new)** | **Learned salience: a logistic-regression / small MLP scorer over per-handoff features (analogous to :class:`LearnedTeamAdmissionPolicy`) outperforms the closed-form W15 weights on a held-out test set across 5/5 random splits. Falsifier: any held-out split where the learned salience ties or loses to the closed-form weights by ≥ 0.05. Honest scope: the learned variant is at risk of OOD failure analogous to W4-C1 / W6-C1 / W6-C2; the closed-form weights remain the SDK v3.16 anchor.** | **conjectural** (no learned salience shipped; W15 default is closed-form). |
| **W15-C-SYMMETRIC (SDK v3.16; DISCHARGED-NEGATIVE by W17-Λ-symmetric in SDK v3.18)** | **Originally: Symmetric-corroboration multi-hypothesis structural limit; the natural next-axis open question for SDK v3.17+.** | **DISCHARGED as a negative theorem** by W17-Λ-symmetric on R-64-SYM (SDK v3.18). The construction shows every capsule strategy in the SDK ties FIFO at 0.000 under both ``T_decoder ∈ {None, 24}`` by construction; the priority decoder still elects the right specific-tier root_cause but ``services_correct`` set-equality fails because the W11 contradiction-aware drop fires symmetrically. **The wall is real and structural** — escape requires a learned or LLM-distilled semantic-disambiguator beyond the closed-form capsule surface (W17-C-DISAMBIGUATOR, conjectural). |
| **W15-C-COMPOSE-W14 (SDK v3.16; PARTIALLY DISCHARGED by W16-Λ-real-replay in SDK v3.17)** | **Originally: W15 + W14 compose on real Ollama; running W15 over the W14-emitted stream closes the 1/8 model-error failure W14 alone leaves, achieving ``accuracy_full ≥ 0.625``.** | **PARTIALLY DISCHARGED-empirical** by W16-Λ-real-replay in SDK v3.17. The replay path over the recorded ``phase61_real_ollama_structured_qwen2_5_14b_n8.json`` bytes shows the composition delivers a strict +0.500 gain over the FIFO-packed-W14-only baseline at T_decoder=14 — but does NOT close the 1/8 model-error failure (composed accuracy_full = 0.500 = W14-only loose-budget accuracy). The composition is *robust to budget pressure* (the recovered W14 anchor) but does not *transcend* the upstream model-side judgment failure. The honest revised reading: W15 + W14 compose by making the W14 result *robust to bounded context*; closing the 1/8 model-side failure remains W16-C-LIVE-OLLAMA / W14-C2 (magnitude-hint extension), conjectural. |
| **W16-C1 (SDK v3.17; new)** | **Cross-bench transfer of the W14+W15 composition: the layered composition pattern (structured producer protocol + salience-aware decoder packing under T_decoder) generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families (security-incident / robotics / compliance-review) when the family admits both an observation/diagnosis tier partition AND a closed-vocabulary CCK + magnitude vocabulary AND multi-hypothesis events with asymmetric corroboration. Falsifier: a benchmark family where one of the two layers is structurally absent (e.g. a single-round bench has no W14 round-1/round-2 split; a single-hypothesis bench has no W11-drop trigger).** | **conjectural** (only the incident-triage schema + CCK + magnitude vocabulary ships; cross-bench schemas not yet built). |
| **W16-C-LIVE-OLLAMA (SDK v3.17; DISCHARGED by W17-1 in SDK v3.18)** | **Originally: a fresh live Ollama probe under R-63-COMPOSED-TIGHT closes the 1/8 model-error failure W14-only leaves, achieving ``accuracy_full ≥ 0.625``.** | **DISCHARGED-empirical** by W17-1 on R-64-LIVE-MAGHINT (SDK v3.18). The fresh live probe achieves ``accuracy_full = 1.000`` (closes the 1/8 miss entirely; bench property holds in 8/8) — but the load-bearing intervention is *not* the live re-run alone (the W17-Λ-no-hint anchor on R-64-LIVE-STRUCT reproduces the recorded 0.500 envelope on the fresh probe). The magnitude-hint extension (W17) is what closes the gap from 0.500 to 1.000. The original conjecture's premise (a live re-run alone closes the gap) is **falsified-empirical**; the closure-conditional generalisation (a live re-run + magnitude-hint extension closes the gap) is **W17-1**, proved-conditional + empirical-research. |
| **W16-C-CROSS-MODEL (SDK v3.17; PARTIALLY DISCHARGED by W17-C-XMODEL in SDK v3.18)** | **Originally: cross-model transfer of the composition to qwen3.5:35b under MLX-distributed inference.** | **PARTIALLY DISCHARGED-empirical** by W17-C-XMODEL on a fresh live ``qwen3.5:35b`` Ollama probe (NOT MLX-distributed; the simpler Ollama backend with ``think = False`` was reachable on Mac-1) under the W17 magnitude-hinted prompt: bench property holds in 8/8; ``capsule_attention_aware = 0.750``; +0.750 strict gain over FIFO-pack and substrate FIFO. The strict-gain clause is met; the saturated full-correctness clause (1.000 on 35B) remains conjectural and bounded by a 35B-specific specific-tier judgment artifact. The MLX-distributed clause of the original W16-C-CROSS-MODEL (vs the Ollama backend on Mac-1) is *orthogonal* to W17-C-XMODEL and remains conjectural pending Mac-2 reachable. |
| **W16-C-LEARNED-COMPOSE (SDK v3.17; new)** | **Learned salience + learned producer: a learned salience scorer (W15-C-LEARNED) plus a learned producer protocol (W14-C5 multi-hypothesis variant) outperforms the closed-form W16 composition on a held-out test set across 5/5 random splits. Falsifier: any held-out split where the learned composition ties or loses to the closed-form composition by ≥ 0.05.** | **conjectural** (no learned salience and no multi-hypothesis producer variant shipped; the closed-form composition remains the SDK v3.17 anchor). |
| **W16-C-SYMMETRIC (SDK v3.17; DISCHARGED-NEGATIVE by W17-Λ-symmetric in SDK v3.18)** | **Originally: Symmetric-corroboration limit on the composed regime; SDK v3.18+ candidate.** | **DISCHARGED as a negative theorem** by W17-Λ-symmetric on R-64-SYM (SDK v3.18). See the W15-C-SYMMETRIC discharge above; W16-C-SYMMETRIC is the same wall stated under the W16 framing. **The wall is real and structural** for the closed-form capsule surface; escape requires a learned or LLM-distilled semantic-disambiguator (W17-C-DISAMBIGUATOR, conjectural). |
| **W17-C-DISAMBIGUATOR (SDK v3.18; new)** | **Semantic-disambiguator beyond the closed-form capsule surface: a learned or LLM-distilled disambiguator that consumes the round-2 disambiguator's evidence text directly can in principle distinguish ``orders_payments_join`` (gold A_B in deadlock) from a generic decoy whose round-1 mentions are observationally identical. The natural research move beyond the W17-Λ-symmetric wall.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.18; named research frontier for SDK v3.19+). |
| **W17-C-LEARNED-HINT (SDK v3.18; new)** | **Learned threshold variant: a per-kind data-driven threshold table outperforms the closed-form :data:`INCIDENT_TRIAGE_DEFAULT_MAGNITUDE_THRESHOLDS` on a held-out test set across 5/5 random splits. Falsifier: any held-out split where the learned threshold ties or loses to the closed-form table by ≥ 0.05.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.18; the closed-form table is the W17-1 anchor). |
| **W17-C-CROSS-BENCH (SDK v3.18; new)** | **Cross-bench transfer of the magnitude-hint extension: the W17 protocol generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits a closed-vocabulary kind → qualifying-threshold mapping AND the LLM is observed to make relative-magnitude judgments on its events. Falsifier: a benchmark family where the bench property cannot be made to hold under any reasonable threshold table on the calibrated prompt.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.18; only the incident-triage threshold table ships). |

Names the structural limit when round-2 evidence is adversarially-relational; no closed-form bundle-relational scorer that *trusts* the disambiguator's payload can escape this regime without an outside-information axis (W18-C-OUTSIDE, conjectural).** | **proved-empirical (n=8 falsifier saturated) + structural sketch** | `docs/data/phase65_cross_regime_synthetic.json::r65_deceive`; `Phase65FalsifierTests::test_w18_lambda_deceive_picks_decoy_and_fails`. |

Falsifier: a hand-constructed adversarial setting where the outside source is itself compromised AND the deceptive round-2 mention is internally consistent with the outside source. Honest cap: even with outside information, an adversarial round-2 + adversarial outside source jointly bound the closed-form scorer's reach.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.19; named structural escape from the W18-Λ-deceive falsifier). |

Honest scope: free-form natural-language relational mentions (e.g. ``"the join between orders and payments"``) fall *outside* the W18 exact-match closure by construction; W18-Λ-real is partially closed when the LLM is prompted to emit closed-vocabulary relational compounds (analogous to W14 structured-prompt) and conjectural otherwise. | **W19-2 (SDK v3.20)** | **W19 determinism + closed-form correctness (proved by inspection + mechanically-checked): (a) ``_w19_canonical_primary_index`` is byte-deterministic given the union, the round_hint, and the optional raw_union — uses a stable canonical sort with canonical-role-for-kind tiebreak then raw-kind tiebreak; (b) ``_w19_witness_counts`` is byte-deterministic given the union, the primary index, and the admitted-tag list — deduplicates byte-identical witnesses by ``(source_role, claim_kind, payload_sha)``; (c) the W19 branch decision is byte-deterministic given the W18 named set, the witness counts, and the candidate set — the inversion guard fires iff ``0 < |N| < |U|`` AND ``max_aw(U \\ N) > max_aw(N)``; the confound refinement fires iff W18 abstained AND there is a unique strict-max-aw subset M ⊊ U with ``|M| ≥ 1``; otherwise W19 falls through to W18; (d) the W19 method consumes only the W18-packed bundle (which itself reads only the W15-packed bundle) — no extra capsule reads, no global state — so token-budget accounting is byte-for-byte preserved (bounded-context honesty).** | **proved (by inspection) + mechanically-checked** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::BundleContradictionDisambiguator,_w19_canonical_primary_index,_w19_witness_counts,_INCIDENT_TRIAGE_CANONICAL_ROLE_FOR_KIND`; `W19PrimaryIndexTests`, `W19WitnessCountsTests`, `W19DecoderUnitTests`, `Phase66TokenEfficiencyTests`. |
