The W19 surface is purely additive on top of the W18 surface; with ``enabled = False`` it reduces to W18 byte-for-byte. **All prior coordpy tests pass** (450 / 450 in the coordpy suite: 405 pre-existing + 45 new W19 tests).** | **proved-empirical (cross-regime audit)** | `Phase66BackwardCompatTests::test_w19_matches_w18_on_phase58_default,..._matches_w18_on_phase65_default_banks`; `vision_mvp/tests/` (full coordpy suite). |
| **W19-Λ-total (SDK v3.20; new)** | **W19-Λ-total falsifier (proved-empirical n=8 saturated): on the R-66-DECEIVE-TOTAL bank where the round-2 disambiguator's primary mentions DECOY service tags ONLY AND there is *no* secondary specific-tier witness anywhere in the bundle, the bundle is exhausted of asymmetric signal: every admitted tag's W19 witness count is zero; the W19 inversion guard cannot fire; the W19 confound refinement cannot find a strict-max subset; W19 reduces to W18 byte-for-byte and FAILS at ``accuracy_full = 0.000`` (W19 picks decoy via the ``W19_BRANCH_PRIMARY_TRUSTED`` branch, exactly as W18 does on R-65-DECEIVE). Names the structural limit when the bundle is exhausted of asymmetric signal — the closed-form bundle-only scope cannot escape this regime; the natural escape is outside information (W19-C-OUTSIDE, conjectural).** | **proved-empirical (n=8 falsifier saturated) + structural sketch** | `docs/data/phase66_cross_regime_synthetic.json::r66_deceive_total`; `Phase66FalsifierTests::test_w19_lambda_total_ties_fifo`; structural: zero witnesses → W19 inversion guard cannot fire → W19 reduces to W18 → W18 trusts decoy-only primary → fail. |
| **W19-Λ-outside (SDK v3.20; new)** | **W19-Λ-outside falsifier (proved-empirical n=8 saturated): on the R-66-OUTSIDE-REQUIRED bank where the round-2 disambiguator's primary mentions DECOY service tags ONLY AND the secondary witness mentions BOTH gold AND decoy service tags (so the asymmetric-witness count is uniform across all admitted tags), the W19 confound refinement cannot find a unique strict-max-aw subset; W19 abstains via ``W19_BRANCH_ABSTAINED_SYMMETRIC``; ties FIFO at ``accuracy_full = 0.000`` on 8/8 cells. Names the structural limit when bundle-internal contradiction is itself symmetric — the closed-form bundle-only scope cannot escape this regime; the natural escape is outside information (W19-C-OUTSIDE, conjectural).** | **proved-empirical (n=8 falsifier saturated) + structural sketch** | `docs/data/phase66_cross_regime_synthetic.json::r66_outside_required`; `Phase66FalsifierTests::test_w19_lambda_outside_ties_fifo_via_abstention`; structural: uniform aw → no strict max → abstain → tie FIFO. |
| **W19-C-LEARNED (SDK v3.20; new)** | **Learned bundle-contradiction trust scorer: a small distilled trust scorer (e.g. logistic regression over per-tag witness-count features plus character-bigram bundle features OR a learned sequence-pair scorer over the primary's and secondary's payload bytes) outperforms the closed-form witness-count rule on a held-out cross-bench when the LLM emits free-form natural-language asymmetric witnesses outside the synthetic bench's exact-match closure. Falsifier: a held-out cross-bench where the learned scorer ties or loses to the closed-form rule by ≥ 0.05 across 5/5 random splits.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.20; the closed-form scorer is the W19-1 anchor). |
| **W19-C-OUTSIDE (SDK v3.20; new)** | **Outside-information escape from W19-Λ-total AND W19-Λ-outside: a scorer with access to an outside-information axis (e.g. service-graph topology, prior reliability scores, cross-incident historical evidence, an external service registry) can detect the W19-Λ-total regime by cross-referencing the primary's named service tags against an outside source AND can break the W19-Λ-outside symmetry by appealing to outside-source asymmetry (e.g. "gold service A has a documented dependency on gold service B; decoy has none"). Falsifier: a hand-constructed adversarial setting where the outside source is itself compromised AND the deceptive primary AND symmetric witnesses are all internally consistent with the outside source. Honest cap: even with outside information, an adversarially-crafted joint deception (primary + secondary + outside source all internally consistent) bounds the closed-form scorer's reach; the W19-C-OUTSIDE escape is *partial* by design — it widens the bundle-only scope to "bundle + outside source", but it does not escape *every* possible adversarial regime.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.20; named structural escape from BOTH W19-Λ-total and W19-Λ-outside falsifiers). |
| **W19-Λ-real (SDK v3.20; new)** | **Real-LLM transfer of the W19 method: when a real LLM produces the round-2 disambiguator AND the secondary witness (instead of the synthetic ``IdentityExtractor``), the W19 strict gain on R-66-DECEIVE-NAIVE / R-66-CONFOUND-RESOLVABLE transfers iff (a) the LLM emits the secondary witness in the same closed-vocabulary form (synonym specific-tier kinds + relational-compound payloads); AND (b) the secondary witness is from a *non-canonical* producer role (so the ``_w19_canonical_primary_index`` correctly identifies the canonical primary). Honest scope: free-form natural-language witnesses (e.g. ``"the affected services are orders and payments"`` instead of ``"DEADLOCK_DETECTED relation=orders_payments_join"``) fall *outside* the W19 exact-match closure by construction; W19-Λ-real is partially closed when the LLM is prompted to emit closed-vocabulary secondary witnesses (analogous to W14 structured-prompt + W17 magnitude-hinted) and conjectural otherwise. Falsifier: a real-LLM probe on R-66-DECEIVE-NAIVE where the LLM emits witnesses outside the closure on > 30 % of cells AND W19 ties FIFO at 0.000 on the corresponding cells.** | **proved-conditional + empirical-research / conjectural-empirical-on-Mac-1** (Mac-1 reachable + the LLM's secondary-witness emission style observed). |
| **W19-C-CROSS-BENCH (SDK v3.20; new)** | **Cross-bench transfer of the bundle-contradiction-aware trust scorer: the W19 method generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits (a) a closed-vocabulary specific-tier set, AND (b) a canonical-role-for-kind mapping (analogous to :data:`_INCIDENT_TRIAGE_CANONICAL_ROLE_FOR_KIND`) so the canonical primary is identifiable, AND (c) at least one specific-tier witness in the union from a non-canonical role. Falsifier: a benchmark family where the round-2 disambiguator family does not admit either a closed-vocabulary specific-tier set OR a canonical-role-for-kind mapping AND no closed-form scorer can produce a strict gain over the W18 baseline.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.20; only the incident-triage canonical-role-for-kind table ships). |

## Outside-witness acquisition disambiguator (W20-Λ-outside-extension, W20-Λ-none, W20-Λ-compromised, W20-Λ-joint-deception, W20-1..W20-3, W20-Λ-real, W20-C-LEARNED, W20-C-MULTI-ORACLE, W20-C-LIVE-WITH-REGISTRY, W20-C-CROSS-BENCH) — SDK v3.21

| Theorem | Statement | Status | Anchor |
| ------- | --------- | ------ | ------ |
| **W20-Λ-outside-extension (SDK v3.21; extension of W19-Λ-outside)** | **W19-Λ-outside extends verbatim to R-67-OUTSIDE-REQUIRED-BASELINE for every closed-form bundle-only scorer including W19 itself: on the R-67-OUTSIDE-REQUIRED bundle shape (deceptive primary mentions decoy only AND symmetric secondary witness mentions all three), with no oracle registered (or an :class:`AbstainingOracle`), every capsule strategy in the SDK pre-W20 — substrate FIFO, capsule_fifo, capsule_priority, capsule_coverage, W7-2 cohort, W8 corroboration, W9 multi-service, W11 multi-round, W12 robust-multi-round, W13 layered, W15 ``AttentionAwareBundleDecoder``, W18 ``RelationalCompatibilityDisambiguator``, AND W19 ``BundleContradictionDisambiguator`` — ties FIFO at ``accuracy_full = 0.000``. Sketch: W19's witness counter sees uniform aw across {gold_A, gold_B, decoy} (the symmetric secondary mentions all three) → confound branch finds no strict-max subset proper of admitted_tags → abstains via ``W19_BRANCH_ABSTAINED_SYMMETRIC``. The wall is real and structural for every bundle-only scorer.** | **proved-empirical (n=8 saturated × 5 seeds) + structural sketch** | `docs/data/phase67_cross_regime_K12_n8.json::r67_outside_required_baseline.pooled` (every capsule strategy at 0.000); `docs/data/phase67_seed_sweep_loose_K12_n8.json` (5/5 seeds reproduce). |
| **W20-1 (SDK v3.21)** | **Outside-witness acquisition disambiguator sufficiency on the bundle-only-insufficient-but-outside-resolvable regime: pairing the W19 ``BundleContradictionDisambiguator`` with the new ``OutsideWitnessAcquisitionDisambiguator`` (W20: when inner W19 returns a trigger branch — default ``{W19_BRANCH_ABSTAINED_SYMMETRIC, W19_BRANCH_ABSTAINED_NO_SIGNAL}`` — issues exactly one hypothesis-conditioned :class:`OutsideQuery` carrying admitted_tags + elected_root_cause + primary_payload + witness_payloads; bounded by ``max_response_tokens``; truncates the oracle's reply; tokenises through the same closure W18 / W19 use; projects the answer onto the positive set of admitted-tag mentions in the reply) over a deterministic :class:`ServiceGraphOracle` achieves ``accuracy_full = 1.000`` on R-67-OUTSIDE-RESOLVES-LOOSE (``T_decoder = None``) AND R-67-OUTSIDE-RESOLVES-TIGHT (``T_decoder = 24``), strictly improving over every non-W20 capsule baseline including W19 by ``+1.000`` on both, stable across 5/5 alternate ``bank_seed`` values (11, 17, 23, 29, 31). Min gap ``w20 − w19 = +1.000`` per seed (saturated; well above the 0.50 strong-bar threshold). Also verified at n=12 (``+1.000`` strict gain). The first capsule-native multi-agent-coordination method that crosses the W19-Λ-outside wall on a regime where the wall actually applies.** | **proved-conditional + proved-empirical (n=80 saturated across 5 seeds × 2 budgets, also n=12)** | `docs/data/phase67_cross_regime_K12_n8.json::r67_outside_resolves_loose,r67_outside_resolves_tight`; `docs/data/phase67_seed_sweep_loose_K12_n8.json`, `phase67_seed_sweep_tight_K12_n8.json`; `Phase67DefaultConfigTests::test_w20_strict_win_resolves_loose,..._tight`; `Phase67SeedStabilityTests::test_loose_min_gap_at_strong_bar,..._tight`. |
| **W20-2 (SDK v3.21)** | **W20 determinism + closed-form correctness (proved by inspection + mechanically-checked): (a) ``OutsideWitnessAcquisitionDisambiguator.decode_rounds`` is byte-deterministic given a deterministic oracle; (b) the W20 trigger gate is byte-deterministic given the inner W19 branch and the configured trigger set; (c) the per-tag outside-witness count is byte-deterministic given the oracle's reply tokens and the admitted-tag list — uses the SAME ``_relational_compatibility_score`` W18 / W19 use; (d) the W20 projection is positive-set: every admitted tag the oracle's reply mentions at all is in the projected ``services`` answer; abstain on null hit / full-set hit / empty admitted set; (e) the W20 method consumes only the W15-packed bundle (which itself is shared with W18 / W19) — no extra capsule reads, no global state — so token-budget accounting is byte-for-byte preserved (bounded-context honesty); (f) ``n_outside_tokens`` is recorded as a strict additional cost separate from ``tokens_kept``.** | **proved (by inspection) + mechanically-checked** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::OutsideWitnessAcquisitionDisambiguator,OutsideWitnessOracle,ServiceGraphOracle,OutsideQuery,OutsideVerdict,W20OutsideResult`; `ServiceGraphOracleTests`, `W20DecoderUnitTests`, `Phase67TokenBudgetHonestyTests`. |
| **W20-3 (SDK v3.21)** | **Backward-compat with R-54..R-66 (proved-empirical full programme regression): on R-54..R-66 default banks, the W20 method ties the W19 method byte-for-byte on the answer field — either via ``W20_BRANCH_NO_TRIGGER`` (W19 returns a non-trigger branch — INVERSION / CONFOUND_RESOLVED / PRIMARY_TRUSTED) or via ``W20_BRANCH_OUTSIDE_ABSTAINED`` (oracle returns ``None``). On R-67-OUTSIDE-REQUIRED-BASELINE (no oracle / abstaining oracle) W20 ties W19 byte-for-byte AND ties FIFO at 0.000. With ``enabled = False`` it reduces to W19 byte-for-byte. The W20 surface is purely additive on top of the W19 surface. **All prior coordpy tests pass** (585 / 585 in the coordpy suite: 545 pre-existing + 40 new W20 tests).** | **proved-empirical (cross-regime audit)** | `Phase67BackwardCompatTests::test_w20_matches_w19_on_phase66_default_banks,..._w20_disabled_reduces_to_w19_byte_for_byte`; `vision_mvp/tests/` (full coordpy suite). |
| **W20-Λ-none (SDK v3.21; new)** | **W20-Λ-none falsifier (proved-empirical n=8 saturated): on the R-67-OUTSIDE-NONE bank where the registered :class:`AbstainingOracle` returns ``None`` for every cell, W20 falls through to W19's symmetric abstention; ``accuracy_full = 0.000`` on 8/8 cells; W20 branches: ``outside_abstained: 8``. Names the structural limit when the registered outside source has no signal — the W20 escape requires an oracle that actually produces an asymmetric reply.** | **proved-empirical (n=8 falsifier saturated) + structural sketch** | `docs/data/phase67_cross_regime_K12_n8.json::r67_outside_none`; `Phase67FalsifierTests::test_w20_lambda_none_ties_fifo`; structural: oracle returns None → W20 falls through to W19's symmetric abstention. |
| **W20-Λ-compromised (SDK v3.21; new)** | **W20-Λ-compromised falsifier (proved-empirical n=8 saturated): on the R-67-OUTSIDE-COMPROMISED bank where the registered :class:`CompromisedServiceGraphOracle` returns a payload mentioning ONLY the decoy service (the gold-set blacklist), W20 trusts the oracle and projects the answer to the decoy set; ``accuracy_full = 0.000`` on 8/8 cells; W20 branches: ``outside_resolved: 8`` (the branch fires but the projected services are wrong). Names the structural limit when the outside source itself is adversarial — the W20-1 escape is *partial* by design, bounded above by oracle integrity.** | **proved-empirical (n=8 falsifier saturated) + structural sketch** | `docs/data/phase67_cross_regime_K12_n8.json::r67_outside_compromised`; `Phase67FalsifierTests::test_w20_lambda_compromised_fails`. |
| **W20-Λ-joint-deception (SDK v3.21; new)** | **W20-Λ-joint-deception falsifier (proved-empirical n=8 saturated): on the R-67-JOINT-DECEPTION bank where primary + secondary + oracle ALL favour decoy AND are internally consistent, no single-oracle cross-check can detect the deception. W20 trusts the oracle and projects to the decoy set; ``accuracy_full = 0.000`` on 8/8 cells. Names the structural limit when *all* evidence channels are jointly compromised — the natural escape (W20-C-MULTI-ORACLE) consults *multiple* outside oracles and aggregates; remains conjectural and is itself bounded by joint-N-oracle compromise.** | **proved-empirical (n=8 falsifier saturated) + structural sketch** | `docs/data/phase67_cross_regime_K12_n8.json::r67_joint_deception`; `Phase67FalsifierTests::test_w20_lambda_joint_deception_fails`. |
| **W20-Λ-real (SDK v3.21; new)** | **Real-LLM transfer of the W20 method via :class:`LLMAdjudicatorOracle`: when the registered outside oracle is a real LLM (instead of the deterministic :class:`ServiceGraphOracle`), the W20-1 strict gain on R-67-OUTSIDE-RESOLVES transfers iff the LLM's reply token set finds asymmetric service mentions through the same closure W19 / W18 / W13 share. Empirical n=4 probe on Mac-1 Ollama: ``mixtral:8x7b`` (47B-MoE) free-form reply (``"Based on the provided information, the deadlock occurred between the orders and payments service"``) lands gold tokens asymmetrically and achieves ``acc_full = 0.750`` (3/4 cells, 1 cell oracle replied with no admitted-tag tokens → outside_abstained); +0.750 strict gain over W19 on a fresh live LLM. ``qwen2.5-coder:7b`` trusts the deceptive primary on every fired cell (``services=cache``) and FAILS at ``acc_full = 0.000`` — under-scaled-model failure mode. Cross-model split: scale + general knowledge correlates with W20-Λ-real escape; smaller / coding-specialised models can fall into the deception. Honest cap: free-form natural-language replies that do not mention any admitted tag fall *outside* the W20 closure by construction; the natural extensions are W20-C-LIVE-WITH-REGISTRY and W20-C-LEARNED (both conjectural). Falsifier: a real-LLM probe on R-67-OUTSIDE-RESOLVES where the LLM emits asymmetric mentions on < 30 % of cells AND W20 ties W19 on the corresponding cells.** | **proved-conditional + empirical-research / conjectural-empirical-on-Mac-1** | `docs/data/phase67_live_mixtral_8x7b_n4.json` (acc_full=0.750), `docs/data/phase67_live_qwen2_5_coder_7b_n4.json` (acc_full=0.000); cross-model split documented in `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_OUTSIDE_INFORMATION.md`. |
| **W20-C-LEARNED (SDK v3.21; new)** | **Learned outside-source scorer: a small distilled outside-source aggregator (e.g. a learned trust-weighted aggregator over multiple oracle replies + character-bigram bundle features) outperforms the closed-form positive-set rule on a held-out cross-bench where the LLM emits free-form replies outside the synthetic exact-match closure. Falsifier: a held-out cross-bench where the learned scorer ties or loses to the closed-form rule by ≥ 0.05 across 5/5 random splits.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.21; the closed-form scorer is the W20-1 anchor). |
| **W20-C-MULTI-ORACLE (SDK v3.21; new)** | **Multi-oracle aggregation escape from W20-Λ-compromised: consulting *multiple* outside oracles (e.g. service-graph + change-history + on-call notes + LLM adjudicator) and aggregating via majority / weighted vote escapes W20-Λ-compromised when *some* oracles remain trustworthy. The W20-C-MULTI-ORACLE axis is bounded above by the same closed-vocabulary closure; aggregation is a research move, not a structural escape from joint-deception (W20-Λ-joint-deception remains the wall on N-oracle aggregation when ALL N are compromised). Falsifier: a hand-constructed adversarial setting where ≥ ⌈N/2⌉ of the registered oracles are jointly compromised AND the aggregated W20 method ties FIFO at 0.000.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.21; named structural escape from the W20-Λ-compromised falsifier on the bounded-corruption regime). |
| **W20-C-LIVE-WITH-REGISTRY (SDK v3.21; new)** | **LLM adjudicator with explicit service-registry context: when the :class:`LLMAdjudicatorOracle`'s prompt includes the closed-vocabulary service registry (or the relevant subset for the admitted tags) AND the LLM is constrained to reply with service-tag tokens from the registry, the W20-Λ-real wall narrows substantially — the LLM can no longer fall into the deceptive primary because the registry asymmetry is stated in the prompt. Falsifier: a fresh live probe where the registry-prompt LLM ties FIFO at 0.000 on R-67-OUTSIDE-RESOLVES across ≥ 5 / 8 cells.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.21; the closed-form ServiceGraphOracle achieves the same effect mechanically without an LLM). |
| **W20-C-CROSS-BENCH (SDK v3.21; new)** | **Cross-bench transfer of the outside-witness acquisition method: the W20 method generalises to non-incident-triage benchmark families when the family admits (a) a closed-vocabulary specific-tier set, AND (b) an outside source whose reply token set finds asymmetric mentions through the closed-vocabulary closure (e.g. distributed-tracing service graphs, dependency manifests, configuration databases). Falsifier: a benchmark family where the only available outside source emits free-form natural-language replies AND no closed-form scorer over those replies produces a strict gain over the W19 baseline.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.21; only the incident-triage service-graph ships). |

## Trust-weighted multi-oracle adjudicator (W21-1..W21-3-B, W21-Λ-no-quorum, W21-Λ-all-compromised, W21-Λ-partial, W21-Λ-real, W21-C-CALIBRATED-TRUST, W21-C-LIVE-WITH-REGISTRY) — SDK v3.22

| **W21-1 (SDK v3.22)** | **Trust-weighted multi-oracle adjudicator sufficiency on the W20-Λ-compromised regime: pairing the W19 ``BundleContradictionDisambiguator`` with the new ``TrustWeightedMultiOracleDisambiguator`` (W21: when inner W19 returns a trigger branch, issues exactly N hypothesis-conditioned :class:`OutsideQuery` queries — one per registered :class:`OracleRegistration` — bounded by ``max_response_tokens`` per call; tokenises each reply through the same closure W18 / W19 use; counts per-tag votes across non-abstaining oracles; projects the answer onto tags with ≥ ``quorum_min`` votes AND ≥ ``min_trust_sum`` trust mass) over a three-oracle registered set ``(compromised_registry first, service_graph, change_history)`` under default ``quorum_min = 2`` achieves ``accuracy_full = 1.000`` on R-68-MULTI-MAJORITY-LOOSE (``T_decoder = None``) AND R-68-MULTI-MAJORITY-TIGHT (``T_decoder = 24``), strictly improving over every non-W21 capsule baseline including W20 (which trusts the first-registered compromised oracle and FAILS at 0.000) by ``+1.000``, stable across 5/5 alternate ``bank_seed`` values (11, 17, 23, 29, 31). | **W21-Λ-partial (SDK v3.22; new)** | **W21-Λ-partial falsifier under default ``quorum_min = 2`` (proved-empirical n=8 saturated): on the R-68-MULTI-PARTIAL bank where two partial-honest :class:`OnCallNotesOracle` instances each emit a different element of the gold pair (no overlap) plus one :class:`AbstainingOracle`, each gold tag receives exactly one vote; no tag reaches ``quorum_min = 2``; W21 abstains via ``W21_BRANCH_NO_QUORUM``; ``accuracy_full = 0.000`` on 8/8 cells. Names the trade-off between quorum strictness and partial-evidence recovery. The conditional W21-C-PARTIAL-RECOVERY (with ``quorum_min = 1``, W21 recovers the gold pair on the same regime — empirically discharged at n=8 in `docs/data/phase68_cross_regime_K12_n8.json::r68_multi_partial_q1`) is *empirical-on-default-config* but **not** strict at the default ``quorum_min = 2``.** | **proved-empirical (n=8 falsifier saturated under default config; conditional recovery proved-empirical n=8 under override)** | `docs/data/phase68_cross_regime_K12_n8.json::r68_multi_partial,r68_multi_partial_q1`; `Phase68FalsifierTests::test_w21_lambda_partial_default_q2`; `Phase68ConditionalSuccessTests::test_w21_partial_with_quorum_min_1_wins`. |
| **W21-Λ-real (SDK v3.22; new)** | **Real-LLM transfer of the W21 method via :class:`LLMAdjudicatorOracle` as a registered oracle: when one of the registered oracles is a real LLM (alongside deterministic registry oracles), the W21-1 strict gain on R-68-MULTI-MAJORITY transfers iff (a) the deterministic registry alone provides quorum=2 on gold (registry-anchored regime: trivially, +1.000 over W20), OR (b) the LLM's vote is required for quorum AND the LLM lands gold tokens through the W18/W19 closure (coalition regime: cross-model dependent). Empirical n=4 probes on Mac-1 Ollama on the **coalition regime** (1 honest deterministic + 1 LLM + 1 compromised, ``quorum_min = 2``): ``ollama_mixtral:8x7b`` (47B-MoE) lands gold tokens on 3/4 cells → W21 ``acc_full = 0.750``, +0.750 over W20; ``ollama_gemma2:9b`` (9.2B-dense) lands decoy tokens through the closure on 3/4 cells → quorum forms on decoy → W21 ``acc_full = 0.000``, +0.000 over W20. Cross-model split (47B-MoE 0.750 / 9.2B-dense 0.000) is sharp; **scale + general knowledge matter for the W21-Λ-real escape on the LLM-vote-required regime**. The closed-form deterministic registry remains the load-bearing oracle on the synthetic anchor; the live LLM adjudicator path is *probabilistic*.** | **proved-conditional + empirical-research (n=4 saturated × 2 models, two regimes)** | `docs/data/phase68_live_mixed_registry_mixtral_n4.json` (registry-anchored: acc_full=1.000), `phase68_live_coalition_mixtral_n4.json` (coalition: acc_full=0.750), `phase68_live_coalition_gemma2_9b_n4.json` (coalition: acc_full=0.000); cross-model split documented in `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_MULTI_ORACLE_ADJUDICATION.md`. |
| **W21-C-CALIBRATED-TRUST (SDK v3.22; new)** | **Calibrated trust priors escape W21-Λ-all-compromised on bounded-corruption regimes: with trust priors calibrated against held-out historical agreement, a low prior on an uncalibrated / suspected-compromised oracle excludes its vote from quorum aggregation via the ``min_trust_sum`` floor — escapes W21-Λ-all-compromised on regimes where ≥ ``quorum_min`` calibrated oracles remain honest. Falsifier: a hand-constructed adversarial setting where every registered oracle's prior is mis-calibrated (compromised oracles given high priors) AND the W21 method ties W21-Λ-all-compromised at 0.000.** | **conjectural** (out of scope for SDK v3.22; the closed-form ``min_trust_sum = 0.0`` default treats every oracle as equally trusted). |
| **W21-C-LIVE-WITH-REGISTRY (SDK v3.22; partially discharged)** | **LLM adjudicator paired with a deterministic registry as registered "trusted registry" channels: an :class:`LLMAdjudicatorOracle` is registered alongside ≥ 2 deterministic registry oracles (e.g. ``ServiceGraphOracle`` + ``ChangeHistoryOracle``); the deterministic two form quorum=2 on gold *regardless* of whether the LLM lands in the W18/W19 closure. Empirical n=4 × Mac-1 mixtral:8x7b: W21 ``acc_full = 1.000``, +1.000 over W20 (the deterministic registry alone forms quorum). The W21-C-LIVE-WITH-REGISTRY conjecture from SDK v3.21 is therefore **partially discharged**: the live multi-source story works even without the LLM landing in the W18/W19 closure. Falsifier: a fresh live probe on a stricter coalition regime where the deterministic registry alone is insufficient (1 honest deterministic + 1 LLM + 1 compromised) AND the LLM ties FIFO at 0.000 across 5/5 random cross-model probes.** | **proved-conditional + empirical-research (partially discharged at n=4 × mixtral 8x7b on Mac-1; cross-model split sharp)** | `docs/data/phase68_live_mixed_registry_mixtral_n4.json`; `docs/data/phase68_live_coalition_mixtral_n4.json`. |

| **W22-C-CACHE-AMPLIFICATION (SDK v3.23; conjectural, named for the first time)** | **When a probabilistic LLM oracle is registered alongside deterministic oracles in a W22 stack with a ``SharedReadCache``, the cache returns the *first* recorded reply for every subsequent identical OutsideQuery. This freezes the LLM's first sample as the canonical reply across the session. **Conjecture**: in expectation over (model, prompt) pairs at temperature=0, this *amplifies* the variance of the per-cell vote outcome — bad first replies poison many cells; good first replies stabilise many cells. Empirically observed on mixtral:8x7b at temperature=0 on Mac-1 (3/4 cells ratified, 1/4 drifts). **Falsifier**: an LLM adjudicator that is byte-stable across separate sessions (true determinism) would produce ``correctness_ratified_rate = 1.000`` on every cell. *(SDK v3.24: empirically discharged as mitigable on R-70-AMPLIFIED-LLM by W23-2 quorum-keyed cache.)*** | **conjectural; mitigation discharged-empirical (SDK v3.24)** | `docs/data/phase69_live_mixtral_8x7b_n4.json`; `docs/data/phase70_amplified_llm_K12_n8.json`. |

| **W26-L (SDK v3.27; chain-amortisation lower bound)** | **Any capsule-native multi-agent coordination strategy whose producer emits only its own compact state and whose consumers reference it via 1-token-per-cell tokens has a per-cell total visible cost ≥ 1 + K (the floor: 1 producer token + K consumer tokens). W26 attains this floor on every in-window advance cell; the full per-window cost is ``C + K + (W-1)(1 + K)`` where ``W = chain_persist_window`` and ``C = n_w24_visible_tokens_to_decider`` per agent. Proof by inspection: the chain advance token is one whitespace token by ``_whitespace_token_count``; the consumer chain ref is one whitespace token; the visible cost cannot be reduced further without removing either the producer's chain reference or the consumer's resolution reference (which would break the trust boundary).** | **proved (by inspection)** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::ChainAdvanceEnvelope.n_advance_tokens,ChainPersistedFanoutDisambiguator.decode_rounds`; `Phase73ChainSharedTests::test_w26_one_anchor_n_advances` empirically witnesses the floor. |
| **W26-C-K-SCALING (SDK v3.27; conjectural)** | **At fixed ``chain_persist_window = N`` and K consumers, the W26 mean visible cost per cell tends to ``(C + K) / N + (1 + K) × (N-1) / N → 1 + K`` as N → ∞ for stable benches. Measured at K∈{3,5,8,10} on R-73-CHAIN-SHARED with N=16: 5.50 / 7.50 / 10.50 / 12.50 tokens/cell. The advance-cell floor of 1+K dominates the mean at K=10. **Conjecture**: at K → ∞, W26 mean visible cost → K + 1 + (C-1)/N (anchor amortisation), bounded by `1 + K` for any finite N ≥ 1. **Falsifier**: on a workload where the anchor cell's W25 cost grows with K beyond C (e.g. because ``projection_slots`` scales O(K) bytes), the K=∞ asymptote would exceed 1+K. Measured at K=3 only on R-73-CHAIN-SHARED; the 1+K floor is empirically confirmed at K∈{3,5,8,10}.** | **conjectural (K∈{3,5,8,10} measured; K→∞ asymptote unverified)** | `docs/data/phase73_k_scaling.json`; `Phase73KScalingTests::test_w26_savings_over_w24_grows_with_K`. |
| **W26-C-MULTI-HOST (SDK v3.27; conjectural)** | **The W26 ``ChainAnchorEnvelope`` serialises to ≈ 700 bytes (JSON; measured at 701 bytes in R-73-CHAIN-SHARED) and each ``ChainAdvanceEnvelope`` serialises to ≈ 460 bytes (≈ 6,969 bytes / 15 advances). Total wire bytes per chain window: anchor + (W-1) × advance ≈ 700 + 15×460 ≈ 7,600 bytes (vs W25's ~5,885 bytes/16 cells = 367 bytes/cell). **Conjecture**: on a real multi-host deployment, the W26 wire-vs-token tradeoff favours W26 over W25 whenever ``token_cost × (C-1) × (W-1) > advance_bytes/cell × wire_cost × W``. **Falsifier**: a deployment where wire cost per byte exceeds token cost per token + chain-window length is short would make W26 a net loss vs W25. Mac 2 has been ARP-incomplete for 21 consecutive milestones; no real two-host measurement exists. The W24 ``CrossProcessProducerDecoderWire`` (real Python subprocess) is the strongest cross-process honesty validated on this repo and inherited by W26.** | **conjectural** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W26_CHAIN_PERSISTED_FANOUT.md §10`. |

Measured at M ∈ {1, 2} on R-74; the M → ∞ asymptote is unverified.** | **conjectural (M ∈ {1, 2} measured; M → ∞ asymptote unverified)** | `docs/data/phase74_cross_regime.json`, `phase74_signature_period_sweep.json`. |

| **W28-C-CALIBRATED-TRUST (SDK v3.29; conjectural)** | **Trust priors calibrated from held-out probe agreement strictly outperform uniform priors on a held-out test set (analogue of W21-C-CALIBRATED-TRUST). **Falsifier**: a regime where probes are independent of agreement history (i.e. agreement is uncorrelated with future agreement) would make uniform priors optimal. Not exercised in this milestone — natural follow-up.** | **conjectural** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W28_ENSEMBLE_VERIFIED_MULTI_CHAIN.md §6`. |

Cumulative trust boundary across W29 + W30 + W31 = 42 enumerated failure modes.** | **proved (by inspection) + mechanically-checked** | `W31VerifierFailureModeTests` (20 mode tests covering every failure mode plus internal/cross-cell sub-axes, all green); `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::verify_online_calibrated_ratification`. |
| **W31-2 (SDK v3.32)** | **Trivial-online byte-for-W30 reduction: with ``online_enabled=False``, ``manifest_disabled=True``, ``trajectory_window=0``, the W31 layer's per-cell visible-token cost equals W30's byte-for-byte; ``mean_total_w31_visible_tokens == mean_total_w30_visible_tokens`` byte-for-byte on R-78-TRIVIAL-W31 across 5/5 seeds; every cell yields ``W31_BRANCH_TRIVIAL_ONLINE_PASSTHROUGH``. | **W31-3 (SDK v3.32; discharges W30-C-PRIOR-LEARNING)** | **Online prior-learning discharge on R-78-NONSTATIONARY-PRIOR: when the W31 layer is configured with ``online_enabled=True``, ``adaptive_threshold=True``, ``trajectory_window=16`` and the regime has a non-stationary per-partition agreement-rate distribution (CYCLIC=PARTIAL oracle, LINEAR=FULL oracle on the inverted layout), the closed-form running-mean update inside ``OnlineCalibratedOrchestrator`` drives the per-partition prior toward the regime's true agreement-rate distribution; the clipped-median adaptive threshold (median of (1.0, 1.0, 0.6667) clipped to [0.20, 0.80] = 0.8) makes the W30 reroute fire on subsequent CYCLIC cells; ``correctness_ratified_rate_w31 - correctness_ratified_rate_w30 ≥ +0.10`` AND ``trust_precision_w31 = 1.000`` across 5/5 seeds.  Measured: Δ=+0.125, trust_prec=1.000, max overhead = 1 token/cell.  **This is the W30-C-PRIOR-LEARNING empirical discharge** — the FIRST capsule-native multi-agent-coordination method to demonstrate that the closed-form Bayesian-style running-mean update can drive the per-partition calibration prior to track a non-stationary agreement-rate distribution at no extra wire-token cost.  **Falsifier**: in regimes where per-partition agreement-rate is stationary (W31-Λ-no-drift on R-78-NO-DRIFT) OR with frozen threshold = 0.5 (W31-Λ-frozen-threshold on R-78-FROZEN-THRESHOLD), Δ=0.** | **proved-conditional + proved-empirical (5/5 seeds)** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W31_ONLINE_CALIBRATED_GEOMETRY.md §4.1`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase78/nonstationary_prior_seed_sweep.json`; `W31BenchTests::test_h6_nonstationary_prior_clears_delta_010`. |
| **W31-4 (SDK v3.32)** | **Adaptive-threshold strict contribution on R-78-ADAPTIVE-THRESHOLD vs R-78-FROZEN-THRESHOLD: with the same online-learned prior, ``adaptive_threshold=True`` (clipped-median bounded to [0.20, 0.80]) strictly outperforms ``adaptive_threshold=False`` (frozen at 0.5).  Adaptive Δ vs W30 = +0.125; frozen Δ vs W30 = 0.000; difference = +0.125 ≥ +0.05 across 5/5 seeds.  This isolates the adaptive-threshold contribution from the online-prior contribution.  **Falsifier**: a regime where the running mean of every partition stays above 0.5 in the first half-session (W31-Λ-frozen-threshold) would fail to fire any reroute, regardless of adaptive logic.** | **proved-conditional + proved-empirical (5/5 seeds)** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W31_ONLINE_CALIBRATED_GEOMETRY.md §4.2`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase78/adaptive_threshold_seed_sweep.json`, `frozen_threshold_seed_sweep.json`; `W31BenchTests::test_h7_adaptive_minus_frozen_at_least_005`. |
| **W31-5 (SDK v3.32)** | **Manifest cross-component tamper detection on R-78-MANIFEST-TAMPER: the W31 envelope's ``manifest_cid`` (SHA-256 over basis_history_cid + calibration_cid + ancestor_chain_cid + prior_trajectory_cid + threshold_trajectory_cid + route_audit_cid) plus the cross-cell ``registered_prior_trajectory_cid`` check together detect five named tampers per ratified cell: cross-cell prior_trajectory swap (replace cur cell's CID with prior cell's CID, recompute manifest CID self-consistently), manifest_cid byte corruption, observed_agreement out of range, threshold_trajectory value out of range, outer w31_cid byte corruption.  **65/65 = 1.000 rejection rate** at seed 11 across 13 cell-positions × 5 tampers.  **Falsifier**: a tamper that mutates only fields not covered by any of the 14 enumerated failure modes (e.g. ``cell_index`` alone, before the outer CID is recomputed) would slip through; we explicitly cover such cases via the outer w31_cid recompute check.** | **proved-conditional + proved-empirical (1.000 reject rate)** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W31_ONLINE_CALIBRATED_GEOMETRY.md §4.3`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase78/manifest_tamper_seed_sweep.json`; `W31BenchTests::test_h8_manifest_tamper_reject_rate_above_095`. |
| **W31-Λ-trivial-online (SDK v3.32; named falsifier)** | **W31-Λ-trivial-online: at the trivial-online registry path (``online_enabled=False``, ``manifest_disabled=True``, ``trajectory_window=0``), W31 reduces to W30 byte-for-byte; no wire token charged; every cell yields ``W31_BRANCH_TRIVIAL_ONLINE_PASSTHROUGH``. | **W31-Λ-no-drift (SDK v3.32; named falsifier)** | **W31-Λ-no-drift: when the per-partition agreement-rate distribution is stationary (every partition has FULL oracle), every cell's ``observed_agreement = 1.0``; the running-mean update maintains every prior at 1.0; no reroute fires; ``correctness_ratified_rate_w31 == correctness_ratified_rate_w30`` byte-for-byte. | **W31-Λ-frozen-threshold (SDK v3.32; named falsifier)** | **W31-Λ-frozen-threshold: when ``adaptive_threshold=False``, the threshold trajectory is constant at the W30 default 0.5; on the nonstationary regime, the running mean of CYCLIC = (1+1+1+1+0+0)/6 = 0.6667 > 0.5 — never crosses threshold; no reroute fires; W31 reduces to "online prior + frozen threshold" with no adaptive contribution. | **W31-C-CROSS-HOST-VARIANCE-LIVE-MAGNITUDE-LIVE (SDK v3.32; conjectural; sharpens W30-C-CROSS-HOST-VARIANCE-LIVE-MAGNITUDE-LIVE on the gold-correlation axis)** | **On a regime where two reachable LLM hosts (gemma2:9b on localhost + qwen2.5:14b on 192.168.12.191) systematically disagree at temperature 0 AND the disagreement systematically correlates with the gold-correctness label (i.e. one model's answer is the gold answer, the other is not), the W31 disagreement-routed adjudication strictly improves correctness on live LLM bytes.  **Status**: **infrastructure-discharged on the disagreement-existence axis** — gemma2:9b vs qwen2.5:14b disagree on 2/8 = 0.250 of structured-decision prompts at temperature 0, reproducible byte-for-byte across two runs (Q5: db_query vs logs_pipeline; Q7: api vs storage).  **The first measured live cross-architecture LLM disagreement at temp 0 in the programme** (28th milestone).  The gold-correlation axis remains open: constructing prompts where the disagreement consistently picks the gold-correct vs gold-incorrect answer is the residual work for SDK v3.33.  **Falsifier**: a regime where the live LLM disagreement is uncorrelated with the gold label would not exercise the gold-correlation axis.** | **conjectural; infrastructure-discharged on the existence axis** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W31_ONLINE_CALIBRATED_GEOMETRY.md §4.6`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase78/xllm_live_agreement_probe.json`, `xllm_live_agreement_probe_run2.json`; `vision_mvp/experiments/scripts/phase78_xllm_live_probe.py`. |

| **W31-C-LONG-WINDOW-CONVERGENCE (SDK v3.32; **DISCHARGED on scaling-stability axis at SDK v3.33 / W32-3**)** | **At ``trajectory_window`` much larger than the regime-shift period, the online-learned prior tracks the agreement-rate distribution closely; the discharge gain may grow with window size.  **Status**: **DISCHARGED on scaling-stability axis at SDK v3.33 / W32-3** (W32 EWMA + Page CUSUM mechanism achieves byte-for-W31-equal correctness across 5/5 seeds × long_window ∈ {16, 32, 64, 128} = 20/20 cell-window pairs at trust precision 1.000; zero degradation as window grows). ## Long-window convergent online geometry-aware dense control + EWMA prior accumulator + Page CUSUM change-point detector + gold-correlated disagreement-routing + W32 manifest-v2 CID + first measured live cross-architecture LLM gold-verifiable agreement at temp 0 (W32-1, W32-2, W32-3, W32-4, W32-5, W32-L-CYCLE-CAP, W32-Λ-trivial-long-window, W32-Λ-no-change-point, W32-Λ-frozen-ewma, W32-Λ-mis-correlated-gold, W32-C-CROSS-HOST-LIVE-GOLD-MAGNITUDE, W32-C-LONG-WINDOW-STRICT-GAIN, W32-C-NATIVE-LATENT, W32-C-MULTI-HOST, W32-C-OLD-LINE-EWMA-TRUST) — SDK v3.33

| **W32-1 (SDK v3.33)** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the long-window convergent verifier: ``verify_long_window_convergent_ratification`` enumerates **14 failure modes** disjoint from W22..W31's (``empty_w32_envelope``, ``w32_schema_version_unknown``, ``w32_schema_cid_mismatch``, ``w31_parent_cid_mismatch``, ``convergence_state_cid_mismatch``, ``convergence_state_length_mismatch``, ``convergence_state_unregistered_partition``, ``convergence_state_ewma_out_of_range``, ``convergence_state_cusum_out_of_range``, ``ewma_alpha_out_of_range``, ``cusum_threshold_out_of_range``, ``gold_correlation_cid_mismatch``, ``manifest_v2_cid_mismatch``, ``w32_outer_cid_mismatch``).  ``convergence_state_cid_mismatch`` covers BOTH internal recompute mismatch AND the cross-cell swap (registered-vs-env CID check) — closing the swap-recomputed-self-consistent attack vector that even the W31 manifest CID could not catch.  Soundness holds by inspection on the verify_* enumeration; mechanically-checked on every cell.  Pure function; no side effects. | **W32-3 (SDK v3.33; discharges W31-C-LONG-WINDOW-CONVERGENCE on the scaling-stability axis)** | **Long-window convergent scaling-stability on R-79-LONG-WINDOW: when the W32 layer is configured with ``long_window_enabled=True``, ``change_point_enabled=True``, ``ewma_alpha=0.20``, ``cusum_threshold=1.5``, and the regime is the prefix-then-shift drift_recover regime, the EWMA accumulator + Page CUSUM detector achieves ``correctness_ratified_rate_w32 ≥ correctness_ratified_rate_w31`` byte-for-byte across **5/5 seeds × 4/4 windows = 20/20 cell-window pairs**; ``min_trust_precision_w32 = 1.000`` across all windows.  **This is the W31-C-LONG-WINDOW-CONVERGENCE empirical discharge on the scaling-stability axis** — the FIRST capsule-native multi-agent-coordination method to demonstrate that the EWMA + CUSUM mechanism is structurally stable across long windows with zero degradation.  **Falsifier**: in regimes where the cumulative running mean already tracks the regime within 0.05 of the EWMA (e.g. stationary regimes, W32-Λ-no-change-point), Δ=0.  **The strict-gain axis (Δ ≥ +0.10) is bounded above by the W32-L-CYCLE-CAP limitation theorem on cycle-capped dispatcher regimes** and inherits forward as **W32-C-LONG-WINDOW-STRICT-GAIN**.** | **proved-conditional + proved-empirical (5/5 seeds × 4/4 windows on scaling-stability axis)** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W32_LONG_WINDOW_CONVERGENT.md §4.2`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase79/long_window_sweep.json`; `W32BenchTests::test_h7_long_window_no_degradation`. |

| **W32-L-CYCLE-CAP (SDK v3.33; proved-conditional limitation theorem)** | **The maximum strict correctness gain Δ(W32 - W31) on a long-window prefix-then-shift regime is bounded above by ``min(c_p / 4, c_s) / N`` where ``c_p`` is the prefix-CYCLIC-classified cell count, ``c_s`` is the shift-CYCLIC-classified cell count, and ``N`` is the total bench size.  **Proof sketch**: the W31 cumulative running-mean of CYCLIC drops below the reroute threshold ``θ`` when ``(n_obs_prefix * 1) / (n_obs_prefix + k) < θ``, i.e. when ``k > n_obs_prefix * (1 - θ) / θ ≈ n_obs_prefix / 4`` for ``θ = 0.8``.  After cell ``k``, W31 reroutes correctly; before, it does not.  W32's EWMA at ``α = 0.20`` triggers reroute within 2-3 cells.  The W31-W32 gap is therefore bounded by ``min(k, c_s)`` cells out of ``N`` total.  At the W29 dispatcher's cycle-cap (cycle_window=8 with 3 partitions ⇒ ~25% of cells per partition), ``c_p / N ≤ 0.25``, so ``Δ_max ≤ 0.0625`` on cycle-capped dispatcher regimes.  **This is the structural reason the H6 +0.10 bar cannot clear on the available cycle-capped dispatcher regimes**.  **Falsifier**: a regime that exceeds the cycle-cap (e.g. a single-partition regime, or a regime where the dispatcher cycle-window is < 3) would not be subject to this bound.** | **proved (by inspection) + empirically corroborated on N=64, 96, 128 sweeps** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W32_LONG_WINDOW_CONVERGENT.md §6`. |
| **W32-Λ-trivial-long-window (SDK v3.33; named falsifier)** | **W32-Λ-trivial-long-window: at the trivial-long-window registry path (all knobs trivial), W32 reduces to W31 byte-for-byte; no wire token charged; every cell yields ``W32_BRANCH_TRIVIAL_LONG_WINDOW_PASSTHROUGH``.  Names the structural limit when no EWMA / CUSUM / gold-correlation / manifest-v2 signal is registered: empty payload carries no information beyond what W31 already has.  Empirically confirmed across 5/5 seeds on R-79-TRIVIAL-W32.** | **proved-empirical** | `W32RegistryFactoryTests::test_trivial_registry_is_trivial`; `W32BenchTests::test_h2_trivial_w32_byte_for_w31`. |
| **W32-Λ-no-change-point (SDK v3.33; named falsifier)** | **W32-Λ-no-change-point: when the per-partition agreement-rate distribution is stationary (every cell ratifies, observed_agreement=1 throughout), every EWMA stays at 1.0 and every CUSUM stays at 0; no change-points fire; ``correctness_ratified_rate_w32 == correctness_ratified_rate_w31`` byte-for-byte.  Names the structural limit when there is no agreement-rate drift to exploit.  Empirically confirmed across 5/5 seeds on R-79-NO-CHANGE-POINT (Δ=0.000, n_change_points=0).** | **proved-empirical** | `W32BenchTests::test_w32_lambda_no_change_point_falsifier`. |
| **W32-Λ-frozen-ewma (SDK v3.33; named falsifier; honest empirical correction)** | **W32-Λ-frozen-ewma: when ``ewma_alpha = 1.0`` (degenerate; EWMA reduces to "just the latest observation"), the W32 layer is predicted to regress vs W31 on a noisy regime.  **Empirical correction**: on the available R-79-FROZEN-EWMA (drift_recover) regime, alpha=1.0 slightly OUTPERFORMS alpha=0.20 by Δ=+0.016 across 5/5 seeds — the regime is non-noisy AND the latest observation is informative.  The pre-committed falsifier prediction did NOT fire; the W32 mechanism is more robust than predicted.  The pre-committed framing is retained as an honest empirical finding; the falsifier remains a *theoretical* limit that the available bench does not exercise.** | **proved-empirical (honest correction)** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W32_LONG_WINDOW_CONVERGENT.md §4.6`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase79/frozen_ewma_seed_sweep.json`. |
| **W32-Λ-mis-correlated-gold (SDK v3.33; named falsifier; gate-bounded)** | **W32-Λ-mis-correlated-gold: when the registered gold-correlation map points to the wrong partition (the one that is *less* often correct on disagreed cells), the W32 layer is predicted to regress vs W31 by firing the gold route the wrong way.  **Empirical gate-bounded**: on synthetic banks (R-79-MIS-CORRELATED-GOLD), ``n_gold_routes_fired = 0`` across 5/5 seeds because the gating condition (inner W30 ``disagreement_route_active = True``) is never satisfied without real cross-host disagreement.  The wrong gold map cannot fire ⇒ W32 ties W31.  The falsifier requires real cross-host disagreement (which the live S1 bench measures); on the available LLMs at temp 0, gold-verifiable prompts agree at 0.950, so the gate is also closed there.** | **proved-empirical (gate-bounded)** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W32_LONG_WINDOW_CONVERGENT.md §4.7`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase79/mis_correlated_gold_seed_sweep.json`. |
| **W32-C-CROSS-HOST-LIVE-GOLD-MAGNITUDE (SDK v3.33; conjectural; renamed from W31-C-CROSS-HOST-VARIANCE-LIVE-MAGNITUDE-LIVE on the gold-correlation axis)** | **On a regime where two reachable LLM hosts (gemma2:9b on localhost + qwen2.5:14b on 192.168.12.191) systematically disagree at temperature 0 on gold-verifiable structured-decision prompts AND one host is systematically correct on the disagreed prompts, the W32 gold-correlation map re-routes to the correct host AND the resulting correctness strictly improves over W31.  **Status**: **honestly null on the available LLMs at temp 0 on gold-verifiable prompts** — gemma2:9b vs qwen2.5:14b agree on 19/20 = 0.950 of arithmetic + syntax + factoid + disambiguation prompts; the unique disagreement (D5: TCP three-way handshake second packet) has neither host correct (tokenisation boundary, "synack" vs "syn-ack").  Combined with W31's R-78-XLLM-LIVE result (6/8 = 0.750 agreement on operational-decision prompts), the **prompt-class-dependent cross-architecture disagreement frontier** is now characterised: operational/strategic prompts disagree at 0.250; gold-verifiable factual prompts agree at 0.950.  **Falsifier**: a regime where the live LLM disagreement is uncorrelated with the gold label would not exercise the gold-correlation axis.** | **conjectural; honestly null on available LLMs at temp 0 on gold-verifiable prompts** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W32_LONG_WINDOW_CONVERGENT.md §4.8`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase79/xllm_live_gold_pilot.json`, `xllm_live_gold_run1.json`; `vision_mvp/experiments/scripts/phase79_xllm_gold_pilot.py`. |
| **W32-C-LONG-WINDOW-STRICT-GAIN (SDK v3.33; conjectural; renamed from H6 partial-honest-null)** | **On a regime that exceeds the W32-L-CYCLE-CAP limitation theorem (i.e. a single-partition regime, or a regime where the dispatcher cycle-window is < 3), the W32 EWMA + CUSUM mechanism strictly improves correctness over W31's cumulative running-mean by Δ ≥ +0.10.  **Status**: open; requires a custom dispatcher or single-partition bench to exercise.  **Falsifier**: a regime where the cumulative mean already tracks the regime within 0.05 of the EWMA would not show the strict-gain.** | **conjectural** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W32_LONG_WINDOW_CONVERGENT.md §6`. |
| **W32-C-NATIVE-LATENT (SDK v3.33; conjectural; carries forward W31-C-NATIVE-LATENT)** | **True transformer-internal subspace projection (Grassmannian-style hidden-state share) strictly outperforms the W32 audited-proxy basis on a comparable regime.  Architecture-dependent; explicitly out of scope for the capsule-layer SDK contract. | **W32-C-MULTI-HOST (SDK v3.33; conjectural; carries forward W31-C-MULTI-HOST)** | **Adding a third reachable host (when Mac 2 returns) strictly improves the disagreement-routing signal-to-noise on a regime where a 2-host majority is insufficient.  **Status**: hardware-bounded; 192.168.12.248 ARP-incomplete for **27 consecutive milestones** (ping 100% packet loss; port 11434 unreachable).** | **conjectural; hardware-bounded** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W32_LONG_WINDOW_CONVERGENT.md §6, §9`. |

| **W34-L-MULTI-ANCHOR-CAP (SDK v3.35; limitation theorem)** | **When all K registered anchors are simultaneously compromised at the capsule layer, no multi-anchor mechanism (including W34) can recover.  Proof by inspection: the only signal available at the capsule layer is the agreement between probes; if all K anchors agree on the wrong reference, the EWMA update converges to high agreement on the wrong direction; the intersection of the anchor top_sets matches the wrong reference; W34 ratifies the wrong answer with full trust precision (subjective).  Native-latent (architecture-dependent; W33-C-NATIVE-LATENT) is required to break this — hidden-state-level evidence cannot be spoofed by capsule-layer agreement.** | **proved (by inspection)** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W34_LIVE_AWARE_MULTI_ANCHOR.md §6 (W34-L-MULTI-ANCHOR-CAP)`. |
| **W34-Λ-trivial-multi-anchor (SDK v3.35; named falsifier)** | **W34-Λ-trivial-multi-anchor: at the trivial registry path (``multi_anchor_quorum_min=1``, ``live_attestation_disabled=True``, ``manifest_v4_disabled=True``, ``host_decay_factor=1.0``), W34 reduces to W33 byte-for-byte; no wire token charged; every cell yields ``W34_BRANCH_TRIVIAL_MULTI_ANCHOR_PASSTHROUGH``. | **W34-Λ-no-anchor-disagreement (SDK v3.35; named falsifier)** | **W34-Λ-no-anchor-disagreement: when every registered anchor agrees with the consortium throughout the bench (all-honest regime, R-81-NO-ANCHOR-DISAGREEMENT), the multi-anchor consensus reference (intersection of anchor top_sets) is the same as the single-anchor reference; W34's effective routing equals W33's; ``correctness_ratified_rate_w34 == correctness_ratified_rate_w33`` byte-for-byte.  Names the structural limit when there is no inter-anchor disagreement to exploit.  Empirically confirmed across 5/5 seeds (Δ=0.000).** | **proved-empirical** | `W34FalsifierTests::test_no_anchor_disagreement_no_lift`. |
| **W34-Λ-anchor-betrays (SDK v3.35; named falsifier)** | **W34-Λ-anchor-betrays: when the W33 single-anchor itself becomes compromised mid-session (the original W33 design has no defense against this), W33 single-anchor commits to the wrong detrust direction; W34 with K=2 + ``anchor_quorum_min=2`` recovers because the intersection of anchor top_sets collapses to empty when the anchors disagree, triggering the W34 NO_CONSENSUS abstention.  Distinct from W34-Λ-trivial-multi-anchor: this falsifier requires the multi-anchor mechanism to be *active* (K≥2) AND there to be an actual single-anchor compromise for the lift to materialise.  Empirically confirmed: W33 trust precision = 0.625; W34 trust precision = 1.000; Δ = +0.375 across 5/5 seeds on R-81-DOUBLE-ANCHOR-COMPROMISE.** | **proved-empirical** | `W34DoubleAnchorCompromiseTests::test_h6_strict_trust_precision_gain_5_seeds`; `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W34_LIVE_AWARE_MULTI_ANCHOR.md §4.2`. |
| **W34-Λ-frozen-host-decay (SDK v3.35; named falsifier)** | **W34-Λ-frozen-host-decay: when ``host_decay_factor = 1.0``, the host-aware multiplicative EWMA decay never fires; W34's effective EWMA state equals W33's regardless of host preflight outcome.  Used to attribute the host-decay axis vs the multi-anchor consensus axis.  Empirically confirmed across 5/5 seeds on R-81-FROZEN-HOST-DECAY (Δ=0.000).** | **proved-empirical** | `W34HostDecayTests::test_factor_one_no_decay`; `W34FalsifierTests::test_frozen_host_decay_no_decay`. |
| **W34-Λ-mis-feature-signature (SDK v3.35; named falsifier)** | **W34-Λ-mis-feature-signature: when two distinct LLM responses collide on the W34 response-feature signature (constructed adversarially: two prompts whose responses share first_token_class + length_bucket + structural_hash but differ semantically), the W34 mechanism detects no feature-class shift and is no worse than W33 because the signature is part of the audited *envelope*, not the *routing decision*.  Routing is driven by multi-anchor consensus, not by the signature.  Empirically confirmed: on R-81-MIS-FEATURE-SIGNATURE (all-honest regime), W34 ties W33 on correctness across 5/5 seeds.** | **proved-empirical** | `W34FalsifierTests::test_mis_feature_signature_collision_no_regression`. |
| **W34-C-CROSS-HOST-LIVE-MULTI-ANCHOR (SDK v3.35; conjectural)** | **On a regime where two reachable LLM hosts (e.g. mixtral:8x7b on localhost + qwen3.5:35b on 192.168.12.191) cross-host disagree at temperature 0 AND one host is systematically gold-correlated, the W34 multi-anchor mechanism strictly improves trust precision over W33 single-anchor on live LLM bytes.  **Status**: best-effort live evidence in `xllm_live_pilot.json`; honestly-null acceptable when the available LLMs at temp 0 agree on every prompt class.  **Falsifier**: a regime where the live LLM disagreement is uncorrelated with the gold label OR where every prompt class agrees would not exercise this axis.** | **conjectural; best-effort live evidence** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W34_LIVE_AWARE_MULTI_ANCHOR.md §4.8`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase81/xllm_live_pilot.json`; `vision_mvp/experiments/scripts/phase81_xllm_live_pilot.py`. |
| **W34-C-MULTI-HOST (SDK v3.35; conjectural; carries forward W33-C-MULTI-HOST)** | **Adding a third reachable host (when Mac 2 returns) strictly improves the multi-anchor signal-to-noise on a regime where a 2-host majority is insufficient.  **Status**: hardware-bounded; 192.168.12.248 ARP-incomplete for **29 consecutive milestones** (ping 100% packet loss; port 11434 unreachable).** | **conjectural; hardware-bounded** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W34_LIVE_AWARE_MULTI_ANCHOR.md §6, §10`. |

| **W38-2 (SDK v3.39)** | **Trivial-W38 byte-for-W37 reduction: when consensus is disabled, divergence-abstain is disabled, and manifest-v8 is disabled, W38 reduces to W37 byte-for-byte across 5/5 seeds; overhead = 0 and `all_byte_equivalent_w38_w37 = True`.** | **proved-empirical** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase85/trivial_w38_seed_sweep.json`; `W38BankTests::test_trivial_w38_byte_for_w37`. |
| **W38-3 (SDK v3.39)** | **Disjoint-consensus collusion bound (load-bearing): if the current cell would reroute a W37 trajectory-anchored top_set, AND a registered `ConsensusReferenceProbe` exists whose host topology is mechanically disjoint from W37's trajectory hosts, AND that probe's `consensus_strength >= consensus_strength_min`, AND its top_set diverges from the W37 candidate by `>= divergence_margin_min` (Jaccard), THEN W38 abstains via `CONSENSUS_DIVERGENCE_ABSTAINED` without trust-precision regression.  Measured on R-85-COLLUDED-CROSS-HOST-TRAJECTORY: W37 trust precision = 0.500; W38 trust precision = 1.000; `Δ_trust_precision_w38_w37 = +0.500` (min and max equal across 5/5 seeds); W38 abstains via DIVERGENCE on 8 cells per seed; overhead = 1 token/cell.** | **proved-conditional + proved-empirical** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase85/colluded_cross_host_trajectory_seed_sweep.json`; `W38BankTests::test_colluded_cross_host_trajectory_trust_precision_gain`. |
| **W38-4 (SDK v3.39)** | **Disjoint-topology mechanical enforcement: a `DisjointConsensusReferenceRegistry` whose `consensus_host_ids ∩ trajectory_host_ids != ∅` cannot be constructed (raises `DisjointTopologyError` in `__post_init__`); the verifier additionally rejects envelopes whose registered topology matches an overlapping host set (`w38_disjoint_topology_violation`).** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-tested** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::DisjointConsensusReferenceRegistry`; `W38RegistryTests::test_overlapping_topology_raises`; `W38VerifierTests::test_disjoint_topology_violation_rejected`. |
| **W38-5 (SDK v3.39; no-collusion-consensus-agrees no-regression)** | **When the W37 reroute agrees with the disjoint consensus reference, W38 ratifies and adds no correctness or trust-precision regression.  Measured on R-85-NO-COLLUSION-CONSENSUS-AGREES across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_correctness_w38_w37 = 0.000`; `Δ_trust_precision_w38_w37 = 0.000`.** | **proved-empirical** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase85/no_collusion_consensus_agrees_seed_sweep.json`; `W38BankTests::test_no_collusion_consensus_agrees_no_regression`. |
| **W38-6 (SDK v3.39; no-consensus-reference falsifier)** | **When no consensus reference probe is registered for the current cell, W38 returns `CONSENSUS_NO_REFERENCE` and falls through to W37's decision (NO regression).  Measured on R-85-NO-CONSENSUS-REFERENCE across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_correctness_w38_w37 = 0.000`; `Δ_trust_precision_w38_w37 = 0.000`; W38 audit envelope still records the NO_REFERENCE branch.** | **proved-empirical + proof sketch by inspection** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase85/no_consensus_reference_seed_sweep.json`; `W38BankTests::test_no_consensus_reference_preserves_w37`. |
| **W38-7 (SDK v3.39)** | **Consensus structured-state density: W38 transfers controller-verified disjoint cross-source consensus-reference state at high density while preserving auditability.  On R-85-COLLUDED-CROSS-HOST-TRAJECTORY, W38 carries roughly 9.07k structured bits per visible W38 token (mean) at one visible token overhead/cell.** | **empirical + mechanically bounded** | `DisjointConsensusReferenceRatificationEnvelope.n_structured_bits`; Phase85 artifacts. |
| **W38-L-CONSENSUS-COLLUSION-CAP (SDK v3.39; limitation theorem)** | **When the disjoint consensus reference is itself compromised in lock-step with the colluding trajectory hosts (i.e. emits the same wrong top_set), W38 cannot recover at the capsule layer.  This is the W38 analog of `W34-L-MULTI-ANCHOR-CAP` and `W37-L-MULTI-HOST-COLLUSION-CAP`.  Recovery requires native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer or a 3+-host disjoint consensus topology (W38-C-MULTI-HOST).  Measured on R-85-CONSENSUS-ALSO-COMPROMISED: `Δ_trust_precision_w38_w37 = 0.000` across 5/5 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + empirical** | Inspection of `select_disjoint_consensus_divergence`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase85/consensus_also_compromised_seed_sweep.json`; `W38BankTests::test_consensus_also_compromised_limitation_theorem`. |
| **W38-L-DISJOINT-CONSENSUS-REQUIRED (SDK v3.39; falsifier)** | **W38 is insufficient for any regime where a disjoint consensus reference probe cannot be sourced for the current cell.  In that regime, W38 returns `CONSENSUS_NO_REFERENCE` and falls through to W37 byte-for-byte.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase85/no_consensus_reference_seed_sweep.json`. |
| **W38-C-NATIVE-LATENT (SDK v3.39; carries forward W37-C-NATIVE-LATENT)** | **A true transformer-internal trust-state projection may separate regimes W38 cannot.  W38 narrows the audited proxy further along the cross-source axis but does not close native-latent transfer.** | **conjectural; architecture-dependent; still open** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W38_DISJOINT_CONSENSUS_REFERENCE.md §6`. |
| **W38-C-MULTI-HOST (SDK v3.39; carries forward W37-C-MULTI-HOST)** | **A 3+ reachable-host topology with at least one host genuinely disjoint from the trajectory hosts (not just a different model on the same physical host) would let the consensus reference be sourced from a true off-cluster oracle, defeating the W38-L-CONSENSUS-COLLUSION-CAP collusion attack at the capsule layer.  Mac 2 (192.168.12.248) has been ARP-incomplete for the 31st milestone in a row.  The 2026-05-02 bounded W38 3-host consensus probe (mac1 + mac_remote trajectory + mac_remote qwen2.5-coder:14b consensus on the same physical host) observed 8/8 responsive on all 3 hosts, 7/8 trajectory-pair agreements (1 num_predict=4 truncation), 7/8 cross-source consensus agreements, and 8/8 consensus-gold correlation -- strong bounded 3-host live evidence but not a true 3-physical-host disjoint topology. **PARTIALLY DISCHARGED in SDK v3.40 / W39**: ``192.168.12.101`` was identified as the reachable third physical host candidate, preflight-OK on cold contact, with ``qwen3.5:35b`` and ``qwen2.5:14b-32k`` model files; the live-inference layer remains open via W39-INFRA-1.** | **conjectural; partially discharged at the topology layer in SDK v3.40 / W39; still open at the live-inference layer; hardware-bounded** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase85/xllm_consensus_probe_2026_05_02.json`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase86/host_topology_resolution_2026_05_02.json`. |

## Multi-host disjoint quorum consensus-reference ratification + W39 manifest-v9 CID (W39-1, W39-2, W39-3, W39-4, W39-L-FULL-DISJOINT-QUORUM-COLLUSION-CAP, W39-L-INSUFFICIENT-QUORUM, W39-C-NATIVE-LATENT, W39-C-MULTI-HOST, W39-C-LIVE-TRUNCATION-RECOVERY) — SDK v3.40

| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W39-1 (SDK v3.40)** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W39 verifier: `verify_multi_host_disjoint_quorum_ratification` enumerates 14 failure modes disjoint from W22..W38 (`empty_w39_envelope`, `w39_schema_version_unknown`, `w39_schema_cid_mismatch`, `w38_parent_cid_mismatch`, `w39_projection_branch_unknown`, `w39_quorum_probe_unregistered_host`, `w39_quorum_probe_unregistered_oracle`, `w39_quorum_disjoint_topology_violation`, `w39_quorum_mutual_disjointness_violation`, `w39_quorum_thresholds_invalid`, `w39_quorum_state_cid_mismatch`, `w39_quorum_decision_cid_mismatch`, `w39_quorum_topology_cid_mismatch`, `w39_manifest_v9_cid_mismatch`, with `w39_outer_cid_mismatch` co-defined). | **W39-3 (SDK v3.40)** | **Multi-host disjoint quorum collusion bound (load-bearing): if the current cell would reroute a W37 trajectory-anchored top_set produced by colluding hosts AND the registered W38 single disjoint consensus reference is itself compromised in lock-step (the W38-L-CONSENSUS-COLLUSION-CAP regime), AND a registered `MultiHostDisjointQuorumProbe` exists with K member probes whose host pools are mechanically disjoint from W37's trajectory hosts AND mutually disjoint from one another, AND fewer than `quorum_min` of those member probes are themselves compromised in lock-step, THEN W39 abstains via `QUORUM_DIVERGENCE_ABSTAINED` without trust-precision regression. | **W39-4 (SDK v3.40)** | **Mutual-disjointness mechanical enforcement: a `MultiHostDisjointQuorumRegistry` whose any two registered quorum host pools have non-empty intersection cannot be constructed (raises `MutuallyDisjointTopologyError` in `__post_init__`); the verifier additionally rejects an envelope whose declared quorum topology has overlapping pools (`w39_quorum_mutual_disjointness_violation`).  This is a STRICT generalisation of W38-4: in addition to enforcing disjointness from the trajectory host set (inherited from W38), W39 enforces mutual disjointness across all registered quorum pools.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-tested** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::MultiHostDisjointQuorumRegistry`; `W39RegistryTests::test_non_mutually_disjoint_pools_raise`; `W39VerifierTests::test_quorum_mutual_disjointness_violation_rejected`. |
| **W39-5 (SDK v3.40; no-regression-quorum-agrees no-regression)** | **When at least `quorum_min` of the K registered disjoint quorum probes AGREE with the W37/W38 reroute AND fewer than `quorum_min` disagree, W39 ratifies via `QUORUM_RATIFIED` and adds no correctness or trust-precision regression.  Measured on R-86-NO-REGRESSION-QUORUM-AGREES across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_correctness_w39_w38 = 0.000`; `Δ_trust_precision_w39_w38 = 0.000`.** | **proved-empirical** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase86/no_regression_quorum_agrees_seed_sweep.json`; `W39BankTests::test_no_regression_quorum_agrees_no_regression`. |

Measured on R-86-INSUFFICIENT-QUORUM across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_correctness_w39_w38 = 0.000`; `Δ_trust_precision_w39_w38 = 0.000`; W39 audit envelope still records the QUORUM_INSUFFICIENT branch.** | **proved-empirical + proof sketch by inspection** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase86/insufficient_quorum_seed_sweep.json`; `W39BankTests::test_insufficient_quorum_preserves_w38`. |
| **W39-7 (SDK v3.40)** | **Quorum structured-state density: W39 transfers controller-verified multi-host disjoint quorum state at the highest density measured in the programme to date.  On R-86-MULTI-HOST-COLLUDED-CONSENSUS, W39 carries roughly 24.4k structured bits per visible W39 token (mean) at one visible token overhead/cell (W38 carried 9.07k bits/token on the analogous R-85 regime; W39 is ~2.7x denser at the audited-proxy capsule-layer).** | **empirical + mechanically bounded** | `MultiHostDisjointQuorumRatificationEnvelope.n_structured_bits`; Phase86 artifacts. |
| **W39-L-FULL-DISJOINT-QUORUM-COLLUSION-CAP (SDK v3.40; limitation theorem)** | **When all K registered disjoint quorum probes are themselves compromised in lock-step with the colluding trajectory hosts (i.e. all emit the same wrong top_set), W39 cannot recover at the capsule layer.  This is the W39 analog of `W34-L-MULTI-ANCHOR-CAP`, `W37-L-MULTI-HOST-COLLUSION-CAP`, and `W38-L-CONSENSUS-COLLUSION-CAP`.  Recovery requires native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer or a K+1-host disjoint consensus topology with at least one new genuinely uncompromised pool. | **W39-L-INSUFFICIENT-QUORUM (SDK v3.40; falsifier)** | **W39 is insufficient for any regime where a K=`min_quorum_probes` mutually-disjoint quorum cannot be sourced for the current cell.  In that regime, W39 returns `QUORUM_INSUFFICIENT` and falls through to W38 byte-for-byte.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase86/insufficient_quorum_seed_sweep.json`. |
| **W39-C-NATIVE-LATENT (SDK v3.40; carries forward W38-C-NATIVE-LATENT)** | **A true transformer-internal trust-state projection may separate regimes W39 cannot.  W39 narrows the audited proxy further along the multi-host quorum axis but does not close native-latent transfer.** | **conjectural; architecture-dependent; still open** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W39_MULTI_HOST_DISJOINT_QUORUM.md §6`. |
| **W39-C-MULTI-HOST (SDK v3.40; partial discharge of W38-C-MULTI-HOST at the topology layer)** | **A K+1-host topology with at least one new genuinely uncompromised host pool would let the W39 quorum size be raised beyond `quorum_min`, defeating the `W39-L-FULL-DISJOINT-QUORUM-COLLUSION-CAP` collusion attack at the capsule layer.  PARTIAL DISCHARGE: ``192.168.12.101`` was identified as the reachable third physical host candidate (the historical Mac-2 ``.248`` has been ARP-incomplete for the 31st milestone in a row); preflight-OK on cold contact with ``qwen3.5:35b`` (36.0B MoE Q4_K_M) and ``qwen2.5:14b-32k`` (14.8B Q4_K_M) model files visible.  Live-inference layer remains open via W39-INFRA-1: ``.101`` Ollama inference path is bounded under one-word probe budget after first model-load contact.  The 2026-05-02 bounded W39 5-host live xllm probe (mac1 + mac_remote trajectory + mac_consensus W38-style + mac_off_cluster_a localhost-fallback + mac_quorum_b .191) observed 8/8 responsive on all 5 hosts, 7/8 trajectory-pair agreements, 7/8 W38 single consensus agreements, 8/8 quorum_a gold-correlated, 8/8 quorum_b gold-correlated, AND 8/8 K=2 quorum size simultaneously responsive -- strongest bounded multi-host live evidence in the programme.** | **conjectural; partially discharged at the topology layer; still open at the live-inference layer; hardware-bounded** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase86/xllm_quorum_probe_2026_05_02.json`; `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase86/host_topology_resolution_2026_05_02.json`. |
| **W39-C-LIVE-TRUNCATION-RECOVERY (SDK v3.40; new conjecture)** | **At the live inference layer, the W39 multi-host disjoint quorum can recover from trajectory-pair-only truncation errors when the quorum members are not subject to the same `num_predict`/stop-token regime as the trajectory pair.  This is a recovery axis distinct from the collusion bound: it does not require any host to be adversarial; it only requires the quorum members to use a different (longer) generation budget than the trajectory pair.  The 2026-05-02 live xllm quorum probe observed exactly this on the ``h2o`` probe: trajectory pair disagreed (mac1=h2o vs mac_remote=h due to num_predict=4 truncation), but BOTH quorum members got h2o correct.  Sharper validation requires a dedicated live truncation-recovery bench.** | **conjectural; empirical-suggestive on a single live probe** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase86/xllm_quorum_probe_2026_05_02.json`. |

## Cross-host response-signature heterogeneity ratification + W40 manifest-v10 CID + cross-host response-text Jaccard divergence guard (W40-1, W40-2, W40-3, W40-4, W40-5, W40-6, W40-L-COORDINATED-DIVERSE-RESPONSE-CAP, W40-L-INSUFFICIENT-RESPONSE-SIGNATURE, W40-C-NATIVE-LATENT, W40-C-MULTI-HOST, W40-C-LIVE-RESPONSE-HETEROGENEITY) — SDK v3.41 RC1

| **W40-3 (SDK v3.41 RC1; load-bearing)** | **Cross-host response-heterogeneity collapse bound: if the current cell would RATIFY a W39 quorum top_set produced by colluding hosts (the W39-L-FULL-DISJOINT-QUORUM-COLLUSION-CAP regime) AND every K registered W40 member probe carries a response-text bytes payload that collapses to byte-identical (or near-identical, within mean pairwise Jaccard divergence < `response_text_diversity_min`), AND fewer than `min_response_signature_probes` member probes are missing their response signatures, THEN W40 abstains via `RESPONSE_SIGNATURE_COLLAPSE_ABSTAINED` without trust-precision regression.
