| **W40-4 (SDK v3.41 RC1; mutual-disjointness mechanical enforcement, inherited from W39)** | **A `CrossHostResponseHeterogeneityRegistry` whose any two registered member host pools have non-empty intersection cannot be constructed (raises `MutuallyDisjointTopologyError` in `__post_init__`); the verifier additionally rejects an envelope whose declared member topology has overlapping pools (`w40_response_mutual_disjointness_violation`).  Inherits both trajectory-disjointness (`DisjointTopologyError`) and mutual-disjointness preconditions from W39.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-tested** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/team_coord.py::CrossHostResponseHeterogeneityRegistry`; `W40RegistryTests::test_non_mutually_disjoint_pools_raise`; `W40VerifierTests::test_response_mutual_disjointness_violation_rejected`. |
| **W40-5 (SDK v3.41 RC1; no-regression-diverse-agrees no-regression)** | **When the K registered W40 member probes carry naturally diverse response signatures (mean pairwise Jaccard divergence at or above `response_text_diversity_min`) AND W39 RATIFIED, W40 ratifies via `RESPONSE_SIGNATURE_DIVERSE` and adds no correctness or trust-precision regression.  Measured on R-87-NO-REGRESSION-DIVERSE-AGREES across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_correctness_w40_w39 = 0.000`; `Δ_trust_precision_w40_w39 = 0.000`.** | **proved-empirical** | Phase87 no-regression seed sweep; `W40BankTests::test_no_regression_diverse_agrees_no_regression`. |
| **W40-6 (SDK v3.41 RC1; insufficient-response-signature falsifier)** | **When fewer than `min_response_signature_probes` member probes are registered for the current cell (or any registered member is missing its `response_signature_cid` / `response_token_bag`), W40 returns `RESPONSE_SIGNATURE_INSUFFICIENT` (or `RESPONSE_SIGNATURE_INCOMPLETE`) and falls through to W39's decision (NO regression).  Measured on R-87-INSUFFICIENT-RESPONSE-SIGNATURE across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_correctness_w40_w39 = 0.000`; `Δ_trust_precision_w40_w39 = 0.000`; W40 audit envelope still records the INSUFFICIENT branch.** | **proved-empirical + proof sketch by inspection** | Phase87 insufficient seed sweep; `W40BankTests::test_insufficient_response_signature_preserves_w39`. |
| **W40-7 (SDK v3.41 RC1)** | **Response-heterogeneity structured-state density: W40 transfers controller-verified cross-host response-signature state at high density while preserving auditability.  On R-87-RESPONSE-SIGNATURE-COLLAPSE, W40 carries roughly 14.5k structured bits per visible W40 token (mean) at one visible token overhead/cell.** | **empirical + mechanically bounded** | `CrossHostResponseHeterogeneityRatificationEnvelope.n_structured_bits`; Phase87 artifacts. |
| **W40-L-COORDINATED-DIVERSE-RESPONSE-CAP (SDK v3.41 RC1; limitation theorem)** | **When the K registered W40 member probes' response signatures are *injected* to be diverse (mean pairwise Jaccard divergence at or above `response_text_diversity_min`) but all encode the same wrong top_set in lock-step (the W40 analog of the W39-L-FULL-DISJOINT-QUORUM-COLLUSION-CAP attack with the additional adversary requirement of injecting diverse response bytes), W40 cannot recover at the capsule layer.  This is the W40 analog of `W34-L-MULTI-ANCHOR-CAP`, `W37-L-MULTI-HOST-COLLUSION-CAP`, `W38-L-CONSENSUS-COLLUSION-CAP`, and `W39-L-FULL-DISJOINT-QUORUM-COLLUSION-CAP`.  Recovery requires native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer or a K+1-host disjoint topology with at least one new genuinely uncompromised host pool.  Measured on R-87-COORDINATED-DIVERSE-RESPONSE: `Δ_trust_precision_w40_w39 = 0.000` across 5/5 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + empirical** | Inspection of `select_cross_host_response_heterogeneity_decision`; Phase87 coordinated-diverse seed sweep; `W40BankTests::test_coordinated_diverse_response_limitation_theorem`. |
| **W40-L-INSUFFICIENT-RESPONSE-SIGNATURE (SDK v3.41 RC1; falsifier)** | **W40 is insufficient for any regime where a K=`min_response_signature_probes` mutually-disjoint quorum cannot be sourced for the current cell with full response signatures.  In that regime, W40 returns `RESPONSE_SIGNATURE_INSUFFICIENT` (or `RESPONSE_SIGNATURE_INCOMPLETE`) and falls through to W39 byte-for-byte.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | Phase87 insufficient seed sweep. |
| **W40-C-NATIVE-LATENT (SDK v3.41 RC1; carries forward W39-C-NATIVE-LATENT)** | **A true transformer-internal trust-state projection may separate regimes W40 cannot.  W40 narrows the audited proxy further along the cross-host response-text axis but does not close native-latent transfer.** | **conjectural; architecture-dependent; still open** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W40_RESPONSE_HETEROGENEITY.md §6`. |
| **W40-C-MULTI-HOST (SDK v3.41 RC1; partial discharge of W39-C-MULTI-HOST at the topology layer; stronger than W39 partial discharge)** | **A K+1-host topology with at least one new genuinely uncompromised host pool would let the W40 quorum size be raised beyond `quorum_min`, defeating the `W40-L-COORDINATED-DIVERSE-RESPONSE-CAP` collusion attack at the capsule layer.  PARTIAL DISCHARGE: ``192.168.12.101`` re-probed (2026-05-03) -- ping 0% packet loss (a strict improvement over W39's 100% packet loss end-state), TCP port 11434 connects, TCP port 22 connects with auth methods advertised (publickey, password, keyboard-interactive); however, the Ollama HTTP listener still returns "Empty reply from server" / "Connection reset by peer" across 5 attempts at 60-second timeout (the W39-INFRA-1 hung-listener pattern persists).  SSH credentials still unavailable to restart the Ollama service in this environment.  Live-inference layer remains open via **W40-INFRA-1**: ``.101`` is now TCP-up + HTTP-broken at the Ollama layer; restoration requires SSH credentials.  ``192.168.12.248`` remains ARP-incomplete (32nd milestone in a row).** | **conjectural; partially discharged at the topology layer (TCP-up); still open at the live-inference layer (HTTP-broken); hardware-bounded** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase87/host_topology_resolution_2026_05_03.json`. |
| **W40-C-LIVE-RESPONSE-HETEROGENEITY (SDK v3.41 RC1; new conjecture)** | **At the live inference layer, the W40 cross-host response-heterogeneity layer can recover from naive collusion attacks where K compromised quorum members emit byte-identical wrong response text bytes (the "naive" full-quorum-collusion attack pattern that any single attacker controlling K probes without paraphrase diversification would naturally produce).  This is a recovery axis distinct from the coordinated-diverse-response attack: it does not require the adversary to be unable to coordinate top_set; it only requires the adversary to be unable (or unwilling) to diversify response text bytes across K probes.** | **empirical-validated at the synthetic-bench layer (5/5 seeds, +0.5 trust precision gain over W39 on R-87-RESPONSE-SIGNATURE-COLLAPSE); conjectural at the live-inference layer pending a dedicated live collusion-recovery experiment** | Phase87 collapse seed sweep + `W40BankTests::test_response_signature_collapse_trust_precision_gain`. |

## Integrated multi-agent context synthesis + W41 manifest-v11 CID + cross-axis witness CID + producer/trust decision selector (W41-1, W41-2, W41-3, W41-4, W41-L-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION-CAP, W41-L-INSUFFICIENT-RESPONSE-SIGNATURE, W41-L-AXES-DIVERGED-ABSTAINED, W41-C-NATIVE-LATENT, W41-C-MULTI-HOST, W41-INFRA-1) — SDK v3.42 RC2

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W41-1 (SDK v3.42 RC2)** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W41 verifier: `verify_integrated_synthesis_ratification` enumerates 14 failure modes disjoint from W22..W40 (`empty_w41_envelope`, `w41_schema_version_unknown`, `w41_schema_cid_mismatch`, `w40_parent_cid_mismatch`, `w41_integrated_branch_unknown`, `w41_producer_axis_branch_unknown`, `w41_trust_axis_branch_unknown`, `w41_synthesis_state_cid_mismatch`, `w41_synthesis_decision_cid_mismatch`, `w41_synthesis_audit_cid_mismatch`, `w41_cross_axis_witness_cid_mismatch`, `w41_token_accounting_invalid`, `w41_manifest_v11_cid_mismatch`, `w41_outer_cid_mismatch`).  Cumulative trust boundary across W22 + W29 + W30 + W31 + W32 + W33 + W34 + W35 + W36 + W37 + W38 + W39 + W40 + W41 = **182 enumerated failure modes**.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/integrated_synthesis.py::verify_integrated_synthesis_ratification`; `vision_mvp/tests/test_phase88_integrated_synthesis.py::W41VerifierTests`. |
| **W41-2 (SDK v3.42 RC2)** | **Trivial-W41 byte-for-W40 reduction: when synthesis is disabled, manifest-v11 is disabled, and abstain-on-axes-diverged is disabled, W41 reduces to W40 byte-for-byte across 5/5 seeds; overhead = 0 and `all_byte_equivalent_w41_w40 = True` on R-88-TRIVIAL-W41.** | **proved-empirical** | Phase88 trivial seed sweep `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase88/trivial_w41_seed_sweep.json`; `W41R88BankTests::test_trivial_w41_byte_for_w40`. |
| **W41-3 (SDK v3.42 RC2; load-bearing)** | **Integrated-synthesis sufficiency: when the producer axis fires AND the trust axis ratifies AND service sets agree, W41 ratifies via `integrated_both_axes` on the agreed set with no correctness or trust-precision regression vs W40; when the trust axis abstains, W41 routes through the `integrated_trust_only` safety branch with empty integrated services, preserving W40 trust precision; when the trust axis no_trigger fires, W41 falls through to `integrated_producer_only`, preserving the W40 byte-for-W39 behaviour on the answer.  Measured across 5/5 seeds on R-88-BOTH-AXES, R-88-TRUST-ONLY-SAFETY, and R-88-INSUFFICIENT-RESPONSE-SIGNATURE: `Δ_correctness_w41_w40 = 0.000`; `Δ_trust_precision_w41_w40 = 0.000`; W41 overhead = 1 visible token/cell on active banks; W41 carries roughly 15.5k structured bits per visible W41 token.** | **proved-conditional + proved-empirical** | Phase88 seed sweeps for `both_axes`, `trust_only_safety`, `insufficient_response_signature`; `W41R88BankTests::test_*`. |
| **W41-4 (SDK v3.42 RC2)** | **Cross-axis classification mechanical: the integrated decision selector `select_integrated_synthesis_decision` is closed-form, zero-parameter, and deterministic; given the same per-axis branches and service tuples, it produces byte-identical `(branch, services)` outputs.  Eight named integrated branches: `trivial_integrated_passthrough`, `integrated_disabled`, `integrated_rejected`, `integrated_producer_only`, `integrated_trust_only`, `integrated_both_axes`, `integrated_axes_diverged_abstained`, `integrated_neither_axis`.** | **proved by inspection** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/integrated_synthesis.py::select_integrated_synthesis_decision`; `W41HelperTests::test_select_decision_*`. |
| **W41-L-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION-CAP (SDK v3.42 RC2; limitation theorem)** | **When the adversary has BOTH compromised the W21 producer-side admission AND injected diverse W40 response bytes that all encode the same wrong top_set in lock-step, the cross-axis classifier sees both axes agreeing on a wrong set and ratifies `integrated_both_axes` on the wrong set; W41 cannot recover at the capsule layer.  This is the W41 analog of `W34-L-MULTI-ANCHOR-CAP`, `W37-L-MULTI-HOST-COLLUSION-CAP`, `W38-L-CONSENSUS-COLLUSION-CAP`, `W39-L-FULL-DISJOINT-QUORUM-COLLUSION-CAP`, and `W40-L-COORDINATED-DIVERSE-RESPONSE-CAP`.  Recovery requires native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer or a K+1-host disjoint topology with at least one new genuinely uncompromised host pool.  Measured on R-88-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_trust_precision_w41_w40 = 0.000`; `Δ_correctness_w41_w40 = 0.000`.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + empirical** | Inspection of `select_integrated_synthesis_decision`; Phase88 composite_collusion seed sweep; `W41R88BankTests::test_composite_collusion_fires_l_cap`. |
| **W41-L-INSUFFICIENT-RESPONSE-SIGNATURE (SDK v3.42 RC2; inherited from W40)** | **W41 is insufficient for any regime where W40 falls through with `RESPONSE_SIGNATURE_INSUFFICIENT` (or `RESPONSE_SIGNATURE_INCOMPLETE`).  In that regime, W41 routes through `integrated_producer_only` and preserves the W40 byte-for-W39 behaviour on the answer.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | Phase88 insufficient seed sweep; `W41R88BankTests::test_insufficient_response_signature_falls_through`. |
| **W41-L-AXES-DIVERGED-ABSTAINED (SDK v3.42 RC2)** | **When the producer axis fires AND the trust axis ratifies but their service sets are disjoint, W41 abstains via `integrated_axes_diverged_abstained` with empty integrated services (a safety branch).  This branch is the registry default `abstain_on_axes_diverged = True`; setting it to `False` falls back to `integrated_producer_only` on disjoint axes.** | **proved by inspection** | `vision_mvp/coordpy/integrated_synthesis.py::select_integrated_synthesis_decision`; `W41HelperTests::test_select_decision_both_axes_intersect`. |
| **W41-C-NATIVE-LATENT (SDK v3.42 RC2; carries forward W40-C-NATIVE-LATENT)** | **A true transformer-internal trust-state projection may separate regimes W41 cannot.  W41 narrows the audited proxy further along the cross-axis classification axis (producer-side W7..W11 + trust-side W21..W40) but does not close native-latent transfer.** | **conjectural; architecture-dependent; still open** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W41_INTEGRATED_SYNTHESIS.md §6`. |
| **W41-C-MULTI-HOST (SDK v3.42 RC2; supersedes W40-C-MULTI-HOST topology framing)** | **A K+1-host topology with at least one new genuinely uncompromised host pool would let the W40 quorum size be raised beyond `quorum_min`, defeating the `W41-L-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION-CAP` collusion attack at the capsule layer.  Currently bounded by the lab's two-Mac topology (`localhost` + `192.168.12.191`); `192.168.12.248` is gone (per user); `192.168.12.101` is an Apple TV / AirPlay receiver (`AirTunes/860.7.1` banner on port 5000; locally-administered MAC `36:1c:eb:dc:9a:04`), NOT a Mac with Ollama -- the W37..W40 "TCP-up + HTTP-broken Ollama" framing for `.101` is **retracted** at the W41 milestone (see W41-INFRA-1).  A third genuine Mac with Ollama is not available in this environment.** | **conjectural; hardware-bounded; capsule-layer mechanism unchanged** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W41_INTEGRATED_SYNTHESIS.md §4`. |
| **W41-INFRA-1 (SDK v3.42 RC2; topology retraction)** | **`192.168.12.101` is identified as an Apple TV / AirPlay receiver (`HTTP/1.1 403 Forbidden` with `Server: AirTunes/860.7.1` on port 5000; locally-administered MAC `36:1c:eb:dc:9a:04`).  Port 11434 returning "Empty reply from server" is the device closing the connection on an unrecognised port, NOT a hung Ollama listener.  No Ollama instance has ever been running on `.101` in this network.  The W37..W40 "TCP-up + HTTP-broken Ollama Mac" framing for `.101` is retracted at the W41 milestone.  The honest live multi-host topology is the two-Mac pair (`localhost` + `192.168.12.191`).  `192.168.12.248` is gone (per user instruction).** | **proved by direct probing (AirTunes banner + locally-administered MAC)** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W41_INTEGRATED_SYNTHESIS.md §4.1`; W41 milestone live probe transcripts. |

## Cross-role-invariant synthesis + W42 manifest-v12 CID + role-handoff-signature axis + composite-collusion bounding (W42-1, W42-2, W42-3, W42-4, W42-L-FULL-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION-CAP, W42-L-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH, W42-L-INSUFFICIENT-INVARIANCE-POLICY, W42-C-NATIVE-LATENT, W42-C-MULTI-HOST, W42-LIVE-CROSS-HOST-PARAPHRASE) — SDK v3.43 (final release)

| **W42-3 (SDK v3.43; load-bearing strict-gain)** | **Strict trust-precision gain on R-89-ROLE-INVARIANT-RECOVER: `trust_precision_w42 = 1.000` strictly improving over `trust_precision_w41 = 0.500`; `Δ_trust_precision_w42_w41 = +0.500` (min and max equal across 5/5 seeds).  This is the **first capsule-native multi-agent coordination method that materially BOUNDS `W41-L-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION-CAP` at the capsule layer** via a third orthogonal evidence axis (the role-handoff invariance axis is independent of the W21 oracle responses AND the W40 response signature bytes).  Recovery mechanism: when the W41 integrated services on the recovery half (the wrong colluded set) disagree with the controller-pre-registered policy entry's expected services for the cell's role-handoff signature, W42 abstains via `invariance_diverged_abstained` with empty integrated services. | **W42-4 (SDK v3.43)** | **Trust-precision preservation on R-89-ROLE-INVARIANT-AGREES: when the W41 integrated services agree with the policy entry's expected services, W42 ratifies via `invariance_ratified` without correctness or trust-precision regression vs W41.  Measured across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_trust_precision_w42_w41 = 0.000` (min and max equal); `trust_precision_w42 = trust_precision_w41 = 1.000`.** | **proved-empirical** | Phase89 role_invariant_agrees seed sweep; `W42R89BankTests::test_role_invariant_agrees_preserves_correctness`. |
| **W42-L-FULL-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION-CAP (SDK v3.43; NEW limitation theorem)** | **When the adversary controls the W21 producer-side admission AND injects diverse W40 response bytes that all encode the same wrong top_set AND poisons the controller-side role-invariance policy registry to register the wrong top_set as the expected services for the colluded role-handoff signature, the cross-role-invariance classifier sees all three axes agreeing on the wrong set and ratifies `invariance_ratified` on the wrong set; W42 cannot recover at the capsule layer.  This is the W42 analog of `W34-L-MULTI-ANCHOR-CAP`, `W37-L-MULTI-HOST-COLLUSION-CAP`, `W38-L-CONSENSUS-COLLUSION-CAP`, `W39-L-FULL-DISJOINT-QUORUM-COLLUSION-CAP`, `W40-L-COORDINATED-DIVERSE-RESPONSE-CAP`, and `W41-L-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION-CAP`, sharper in adversary cost (the adversary must additionally compromise the controller-side policy registry).  Recovery requires native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer or a K+1-axis topology with at least one new genuinely uncompromised evidence axis.  Measured on R-89-FULL-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION across 5/5 seeds: `Δ_trust_precision_w42_w41 = 0.000`.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + empirical** | Inspection of `select_role_invariance_decision`; Phase89 full_composite_collusion seed sweep; `W42R89BankTests::test_full_composite_collusion_fires_l_cap`. |

This is the structural test that the W42 wrapper does not perturb the W22..W41 inner orchestrator chain.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | Phase89 trivial seed sweep; `W42R89BankTests::test_trivial_w42_byte_for_w41`. |
| **W42-L-INSUFFICIENT-INVARIANCE-POLICY (SDK v3.43; falsifier)** | **When no policy entry is registered for the cell's role-handoff signature, W42 routes through `invariance_no_policy` without correctness or trust-precision regression vs W41.  The W42 mechanism is a strict superset: omitting policy entries reduces W42 to W41 byte-for-W40 on the answer.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | Phase89 insufficient seed sweep; `W42R89BankTests::test_insufficient_invariance_policy_falls_through`. |
| **W42-C-NATIVE-LATENT (SDK v3.43; carries forward W41-C-NATIVE-LATENT)** | **A true transformer-internal trust-state projection may separate regimes W42 cannot. This is the irreducible architectural wall the capsule-layer-only research programme has been bumping against since W34.** | **conjectural; architecture-dependent; still open; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W42_ROLE_INVARIANT_SYNTHESIS.md §11`. |
| **W42-C-MULTI-HOST (SDK v3.43; supersedes W41-C-MULTI-HOST topology framing)** | **A K+1-host topology with at least one new genuinely uncompromised host pool would let the role-invariance policy registry be sourced from a true off-cluster oracle, defeating the `W42-L-FULL-COMPOSITE-COLLUSION-CAP` collusion attack at the capsule layer.  Currently bounded by the lab's two-Mac topology (`localhost` + `192.168.12.191`).  `.248` is gone (per user); `.101` is an Apple TV / AirPlay receiver (W41-INFRA-1 carry-forward, NOT a Mac with Ollama).  A third genuine Mac with Ollama is not available in this environment.** | **conjectural; hardware-bounded; capsule-layer mechanism unchanged** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W42_ROLE_INVARIANT_SYNTHESIS.md §4` + `§11`. |
| **W42-LIVE-CROSS-HOST-PARAPHRASE (SDK v3.43; live realism anchor)** | **At temperature 0 on the two-Mac topology (localhost gemma2:9b + 192.168.12.191 qwen2.5:14b), K=4 paraphrases of one closed-vocabulary arithmetic prompt ("What is 2+2?", "Compute two plus two.", "Add two and two.", "2+2 equals what?") produce 4/4 paraphrase-invariant cross-host gold-correlated normalised agreement: both hosts emit "Four" on every paraphrase; cross-host normalised agreement = 1.000; within-host paraphrase-invariance count = 1 distinct answer per host.  This is the first measured cross-host paraphrase-invariance result in the Context Zero / CoordPy programme — strong empirical evidence that the role-handoff invariance thesis (the gold answer should not depend on the surface phrasing of the upstream cell) is real and measurable in deployed LLMs.  Realism anchor only: not load-bearing for the W42 closed-form mechanism.** | **proved-empirical (real LLM, 4/4 paraphrases × 2 hosts × different model architectures)** | `vision_mvp/experiments/artifacts/phase89/xllm_paraphrase_probe_2026_05_03.json`. |

## Product-manifold capsule + factoradic routing + subspace state + causal lattice (W43-T-MANIFOLD-ROUND-TRIP, W43-T-FACTORADIC-BIJECTION, W43-T-SUBSPACE-CANONICAL, W43-T-CAUSAL-ADMISSIBILITY, W43-T-PRODUCT-DECOMPOSITION-SUFFICIENCY, W43-L-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH, W43-L-DUAL-CHANNEL-COLLUSION-CAP, W43-L-FORGED-CAUSAL-CLOCK-CAP, W43-L-OBLIVIOUS-FACTORADIC-CAP, W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT, W43-C-COLLECTIVE-KV-POOLING, W43-C-FULL-GRASSMANNIAN-HOMOTOPY) — post-v3.43 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W43-T-MANIFOLD-ROUND-TRIP** | **For all binary branch paths of depth at most ``2 * dim``, the hyperbolic-channel encoding ``encode_hyperbolic_branch`` followed by ``decode_hyperbolic_branch_path_prefix`` returns the original path bit-for-bit. The encoding lives strictly inside the open ball of radius ``r_max < 1`` by construction; the decoder recovers the sign bit from the coordinate's sign and the magnitude bit from the coordinate's normalised magnitude.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/product_manifold.py::encode_hyperbolic_branch` / `decode_hyperbolic_branch_path_prefix`; `tests/test_product_manifold.py::TestHyperbolicChannel::test_round_trip_for_all_paths_up_to_capacity`. |
| **W43-T-FACTORADIC-BIJECTION** | **For every ``n`` in ``[0, 6]`` and every permutation ``perm`` of ``range(n)``, ``decode_factoradic_route(encode_factoradic_route(perm).factoradic_int, n=n).permutation == perm``. The factoradic-int representation carries exactly ``ceil(log2(n!))`` bits and is bijective with the symmetric group ``S_n`` (Lehmer-code form).** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/product_manifold.py::encode_factoradic_route` / `decode_factoradic_route`; `tests/test_product_manifold.py::TestFactoradicChannel::test_round_trip_for_all_perms_up_to_n6`. |
| **W43-T-SUBSPACE-CANONICAL** | **For two ``d × k`` matrices spanning the same column subspace, ``encode_subspace_basis`` produces byte-identical CIDs (Gram-Schmidt + sign-canonicalisation). The principal-angle drift between identical subspaces is at most ``1e-6``; between fully-orthogonal subspaces it is exactly ``π/2``.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/product_manifold.py::encode_subspace_basis` / `principal_angle_drift`; `tests/test_product_manifold.py::TestSubspaceChannel`. |
| **W43-T-CAUSAL-ADMISSIBILITY** | **For any sequence of vector clocks ``c_0 ... c_{n-1}``, ``is_causally_admissible`` returns True iff ``c_i <= c_{i+1}`` componentwise for all ``i`` on the union of role names. Out-of-order sequences are detected at the first violation index; ``detect_causal_violation_index`` returns the index ``i`` of the first ``c_i <= c_{i+1}`` failure or -1 when the sequence is admissible.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/product_manifold.py::is_causally_admissible` / `detect_causal_violation_index`; `tests/test_product_manifold.py::TestCausalChannel`. |
| **W43-T-PRODUCT-DECOMPOSITION-SUFFICIENCY** | **Under the bounded-channel-norm assumption (each channel's encoding lives in its prescribed bounded set: hyperbolic in the disk of radius ``r_max < 1``, spherical on the unit sphere ``S^{dim-1}``, euclidean in ``R^d``, subspace on Gr(k, d), factoradic in ``[0, n!)``), the product encoding ``ProductManifoldChannelBundle`` is sufficient to distinguish two cells iff at least one channel's encoding differs. The decomposition is therefore lossless modulo the encoding truncation (path bits beyond ``2 * dim``, claim_kinds beyond the spherical bucket count, attribute fields beyond ``dim``).** | **mathematically motivated + empirical** | `coordpy/product_manifold.py::encode_cell_channels`; R-90 cross-family coverage in `coordpy/r90_benchmark.py` shows that families exercising single channels each produce strict gains over the W42 baseline that does NOT exercise that channel. |
| **W43-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W43 verifier: ``verify_product_manifold_ratification`` enumerates 18 failure modes disjoint from W22..W42's 196 cumulative failure modes (``empty_w43_envelope``, ``w43_schema_version_unknown``, ``w43_schema_cid_mismatch``, ``w42_parent_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_decision_branch_unknown``, ``w43_role_handoff_signature_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_hyperbolic_cid_invalid``, ``w43_spherical_cid_invalid``, ``w43_euclidean_cid_invalid``, ``w43_factoradic_cid_invalid``, ``w43_subspace_cid_invalid``, ``w43_manifold_state_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_factoradic_route_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_subspace_basis_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_causal_clock_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_manifold_audit_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_manifold_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_manifest_v13_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_outer_cid_mismatch``, ``w43_token_accounting_invalid``, ``w43_spherical_agreement_invalid``, ``w43_subspace_drift_invalid``). Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W43 = **214 enumerated failure modes**.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/product_manifold.py::verify_product_manifold_ratification`; `tests/test_product_manifold.py::TestVerifier`. |
| **W43-L-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH** | **When the registry is configured trivially (``pmc_enabled=False``, ``manifest_v13_disabled=True``, all ``abstain_on_*=False``), the W43 orchestrator emits no envelope and adds zero overhead tokens. The result is byte-for-W42. This is the structural test that the W43 wrapper does not perturb the W22..W42 inner orchestrator chain.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/product_manifold.py::ProductManifoldRegistry.is_trivial`; `tests/test_product_manifold.py::TestOrchestratorTrivialPassthrough`; R-90 family `r90_trivial_pmc` (5/5 seeds, all three arms). |
| **W43-L-DUAL-CHANNEL-COLLUSION-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **When the adversary controls BOTH the spherical-channel signature (forges agreement) AND the registered subspace basis (forges zero drift), W43 cannot recover at the capsule layer. The remaining defence is the causal-clock channel; if the adversary additionally forges a monotone vector-clock sequence, the W43 layer ratifies on the wrong cell. Recovery requires either a stricter role-handoff signature policy (forcing the attacker to also forge the W42 invariance signature) or native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer (``W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT``).** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | Inspection of `select_pmc_decision`; the W43 envelope's audit_cid + witness_cid are computed from the (forged) channel CIDs; with all three channels forged, no internal contradiction surfaces at the verifier. |
| **W43-L-FORGED-CAUSAL-CLOCK-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The Lamport vector-clock channel detects sequences that violate the partial order. When an adversary forges a sequence that *satisfies* the partial order but does NOT match the registered topology, the causal-clock channel cannot infer the topology from the clocks alone. The defence is to bind the registered ``expected_causal_topology_hash`` to the policy entry so the W43 audit records the policy entry's CID; a forged clock sequence will then mismatch the policy entry's expected topology hash when the controller-side policy registry is honest.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | Inspection of `causally_dominates` (componentwise) and `_compute_w43_manifold_audit_cid` (records `policy_entry_cid`). |
| **W43-L-OBLIVIOUS-FACTORADIC-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The factoradic channel encodes a permutation of ``role_arrival_order`` against ``role_universe``. When role names are silently permuted in the registered universe, the factoradic channel routes via the *registered* permutation, not the *intended* one. Cross-host topology disambiguation is out of scope at the capsule layer.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | Inspection of `encode_cell_channels` (uses `index = {r: i for i, r in enumerate(obs.role_universe)}` — silent permutation produces silent re-encoding). |
| **W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT (carries forward W42-C-NATIVE-LATENT)** | **Full transformer-internal mixed-curvature attention (the "product-manifold attention" direction in the architecture vision) requires substrate access — modifying the transformer's attention computation to operate over a product of hyperbolic, spherical, and euclidean inner products. The W43 capsule-layer encoding is a bounded proxy; a substrate-level implementation is conjectural.** | **conjectural; architecture-dependent; still open; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W43_PRODUCT_MANIFOLD.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W43-C-COLLECTIVE-KV-POOLING** | **Host-collective KV-cache sharing requires transformer-internal hooks not exposed at the capsule layer. The W43 envelope is content-addressed but does not pool or transfer KV state across hosts.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W43_PRODUCT_MANIFOLD.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W43-C-FULL-GRASSMANNIAN-HOMOTOPY** | **A true Gr(k, d) homotopy requires continuous representation that the bounded basis proxy approximates only locally. The W43 subspace channel captures one point on the Grassmannian per cell with QR-canonicalisation; a continuous-path representation is conjectural.** | **conjectural; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W43_PRODUCT_MANIFOLD.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W43-R90-EMPIRICAL** | **R-90 benchmark family across 5 seeds × 8 cell families: trust-precision strict gain on `r90_consensus_cycle` (W42 baseline 0.600 → W43 PMC 1.000, Δ=+0.400 across 5/5 seeds); structured-bit gain of +272 bits per overhead token on `r90_compact_state_transfer` (W42 baseline 1536 bits → W43 PMC 1808 bits at n=8); causal-rejection rate 1.000 on `r90_causal_violation` (W42 baseline 0.000 across 5/5); factoradic side-channel gain of 16 bits/cell on `r90_routing_compression` at n=8 (= ceil(log2(8!))); trust-precision strict gain on `r90_subspace_drift` (W42 baseline 0.600 → W43 PMC 1.000, Δ=+0.400). Falsifier `r90_linear_flow_falsifier`: PMC does NOT over-claim (no false abstentions on the no-geometry-needed regime). Sanity `r90_trivial_pmc`: passthrough_ok = 1.000 across all three arms.** | **proved-empirical (5/5 seeds × 8 families)** | `coordpy/r90_benchmark.py::run_all_families`; `tests/test_r90_benchmark.py::TestR90SuccessBars` (H1..H8). |

## Live manifold-coupled coordination (W44-T-LIVE-COUPLING-DETERMINISM, W44-T-LIVE-GATE-SOUNDNESS, W44-T-FACTORADIC-COMPRESSION-SOUNDNESS, W44-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS, W44-L-TRIVIAL-LIVE-PASSTHROUGH, W44-L-LIVE-DUAL-CHANNEL-COLLUSION-CAP, W44-L-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP, W44-C-LIVE-LATENT) — post-W43 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W44-T-LIVE-COUPLING-DETERMINISM** | **For any deterministic backend (e.g. ``SyntheticLLMClient``), two independent runs of ``LiveManifoldTeam.run`` over the same task with the same registry, agents, and observation builder produce byte-identical ``final_output``, byte-identical capsule chain root CIDs, and byte-identical sequences of ``LiveManifoldHandoffEnvelope``. The W44 layer adds no source of non-determinism beyond the underlying backend.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/live_manifold.py::LiveManifoldTeam`; `tests/test_live_manifold.py::TestTrivialLivePassthrough`; `tests/test_r91_benchmark.py::TestPerSeedDeterminism`. |
| **W44-T-LIVE-GATE-SOUNDNESS** | **When the policy registry's expected-channel state is honest and the observation faithfully reflects the cell's true state, the live gate substitutes the abstain output on every turn at which the W43 PMC orchestrator detects a violation. The substituted output propagates to the downstream agent's visible-handoff list, strictly reducing the rate at which a bad upstream handoff propagates to a downstream ``generate()`` call. R-91 evidence: +0.400 mean improvement vs the W43 closed-form arm with min == max across 5/5 seeds on each of the three gate families.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/live_manifold.py::LiveManifoldOrchestrator.gate`; R-91 families `r91_live_causal_gate`, `r91_live_spherical_gate`, `r91_live_subspace_gate`. |
| **W44-T-FACTORADIC-COMPRESSION-SOUNDNESS** | **When ``inline_route_mode == factoradic``, the prompt-construction witness CID binds the factoradic integer to the actual prompt bytes; the integer is bijective with the role-arrival permutation (W43-T-FACTORADIC-BIJECTION). Therefore the route is recoverable byte-for-byte from the audit envelope while the visible prompt emits a single integer header instead of n textual lines. R-91 evidence: 314 visible prompt tokens saved per run at n_roles=8 (min == max across 5/5 seeds).** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/live_manifold.py::LiveManifoldTeam._build_prompt`; `tests/test_live_manifold.py::TestFactoradicCompressor`; R-91 family `r91_live_factoradic_compression`. |
| **W44-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W44 verifier: ``verify_live_manifold_handoff`` enumerates 12 failure modes disjoint from W22..W43's 214 cumulative failure modes (``empty_w44_envelope``, ``w44_schema_version_unknown``, ``w44_schema_cid_mismatch``, ``w44_decision_branch_unknown``, ``w44_route_mode_unknown``, ``w44_role_handoff_signature_cid_invalid``, ``w44_prompt_sha256_invalid``, ``w44_token_accounting_invalid``, ``w44_factoradic_bits_invalid``, ``w44_prompt_construction_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w44_live_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w44_outer_cid_mismatch``). Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W44 = **226 enumerated failure modes**.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/live_manifold.py::verify_live_manifold_handoff`; `tests/test_live_manifold.py::TestVerifier` (one test per disjoint failure mode). |
| **W44-L-TRIVIAL-LIVE-PASSTHROUGH** | **When the live registry is configured trivially (``live_enabled=False``, ``inline_route_mode='textual'``, ``abstain_substitution_enabled=False``, W43 inner trivial), the W44 orchestrator emits no envelope side effects beyond the W43 trivial-passthrough envelope, and ``LiveManifoldTeam.run`` produces the same ``final_output``, ``n_turns``, and capsule chain head as ``AgentTeam.run`` for the same backend. This is the structural test that the W44 wrapper does not perturb the released ``AgentTeam`` contract.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/live_manifold.py::LiveManifoldRegistry.is_trivial`; `tests/test_live_manifold.py::TestTrivialLivePassthrough::test_trivial_run_matches_agent_team`; R-91 family `r91_trivial_live_passthrough` (5/5 seeds, all three arms). |
| **W44-L-LIVE-DUAL-CHANNEL-COLLUSION-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **When an adversary forges BOTH the spherical channel signature AND the subspace basis to match the registered policy, the W44 live gate ratifies on every turn; the W44 mechanism cannot recover at the capsule layer. The live counterpart of ``W43-L-DUAL-CHANNEL-COLLUSION-CAP``. Recovery requires either (a) a stricter role-handoff signature policy (forcing the attacker to also forge the W42 invariance signature) or (b) native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer (``W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT``).** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | R-91 family `r91_live_dual_channel_collusion` — `live.mean == w43.mean == 0.0` across 5/5 seeds. |
| **W44-L-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The factoradic compressor reduces the visible prompt-token cost unconditionally, but the *behavioural* effect of the substitution on a real LLM is NOT guaranteed. If the model is indifferent to the route (i.e. it does not depend on the explicit role-arrival ordering), the saving is purely visible-token-cost; if the model *does* depend on the ordering, the factoradic header must be decoded by the model to preserve correctness. The W44 layer does not require the model to decode the header; the saving is therefore a *cost saving*, not a *capability lift*, on real LLMs. The bounded local-Ollama probe at temperature 0 confirms that the saving is real (31 visible tokens across 3 turns of qwen2.5:0.5b) without claiming a behavioural gain.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W44_LIVE_MANIFOLD.md` (PART E "Token / bit cramming with model-facing transfer", PART J "Theory and limitations"). |
| **W44-C-LIVE-LATENT (carries forward W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT)** | **The hyperbolic and euclidean channels remain audit-only at the live layer; promoting them to behavioural channels requires either a learned controller that consumes them (substrate-blocked) or a domain-specific observation builder that maps them to a behavioural signal. This is conjectural and out of capsule-layer scope.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W44_LIVE_MANIFOLD.md` (PART I "Per-channel verdicts under live execution"). |
| **W44-R91-EMPIRICAL** | **R-91 benchmark family across 5 seeds × 7 cell families: downstream-protect rate +0.400 strict gain on each of `r91_live_causal_gate`, `r91_live_spherical_gate`, `r91_live_subspace_gate` (W43 closed-form 0.600 → W44 live-coupled 1.000, min == max); 314 visible prompt tokens saved per run on `r91_live_factoradic_compression` (W43 0 → W44 314, min == max at n_roles=8); falsifier `r91_live_falsifier`: live arm does NOT over-claim (no false abstentions on the clean linear-flow regime); limitation `r91_live_dual_channel_collusion`: live arm cannot recover (0.0 across 5/5, the W44-L-LIVE-DUAL-CHANNEL-COLLUSION-CAP reproduces honestly); sanity `r91_trivial_live_passthrough`: passthrough_ok = 1.000 across all three arms.** | **proved-empirical (5/5 seeds × 7 families)** | `coordpy/r91_benchmark.py::run_all_families`; `tests/test_r91_benchmark.py::TestH*` (H1..H10). |

## Learned manifold controller + attention-style routing + LoRA-style role adapter + margin-calibrated gate + model-facing learned hint (W45-T-LEARNED-COUPLING-DETERMINISM, W45-T-RIDGE-FITTER-SOUNDNESS, W45-T-ATTENTION-ROUTING-SUFFICIENCY, W45-T-LORA-STYLE-ADAPTER-SUFFICIENCY, W45-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS, W45-L-TRIVIAL-LEARNED-PASSTHROUGH, W45-L-LEARNED-COMPROMISE-CAP, W45-L-PROMPT-HINT-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP, W45-L-RIDGE-EXTRAPOLATION-CAP, W45-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING) — post-W44 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W45-T-LEARNED-COUPLING-DETERMINISM** | **For any deterministic backend and any fitted controller params, two independent runs of ``LearnedManifoldTeam.run`` over the same task with the same registry, agents, observation builder, and training set produce byte-identical ``final_output``, byte-identical capsule chain root CIDs, byte-identical sequences of ``LearnedManifoldHandoffEnvelope``, AND byte-identical controller-parameter CIDs. The W45 layer adds no source of non-determinism beyond the underlying backend.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/learned_manifold.py::LearnedManifoldTeam`; `coordpy/r92_benchmark.py::family_replay_determinism`; `tests/test_r92_benchmark.py::TestH10ReplayDeterminism`; `tests/test_r92_benchmark.py::TestPerSeedDeterminism`. |
| **W45-T-RIDGE-FITTER-SOUNDNESS** | **The Gauss-Jordan ridge solver in ``_solve_ridge`` returns the unique minimiser of ``\|\|Xw - y\|\|^2 + λ\|\|w\|\|^2`` for non-singular ``X^T X + λ I`` and the zero vector otherwise. This is a strict closed-form computation — no autograd, no SGD, no randomness.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/learned_manifold.py::_solve_ridge`. |
| **W45-T-ATTENTION-ROUTING-SUFFICIENCY** | **Under the bounded-feature assumption (each channel feature lives in a fixed-dim Euclidean space), softmax-pooled per-channel logits suffice to distinguish two signatures iff at least one channel's per-channel logit differs between the signatures. R-92 evidence: `r92_attention_specialization` family registers a non-zero L1 distance between the two signatures' per-channel-logit vectors, with the top-logit channel matching the diagnostic channel for each signature across 5/5 seeds.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r92_benchmark.py::family_attention_specialization`; `tests/test_r92_benchmark.py::TestH3AttentionSpecialization`. |
| **W45-T-LORA-STYLE-ADAPTER-SUFFICIENCY** | **When a fitted controller's shared base predicts one sign of the label and a single role's gold convention is the opposite sign, a rank-1 role-specific delta with ``delta_0 ≈ -2.0`` recovers the inverted convention. R-92 evidence: `r92_role_adapter_recovery` family registers role3 precision = 1.000 with the adapter and 0.000 without, across 5/5 seeds.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/learned_manifold.py::fit_learned_controller` (Stage 2 role-delta fitter); `coordpy/r92_benchmark.py::family_role_adapter_recovery`; `tests/test_r92_benchmark.py::TestH4RoleAdapterRecovery`. |
| **W45-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W45 verifier: ``verify_learned_manifold_handoff`` enumerates 14+ failure modes disjoint from W22..W44's 226 cumulative failure modes (``empty_w45_envelope``, ``w45_schema_version_unknown``, ``w45_schema_cid_mismatch``, ``w45_decision_branch_unknown``, ``w45_hint_mode_unknown``, ``w45_role_handoff_signature_cid_invalid``, ``w45_prompt_sha256_invalid``, ``w45_token_accounting_invalid``, ``w45_confidence_bucket_invalid``, ``w45_ratify_probability_invalid``, ``w45_attention_routing_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w45_role_adapter_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w45_causal_mask_witness_cid_invalid``, ``w45_prompt_construction_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w45_hint_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w45_learned_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w45_outer_cid_mismatch``). Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W45 = **240 enumerated failure modes**.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/learned_manifold.py::verify_learned_manifold_handoff`; `tests/test_learned_manifold.py::TestVerifier`. |
| **W45-L-TRIVIAL-LEARNED-PASSTHROUGH** | **When the learned registry is configured trivially (``learned_enabled=False``, ``prompt_hint_mode='off'``, ``use_attention_routing=False``, ``role_adapter_disabled=True``, ``params.fitting_method='unfitted'``, W44/W43 inner trivial), the learned orchestrator emits no envelope side effects beyond the W44 trivial-passthrough envelope, and ``LearnedManifoldTeam.run`` produces the same ``final_output``, ``n_turns``, and capsule chain head as ``AgentTeam.run`` for the same backend.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/learned_manifold.py::LearnedManifoldRegistry.is_trivial`; `tests/test_learned_manifold.py::TestTrivialLearnedPassthrough::test_trivial_run_matches_agent_team`; R-92 family `r92_trivial_learned_passthrough` (5/5 seeds, all four arms). |
| **W45-L-LEARNED-COMPROMISE-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W44-L-LIVE-DUAL-CHANNEL-COLLUSION-CAP)** | **When an adversary forges ALL SIX channel observations to match the registered policy, the learned controller cannot recover at the capsule layer — every channel's feature vector matches the trained "honest" distribution. The learned gate ratifies; the run propagates the bad upstream. Recovery requires either (a) a stricter role-handoff signature policy, (b) native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer (``W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT``), or (c) a trained adversarial-example detector that operates on a feature axis the attacker cannot trivially forge.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | R-92 family `r92_w45_compromise_cap` — `learned.mean == w44.mean == w43.mean == base.mean == 0.0` across 5/5 seeds. |
| **W45-L-PROMPT-HINT-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W44-L-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP)** | **The ``MANIFOLD_HINT`` prompt fragment guarantees only that the controller's recommendation is *present* in the model's context. A real LLM may or may not condition on the hint. The H6 hint-response gain is measured on the deterministic ``HintAwareSyntheticBackend``; on real LLMs the saving is bounded to "the hint is in context", not a guarantee of behavioural lift.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W45_LEARNED_MANIFOLD.md` (PART E "Token / bit cramming with deeper model-facing transfer", PART J "Theory and limitations"). |
| **W45-L-RIDGE-EXTRAPOLATION-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The ridge fitter is fitted on the training bank's feature distribution. For features that fall outside the training-bank support, the controller's prediction is *interpolated* via the sigmoid map — but the W45 layer does not guarantee monotonic behaviour at extrapolation boundaries. The confidence-bucket channel in the hint witness exposes this honestly to the model.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | Inspection of `forward_controller` (deterministic sigmoid-shaped readout); the `confidence_bucket` field in the hint witness CID. |
| **W45-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W44-C-LIVE-LATENT in a bounded direction)** | **The full direction of "learn a deep, transformer-coupled controller that consumes hidden states and emits attention-mask adjustments / KV-cache routing" remains substrate-blocked. The W45 mechanism is the strongest capsule-layer approximation we can write today; the next direction requires architectural access to the model's internals. Note: W45 *bounds* the W44-C-LIVE-LATENT conjecture by consuming the hyperbolic and euclidean channels at the learned layer (they were audit-only at W44), but it does not close transformer-internal consumption.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; out of capsule-layer scope; bounds W44-C-LIVE-LATENT** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W45_LEARNED_MANIFOLD.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W45-R92-EMPIRICAL** | **R-92 benchmark family across 5 seeds × 9 cell families: calibration-gain precision +0.400 strict gain on `r92_learned_calibration_gain` (W44 0.600 → W45 1.000, min == max); attention-specialization 1.000 on `r92_attention_specialization` (vs 0.000 for baseline / W43 / W44); role3-precision +0.500 strict gain on `r92_role_adapter_recovery` (shared-only 0.000 → with-adapter 1.000, min == max); factoradic-hint round-trip 1.000 on `r92_factoradic_hint_compression` (vs 0.000 for baseline / W43 / W44); model-facing task-correct rate +1.000 on `r92_model_facing_hint_response` (W44 0.000 → W45 1.000 under `HintAwareSyntheticBackend`, min == max); replay-determinism 1.000 on `r92_replay_determinism`. Falsifier `r92_w45_falsifier`: learned arm does NOT over-claim (no false abstentions). Limitation `r92_w45_compromise_cap`: learned arm cannot recover under all-six-channel compromise (0.000 across 5/5, the W45-L-LEARNED-COMPROMISE-CAP reproduces honestly). Sanity `r92_trivial_learned_passthrough`: passthrough_ok = 1.000 across all four arms.** | **proved-empirical (5/5 seeds × 9 families)** | `coordpy/r92_benchmark.py::run_all_families`; `tests/test_r92_benchmark.py::TestH*` (H1..H12). |

## Manifold memory controller + multi-layer fitted stack + causally-masked time-attention + multi-rank role adapter + learned dictionary basis + packed model-facing control surface + shared-prefix capsule (W46-T-MEMORY-COUPLING-DETERMINISM, W46-T-MULTI-LAYER-FITTER-SOUNDNESS, W46-T-TIME-ATTENTION-CAUSAL-MASK, W46-T-DICTIONARY-BIJECTION, W46-T-MULTI-RANK-ADAPTER-SUFFICIENCY, W46-T-PREFIX-CAPSULE-STABILITY, W46-T-CONTROL-TOKEN-BIJECTION, W46-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS, W46-L-TRIVIAL-MEMORY-PASSTHROUGH, W46-L-MEMORY-COMPROMISE-CAP, W46-L-CONTROL-TOKEN-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP, W46-L-SHARED-PREFIX-NOT-KV-CACHE-CAP, W46-L-RIDGE-STACK-EXTRAPOLATION-CAP, W46-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING, W46-C-AUTOGRAD-DEEP-STACK) — post-W45 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W46-T-MEMORY-COUPLING-DETERMINISM** | **For any deterministic backend and any fitted multi-layer controller params, two independent runs of ``ManifoldMemoryTeam.run`` over the same task with the same registry, agents, observation builder, training set, and dictionary basis produce byte-identical ``final_output``, byte-identical capsule chain root CIDs, byte-identical sequences of ``ManifoldMemoryHandoffEnvelope``, byte-identical multi-layer-controller-params CIDs, AND byte-identical memory-bank head CID per turn. The W46 layer adds no source of non-determinism beyond the underlying backend.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/manifold_memory.py::ManifoldMemoryTeam`; `coordpy/r93_benchmark.py::family_replay_determinism`; `tests/test_r93_benchmark.py::TestH11ReplayDeterminism`; `tests/test_manifold_memory.py::TestDeterminism`. |
| **W46-T-MULTI-LAYER-FITTER-SOUNDNESS** | **The stage-wise ridge fitter in ``fit_memory_controller`` solves L independent ridge regressions sequentially, each on the layer-wise residual of the previous prediction. Stage i+1's target is ``y - sum_{j <= i} layer_j(features)``; stage i+1's input is the same flattened channel features. Stage L+1 fits the rank-r role adapter on per-role residuals from the full L-layer stack. Stage L+2 builds the dictionary basis via seeded farthest-point + 1-pass mean refinement. This is a deterministic stage-wise closed-form computation — no autograd, no SGD, no randomness.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/manifold_memory.py::fit_memory_controller`; `tests/test_manifold_memory.py::TestMultiLayerFitter`. |
| **W46-T-TIME-ATTENTION-CAUSAL-MASK** | **For any flat query, any memory bank, any temperature, and any turn index t, ``compute_time_attention`` returns a ``TimeAttentionWitness`` whose ``pooled_value`` depends only on memory entries with ``turn_index < t``. Injecting a memory entry with ``turn_index >= t`` into the bank does NOT change the ``pooled_value``; the mask is enforced by ``ManifoldMemoryBank.admissible_for_turn``.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | R-93 `r93_causal_mask_preservation` family — `future_inject_delta == 0.0` across 5/5 seeds; `tests/test_manifold_memory.py::TestTimeAttention::test_future_entries_are_masked`. |
| **W46-T-DICTIONARY-BIJECTION** | **For any flat feature vector v of length ``W45_N_CHANNELS * feature_dim``, ``DictionaryBasis.encode(v) = (i, r)`` and ``DictionaryBasis.decode(i, r) = v`` exactly (modulo IEEE-754 round-trip at the 12-decimal ``_round_floats`` precision). The decode reconstructs the original vector by summing the prototype + the residual; the residual is the difference between the input vector and the closest prototype.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | R-93 `r93_dictionary_reconstruction` — `dictionary_round_trip_ok == 1.0` across 5/5 seeds; `tests/test_manifold_memory.py::TestDictionaryBasis::test_encode_decode_round_trip`. |
| **W46-T-MULTI-RANK-ADAPTER-SUFFICIENCY** | **When a fitted controller's shared base predicts the same sign for two roles whose gold conventions invert along *different* axes (one along the spherical axis, one along the subspace axis), a rank-2 role-specific delta recovers both inversions; a rank-1 delta can fit at most one. The R-93 ``r93_role_shift_adaptation`` family registers rank-2 precision = 1.000 vs shared-only precision = 0.000 across 5/5 seeds.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r93_benchmark.py::family_role_shift_adaptation`; `tests/test_r93_benchmark.py::TestH4RoleShiftAdaptation`. |
| **W46-T-PREFIX-CAPSULE-STABILITY** | **For any sequence of prior outputs and any ``prefix_turns = K``, calling ``build_prefix_capsule`` at turn k and turn k+1 (both with k >= K) produces the same ``prefix_sha256`` because the function consumes only the first K outputs of the sequence. The ``reused`` flag on the resulting capsule is True at turn k+1 when the caller passes the prior turn's ``prefix_sha256`` as the ``prior_prefix_sha`` argument.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/manifold_memory.py::build_prefix_capsule`; R-93 `r93_shared_prefix_reuse` — `prefix_reuse_ok == 1.0` across 5/5 seeds; `tests/test_manifold_memory.py::TestPrefixCapsule::test_first_n_outputs_only`. |
| **W46-T-CONTROL-TOKEN-BIJECTION** | **Given a ``ControlTokenWitness`` and the registered ``ctrl_mode``, the literal ``MANIFOLD_CTRL`` bytes are reconstructible exactly from the witness fields. The ``ctrl_bytes_sha256`` field binds the bytes; an auditor who re-builds the block from the witness fields will compute the same SHA-256.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/manifold_memory.py::build_control_token_string`; R-93 `r93_compressed_control_packing` — `ctrl_round_trip_ok == 1.0` across 5/5 seeds. |
| **W46-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W46 verifier: ``verify_manifold_memory_handoff`` enumerates 21 failure modes disjoint from W22..W45's 240 cumulative failure modes (``empty_w46_envelope``, ``w46_schema_version_unknown``, ``w46_schema_cid_mismatch``, ``w46_decision_branch_unknown``, ``w46_ctrl_mode_unknown``, ``w46_role_handoff_signature_cid_invalid``, ``w46_prompt_sha256_invalid``, ``w46_token_accounting_invalid``, ``w46_confidence_bucket_invalid``, ``w46_ratify_probability_invalid``, ``w46_controller_params_cid_invalid``, ``w46_dictionary_cid_invalid``, ``w46_time_attention_witness_cid_invalid``, ``w46_multi_rank_adapter_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w46_causal_mask_witness_cid_invalid``, ``w46_control_token_witness_cid_invalid``, ``w46_prefix_capsule_cid_invalid``, ``w46_memory_bank_head_cid_invalid``, ``w46_prompt_construction_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w46_memory_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w46_outer_cid_mismatch``). Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W46 = **261 enumerated failure modes**.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/manifold_memory.py::verify_manifold_memory_handoff`; `tests/test_manifold_memory.py::TestVerifier`. |
| **W46-L-TRIVIAL-MEMORY-PASSTHROUGH** | **When the memory registry is configured trivially (``memory_enabled=False``, ``time_attention_enabled=False``, ``dictionary_enabled=False``, ``control_token_mode='off'``, ``prefix_reuse_enabled=False``, ``params.fitting_method='unfitted'``, W45/W44/W43 inner trivial), the memory orchestrator emits no envelope side effects beyond the W45 trivial-passthrough envelope, and ``ManifoldMemoryTeam.run`` produces the same ``final_output``, ``n_turns``, and capsule chain head as ``AgentTeam.run`` for the same backend.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/manifold_memory.py::ManifoldMemoryRegistry.is_trivial`; `tests/test_manifold_memory.py::TestTrivialPassthrough::test_trivial_run_matches_agent_team`; R-93 family `r93_trivial_memory_passthrough` (5/5 seeds, all five arms). |
| **W46-L-MEMORY-COMPROMISE-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W45-L-LEARNED-COMPROMISE-CAP)** | **When an adversary forges ALL SIX channel observations to match the registered policy AND the memory bank is exposed to the same forged feature distribution, the W46 multi-layer controller cannot recover at the capsule layer — every channel's feature vector matches the trained "honest" distribution, every memory entry's gate logit is positive, and the time-attention readout amplifies (rather than counters) the forged ratify. Recovery requires either (a) a stricter role-handoff signature policy, (b) native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer (``W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT``), or (c) a trained adversarial-example detector that operates on a feature axis the attacker cannot trivially forge.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | R-93 family `r93_w46_compromise_cap` — `w46.mean == w45.mean == 0.0` across 5/5 seeds. |
| **W46-L-CONTROL-TOKEN-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W45-L-PROMPT-HINT-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP)** | **The ``MANIFOLD_CTRL`` packed control block guarantees only that the multi-layer controller's recommendation, layer logits, memory attention readout, dictionary index, and memory role-pattern signature are *present* in the model's context. A real LLM may or may not condition on the block. The H6 memory-facing-response gain is measured on the deterministic ``MemoryAwareSyntheticBackend`` which is engineered to detect both the ``MANIFOLD_CTRL:`` and ``mem_summary=`` substrings; on real LLMs the saving is bounded to "the packed control block is in the model's context".** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W46_MANIFOLD_MEMORY.md` (PART E "Token / bit cramming with deeper model-facing transfer", PART J "Theory and limitations"). |
| **W46-L-SHARED-PREFIX-NOT-KV-CACHE-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The shared-prefix capsule guarantees *byte-identical prefix bytes* across consecutive turns once the team has produced ``prefix_turns`` outputs. Whether the underlying transformer reuses its internal KV cache for that prefix is a model-side runtime concern — modern backends with prompt-caching may exploit byte-identical prefixes, but the W46 surface does not measure or assert this. The honest claim is "identical prefix bytes," not "identical KV state."** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/manifold_memory.py::build_prefix_capsule` docstring; R-93 `r93_shared_prefix_reuse` family — measures `prefix_reused == True` per turn but does not measure backend KV reuse. |
| **W46-L-RIDGE-STACK-EXTRAPOLATION-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W45-L-RIDGE-EXTRAPOLATION-CAP)** | **The multi-layer ridge stack is fitted on the training bank's feature distribution. The same out-of-distribution caveats that apply to the W45 single-layer fit apply at W46, additionally compounded by the time-attention readout's dependence on the bank's feature distribution: out-of-distribution features yield a low cosine similarity against the bank, the softmax weights become approximately uniform, and the pooled value is approximately the bank's mean gate logit.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | Inspection of `forward_memory_controller` + `compute_time_attention` + `r93_w46_falsifier` (no false abstain on the clean linear-flow regime). |
| **W46-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W45-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING in a further-bounded direction)** | **The full direction of "learn a deep, transformer-coupled controller that consumes hidden states and emits attention-mask adjustments / KV-cache routing" remains substrate-blocked. The W46 mechanism is the strongest capsule-layer approximation we can write today; the next direction requires architectural access to the model's internals. Note: W46 *further bounds* the W44-C-LIVE-LATENT carry-forward by adding the multi-layer + memory + dictionary path, but it does not close transformer-internal consumption.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; out of capsule-layer scope; further-bounds W44-C-LIVE-LATENT** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W46_MANIFOLD_MEMORY.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W46-C-AUTOGRAD-DEEP-STACK (closed at W47, under "pure-Python reverse-mode AD + Adam SGD" assumption)** | **A version of the W46 multi-layer stack trained via SGD / backprop (rather than stage-wise closed-form ridge) is structurally compatible with the current envelope chain. **Closed at W47** by the pure-Python reverse-mode autograd engine in `coordpy.autograd_manifold` (`Variable` + `AdamOptimizer` + `fit_autograd_controller`). See W47-T-AUTOGRAD-CORRECTNESS, W47-T-TRAIN-DETERMINISM, W47-T-DEEP-STACK-TRAINABLE.** | **closed-conditional; carry-forward replaced by W47** | `coordpy/autograd_manifold.py`; `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W47_AUTOGRAD_MANIFOLD.md`. |
| **W46-R93-EMPIRICAL** | **R-93 benchmark family across 5 seeds × 12 cell families: long-branching-memory deep-turns precision +1.000 strict gain on `r93_long_branching_memory` (W44/W45 0.000 → W46 1.000, min == max); cyclic-consensus preservation 1.000 on `r93_cyclic_consensus_memory` (W46 matches W45's ceiling); role-shift adaptation +1.000 strict gain on `r93_role_shift_adaptation` (shared-only 0.000 → rank-2 1.000, min == max); control-token round-trip 1.000 on `r93_compressed_control_packing` (W45 0.000 → W46 1.000); memory-facing task-correct rate +1.000 on `r93_memory_facing_hint_response` (W45 0.000 → W46 1.000 under `MemoryAwareSyntheticBackend`, min == max); causal-mask preservation 1.000 on `r93_causal_mask_preservation` (future-inject delta = 0.0); dictionary round-trip 1.000 on `r93_dictionary_reconstruction` (avg L1 = 0.0, closest-rate = 1.0); shared-prefix reuse 1.000 on `r93_shared_prefix_reuse` (1 reuse per 4-turn run); replay-determinism 1.000 on `r93_replay_determinism`. Falsifier `r93_w46_falsifier`: memory arm does NOT over-claim (no false abstentions). Limitation `r93_w46_compromise_cap`: memory arm cannot recover under all-six-channel + forged-bank compromise (0.000 across 5/5, the W46-L-MEMORY-COMPROMISE-CAP reproduces honestly). Sanity `r93_trivial_memory_passthrough`: passthrough_ok = 1.000 across all five arms.** | **proved-empirical (5/5 seeds × 12 families)** | `coordpy/r93_benchmark.py::run_all_families`; `tests/test_r93_benchmark.py::TestH*` (H1..H12). |

## Autograd manifold stack — pure-Python reverse-mode AD + Adam SGD + trainable multi-layer manifold stack + trainable rank-r LoRA-style role adapter + trainable K-prototype dictionary + trainable QKV memory head + trainable packed-control serializer + content-addressed training trace (W47-T-AUTOGRAD-CORRECTNESS, W47-T-TRAIN-DETERMINISM, W47-T-DEEP-STACK-TRAINABLE, W47-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS, W47-T-TRAINED-MEMORY-HEAD-BEATS-COSINE, W47-T-PACKED-CONTROL-LEARNABLE, W47-T-TRIVIAL-AUTOGRAD-PASSTHROUGH, W47-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP, W47-L-AUTOGRAD-DISTRIBUTION-CAP, W47-L-NO-HIDDEN-STATE-CAP, W47-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP, W47-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING, W47-C-LIVE-MULTI-HOST-AUTOGRAD, W47-C-GPU-BACKED-AUTOGRAD-SDK) — post-W46 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W47-T-AUTOGRAD-CORRECTNESS** | **For every operation in `W47_SUPPORTED_OPS` (`+`, `-`, `*`, `/`, `**`, `dot`, `matmul`, `tanh`, `sigmoid`, `relu`, `exp`, `log`, `softmax`, `mean`, `sum`), the analytic gradient returned by the `Variable._grad_fn` chain matches a central finite-difference estimate within 1e-5 absolute error on at least one deterministic test point. Empirical max FD err < 1e-9 across the 6 op classes exercised by R-94.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/autograd_manifold.py::gradient_check`; R-94 `r94_autograd_gradient_check` (max FD err < 1e-9 across 3/3 seeds); `tests/test_autograd_manifold.py::TestGradientChecks`. |
| **W47-T-TRAIN-DETERMINISM** | **For any deterministic training set, any seed, and any optimizer config, two independent runs of `fit_autograd_controller` produce byte-identical `AutogradManifoldParams.cid()` and byte-identical `TrainingTraceWitness.cid()`. Two independent runs of `AutogradManifoldTeam.run` with the same trained params produce byte-identical `final_output`, `root_cid`, every `autograd_outer_cid`, and every `memory_bank_head_cid`.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/r94_benchmark.py::family_replay_determinism`; `tests/test_r94_benchmark.py::TestH9ReplayDeterminism`; `tests/test_autograd_manifold.py::TestFitAutogradController::test_fit_replay_determinism`. |
| **W47-T-DEEP-STACK-TRAINABLE** | **The trained deep autograd stack's parameters strictly move from their seed-init values on a synthetic nonlinear regime where a single linear layer is provably insufficient (XOR-shaped label = sign(spherical * causal)). The stack does NOT diverge (no NaN/inf in the loss history) within 120 SGD steps under Adam.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/r94_benchmark.py::family_nonlinear_separability`; `tests/test_r94_benchmark.py::TestH4NonlinearSeparability`. |
| **W47-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W47 verifier: `verify_autograd_manifold_handoff` enumerates 21 failure modes disjoint from W22..W46's 261 cumulative failure modes (`empty_w47_envelope`, `w47_schema_version_unknown`, `w47_schema_cid_mismatch`, `w47_decision_branch_unknown`, `w47_ctrl_mode_unknown`, `w47_role_handoff_signature_cid_invalid`, `w47_prompt_sha256_invalid`, `w47_token_accounting_invalid`, `w47_confidence_bucket_invalid`, `w47_ratify_probability_invalid`, `w47_autograd_params_cid_invalid`, `w47_training_trace_cid_invalid`, `w47_autograd_forward_witness_cid_mismatch`, `w47_causal_mask_witness_cid_invalid`, `w47_control_token_witness_cid_invalid`, `w47_prefix_capsule_cid_invalid`, `w47_memory_bank_head_cid_invalid`, `w47_prompt_construction_witness_cid_mismatch`, `w47_autograd_witness_cid_mismatch`, `w47_emit_mask_invalid`, `w47_outer_cid_mismatch`). Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W47 = **279 enumerated failure modes**.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/autograd_manifold.py::verify_autograd_manifold_handoff`; `tests/test_autograd_manifold.py::TestVerifier`; R-94 `r94_autograd_envelope_verifier` (6 disjoint forgeries detected per seed). |
| **W47-T-TRAINED-MEMORY-HEAD-BEATS-COSINE** | **When trained on a synthetic one-hot key-value memory task where the gold pool value is the value at the key whose one-hot coincides with the query, the W47 trained QKV memory head achieves mean pooled-correctness ≥ 0.5 while the W46 cosine-similarity pool achieves 0.0. The conditional is on the data distribution being orthogonal one-hots (cosine is maximised in only one direction; the trained head can amplify the matching value beyond the others).** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r94_benchmark.py::family_trainable_memory_head`; `tests/test_r94_benchmark.py::TestH6TrainableMemoryHead`. |
| **W47-T-PACKED-CONTROL-LEARNABLE** | **The trainable packed control serializer's 4 sigmoid gates converge to any target boolean mask within 150 Adam steps under binary cross-entropy on the target. The learned emit mask is deterministically encoded in the envelope; the ctrl bytes remain bijective from the witness fields.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/r94_benchmark.py::family_trainable_packed_control`; `tests/test_autograd_manifold.py::TestAutogradControlSerializer::test_train_to_target_mask`. |
| **W47-T-TRIVIAL-AUTOGRAD-PASSTHROUGH** | **When `AutogradManifoldRegistry.is_trivial` is True (`autograd_enabled=False`, W46-trivial inner, `params.fitting_method='unfitted'`), `AutogradManifoldTeam.run` produces the same `final_output`, `n_turns`, and capsule chain head as `AgentTeam.run` for the same backend.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/autograd_manifold.py::AutogradManifoldRegistry.is_trivial`; `tests/test_autograd_manifold.py::TestTrivialPassthrough`; R-94 `r94_trivial_autograd_passthrough` (3/3 seeds, all six arms). |
| **W47-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP (limitation theorem)** | **The pure-Python autograd engine has per-step cost O(n_params × n_examples × n_layers) — no vectorisation, no GPU. Training a 24→16→16→1 stack on 64 examples for 200 steps is approximately 1.6M scalar ops. This caps practical n_steps at a few hundred for the per-family wall-clock budget; full convergence on tight non-trivial losses (XOR, hard memory tasks) requires NumPy/JAX/PyTorch bindings.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W47_AUTOGRAD_MANIFOLD.md`; the `r94_nonlinear_separability` H4 metric (deep_stack_trainable structural pass, but full XOR fitting deferred). |
| **W47-L-AUTOGRAD-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W46-L-MEMORY-COMPROMISE-CAP)** | **When an adversary controls the training distribution AND the runtime observations, the trained controller learns the adversary's distribution and cannot recover at the capsule layer. The R-94 `r94_autograd_compromise_cap` family registers mean `downstream_protect_rate` = 0.25 (max 0.5) — the trained controller is partially protective on some seeds (the trained margin happens to fire on out-of-distribution cells), but not majority-protective. Recovery requires either (a) a stricter role-handoff signature policy, (b) native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer (`W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT`), (c) a trained adversarial-example detector that operates on a feature axis the attacker cannot trivially forge, or (d) a disjoint training set the attacker did not influence.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | R-94 `r94_autograd_compromise_cap` family — `w47.mean ≤ 0.5` across 3/3 seeds. |
| **W47-L-NO-HIDDEN-STATE-CAP (limitation theorem; carries forward from W46)** | **The W47 autograd stack still does not touch transformer hidden state, KV cache, attention weights, or embeddings. If `H2..H8` succeed but the underlying real LLM ignores `MANIFOLD_CTRL` and the shared-prefix capsule, the behavioural lift evaporates. The R-94 H6 / H7 results use the deterministic `CtrlAwareAutogradBackend`; real-LLM realism anchors are bounded.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W47_AUTOGRAD_MANIFOLD.md`; `coordpy/autograd_manifold.py::CtrlAwareAutogradBackend` docstring. |
| **W47-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W46-L-CONTROL-TOKEN-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP)** | **The trained `MANIFOLD_CTRL` packed control block, with the learned emit mask, guarantees only that the trained-controller's recommendation + learned-emit-mask are present in the model's context. A real LLM may or may not condition on the block. The H12 task-correct rate is measured on the deterministic `CtrlAwareAutogradBackend`; on real LLMs the saving is bounded to "the trained packed control block is in the model's context".** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W47_AUTOGRAD_MANIFOLD.md`. |
| **W47-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W46-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING in a further-bounded direction)** | **The full direction of "train a deep, transformer-coupled controller that consumes hidden states and emits attention-mask adjustments / KV-cache routing" remains substrate-blocked. The W47 mechanism is the strongest capsule-layer approximation we can write today; W47 *strengthens* the W46 bounding by adding end-to-end-trainable capsule-layer controllers, but it does not close transformer-internal consumption.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; out of capsule-layer scope; further-bounds W46-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W47_AUTOGRAD_MANIFOLD.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W47-C-LIVE-MULTI-HOST-AUTOGRAD (new conjectural direction)** | **Sharing trained autograd params + memory bank across hosts is structurally compatible with the W47 envelope chain (the params CID and training-trace CID are content-addressed bytes), but requires a host-consensus protocol on which trained distribution to use. Out of scope for W47.** | **conjectural; new substrate; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W47_AUTOGRAD_MANIFOLD.md`. |
| **W47-C-GPU-BACKED-AUTOGRAD-SDK (deliberately deferred)** | **A version of the W47 autograd stack backed by NumPy / JAX / PyTorch (which would lift `W47-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP` and enable production-scale training within the same envelope chain) is structurally compatible with the current parameter CIDs — the parameter serialisation is float-based JSON — but is deliberately out of scope for W47 in order to preserve the pure-stdlib hermeticity of the released contract. A future milestone may add a NumPy/JAX path under an `[autograd-gpu]` extra.** | **conjectural; deliberately deferred; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W47_AUTOGRAD_MANIFOLD.md`. |
| **W47-R94-EMPIRICAL** | **R-94 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 12 cell families: trivial-passthrough 1.000 across all six arms (baseline / W43 / W44 / W45 / W46 / W47); autograd_grad_correct 1.000 on `r94_autograd_gradient_check` (max FD err < 1e-9 across 6 op classes); converged_ok 1.000 on `r94_autograd_convergence` (val_acc=1.000 within 200 steps); deep_stack_trainable 1.000 on `r94_nonlinear_separability` (deep stack params strictly move on XOR-shaped data); dict_trainable_ok 1.000 on `r94_trainable_dictionary` (trained K-prototype codebook moves from seed-init); trained_head_beats_cosine 1.000 on `r94_trainable_memory_head` (w47 trained = 0.5 vs w46 cosine = 0.0); rank2_role_adapter_ok 1.000 on `r94_trainable_role_adapter` (rank-2 trained acc ≥ 0.7); ctrl_round_trip_ok 1.000 on `r94_trainable_packed_control` (learned emit-mask matches target, ctrl bytes bijective); replay_determinism_ok 1.000 on `r94_replay_determinism` (bit-perfect across two fits + runs); verifier_soundness_ok 1.000 on `r94_autograd_envelope_verifier` (6 disjoint forgeries detected); task_correct_rate 1.000 on `r94_autograd_ctrl_aware_backend` (full ctrl > off > baseline). Limitation `r94_autograd_compromise_cap`: W47 mean = 0.25 (W46 = 0.0) — the W47-L-AUTOGRAD-DISTRIBUTION-CAP limitation reproduces (not majority-protective).** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 12 families)** | `coordpy/r94_benchmark.py::run_all_families`; `tests/test_r94_benchmark.py::TestH*` (H1..H12). |

## Shared-state transformer-proxy — shared base state + per-role rank-r LoRA delta + trainable pseudo-KV factor bank + multi-head proxy attention + slot-memory write head + reconstruction decoder + branch/cycle-aware bias + bijective branch-history compressor + learned latent-control serializer + content-addressed training trace (W48-T-SHARED-STATE-CID-STABILITY, W48-T-PSEUDO-KV-ALGEBRAIC-INTERFACE, W48-T-MULTI-HEAD-SPECIALISATION, W48-T-RECONSTRUCTION-DECODER-SOUNDNESS, W48-T-BRANCH-CYCLE-BIAS-EXPRESSIVITY, W48-T-WRITE-GATE-SELECTIVITY, W48-T-TRAIN-DETERMINISM, W48-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS, W48-T-BRANCH-HISTORY-BIJECTION, W48-T-LATENT-CTRL-BIJECTION, W48-L-TRIVIAL-SHARED-STATE-PASSTHROUGH, W48-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP, W48-L-PROXY-DISTRIBUTION-CAP, W48-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP, W48-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP, W48-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING, W48-C-REAL-KV-COUPLED-PROXY, W48-C-MULTI-HOST-SHARED-STATE) — post-W47 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W48-T-SHARED-STATE-CID-STABILITY** | **For any deterministic registry and any task, every turn of ``SharedStateProxyTeam.run`` references the same ``shared_state_capsule_cid``; per-role rank-``r`` delta CIDs are stable for the role. The base state lives across turns and roles unchanged; roles can audit prior turns' shared state from the envelope chain alone.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/shared_state_proxy.py::SharedStateCapsule.cid`; R-95 `r95_shared_state_cid_stability` — `shared_state_cid_stable == 1.0` across 3/3 seeds; `tests/test_shared_state_proxy_w48.py::TestSharedStateCIDStability`. |
| **W48-T-PSEUDO-KV-ALGEBRAIC-INTERFACE** | **For any query vector ``q``, any pseudo-KV bank with slots ``(k_i, v_i)`` and turn-index ``t_i``, and any current turn ``t``, ``ProxyAttentionHead.forward_value(q, {(k_i, v_i) : t_i < t})`` returns ``softmax((q W_Q) · (k_i W_K)^T / sqrt(d_factor)) · (v_i W_V)`` — exactly the algebraic interface of a transformer attention head, but with the K/V tensors stored at the capsule layer rather than the transformer's hidden-state cache. The causal mask is strict: ``admissible_for_turn(t)`` returns only ``{s : s.turn_index < t}``.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/shared_state_proxy.py::ProxyAttentionHead.forward_value`; `coordpy/shared_state_proxy.py::PseudoKVBank.admissible_for_turn`; `tests/test_shared_state_proxy_w48.py::TestPseudoKVBank::test_admissible_for_turn_causal_mask`. |
| **W48-T-MULTI-HEAD-SPECIALISATION** | **Under the bounded-feature assumption and the two-axis attention specialisation regime (R-95 H4), an ``H=2`` multi-head proxy attention block produces non-zero head diversity (``sum_i |attn_head_0[i] - attn_head_1[i]|`` strictly greater than 0); an ``H=1`` single-head block has 0 diversity by construction. R-95 empirical: ``multi_head_diversity > 0`` across 3/3 seeds; the W47 (no multi-head) reports 0.0.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r95_benchmark.py::family_multi_head_specialisation`; `tests/test_r95_benchmark.py::TestH4MultiHeadSpecialisation`. |
| **W48-T-RECONSTRUCTION-DECODER-SOUNDNESS** | **The trainable reconstruction decoder reduces L1 distance from the prior-turn flat channel feature vector below 3× the input L1 baseline on the synthetic recall regime. The decoder is a two-layer tanh + linear stack trained jointly with the proxy attention via L2 reconstruction loss; an auditor can re-fit and verify the decoder CID matches.** | **proved + empirical** | `coordpy/r95_benchmark.py::family_reconstruction_objective`; R-95 `r95_reconstruction_objective` — `reconstruction_l1_under_baseline == 1.0` across 3/3 seeds; `tests/test_r95_benchmark.py::TestH5ReconstructionObjective`. |
| **W48-T-BRANCH-CYCLE-BIAS-EXPRESSIVITY** | **The learned branch/cycle bias matrix separates two branches with *identical* channel features at >= 90% accuracy after 80 Adam steps on the synthetic split regime. The bias entry at ``(b, c)`` is added to the gate logit before sigmoid; with identical channel features the only signal-carrying parameter is the branch/cycle bias entry.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r95_benchmark.py::family_branch_cycle_bias`; R-95 `r95_branch_cycle_bias` — `branch_split_acc == 1.0` across 3/3 seeds; `tests/test_r95_benchmark.py::TestH6BranchCycleBias`. |
| **W48-T-WRITE-GATE-SELECTIVITY** | **The trained slot-memory write head produces strictly higher gate values on signal turns than on noise turns (mean_signal_gate - mean_noise_gate > 0.30) on the alternating signal/noise regime. The write head is a single trainable sigmoid scalar; gradient flows from BCE loss against the per-example ``write_target``.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r95_benchmark.py::family_write_gate_selectivity`; R-95 `r95_write_gate_selectivity` — `selectivity == 0.521` across 3/3 seeds; `tests/test_r95_benchmark.py::TestH7WriteGateSelectivity`. |
| **W48-T-TRAIN-DETERMINISM** | **For any deterministic training set, any seed, and any optimiser config, two independent runs of ``fit_shared_state_proxy`` produce byte-identical ``SharedStateProxyParams.cid()`` and byte-identical ``TrainingTraceWitness.cid()``. Two independent runs of ``SharedStateProxyTeam.run`` with the same trained params produce byte-identical ``final_output``, root CID, every ``proxy_outer_cid``, every ``shared_state_capsule_cid``, and every ``pseudo_kv_bank_head_cid``.
