Carries forward W47-T-TRAIN-DETERMINISM via the reused W47 pure-Python autograd engine.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/r95_benchmark.py::family_replay_determinism`; `tests/test_r95_benchmark.py::TestH10ReplayDeterminism`; `tests/test_shared_state_proxy_w48.py::TestFitSharedStateProxy::test_fit_replay_determinism`. |
| **W48-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W48 verifier: ``verify_shared_state_proxy_handoff`` enumerates 22 disjoint failure modes (``empty_w48_envelope``, ``w48_schema_version_unknown``, ``w48_schema_cid_mismatch``, ``w48_decision_branch_unknown``, ``w48_role_handoff_signature_cid_invalid``, ``w48_prompt_sha256_invalid``, ``w48_token_accounting_invalid``, ``w48_confidence_bucket_invalid``, ``w48_ratify_probability_invalid``, ``w48_proxy_params_cid_invalid``, ``w48_training_trace_cid_invalid``, ``w48_shared_state_capsule_cid_invalid``, ``w48_pseudo_kv_bank_head_cid_invalid``, ``w48_proxy_attention_cid_invalid``, ``w48_role_state_delta_cid_invalid``, ``w48_write_head_cid_invalid``, ``w48_reconstruction_decoder_cid_invalid``, ``w48_branch_cycle_bias_cid_invalid``, ``w48_latent_control_cid_invalid``, ``w48_proxy_forward_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w48_prompt_construction_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w48_latent_control_witness_cid_invalid``, ``w48_branch_history_witness_cid_invalid``, ``w48_proxy_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w48_emit_mask_invalid``, ``w48_outer_cid_mismatch``) disjoint from W22..W47's 279 cumulative failure modes. Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W48 = **301 enumerated failure modes**.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/shared_state_proxy.py::verify_shared_state_proxy_handoff`; `tests/test_shared_state_proxy_w48.py::TestVerifier`; R-95 `r95_proxy_envelope_verifier` (7 disjoint forgeries detected per seed). |
| **W48-T-BRANCH-HISTORY-BIJECTION** | **For any sequence of branch / cycle ids and any ``(n_branches, n_cycles)`` pair satisfying ``max(branch_id) < n_branches`` and ``max(cycle_id) < n_cycles``, ``decompress_branch_history(compress_branch_history(bp, cp))`` recovers ``(bp, cp)`` exactly. The packed integer occupies ``ceil(log2(n_branches)) + ceil(log2(n_cycles))`` bits per pair.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/shared_state_proxy.py::compress_branch_history` + `decompress_branch_history`; `tests/test_shared_state_proxy_w48.py::TestBranchHistoryCompressor::test_round_trip_exact`. |
| **W48-T-LATENT-CTRL-BIJECTION** | **Given a ``LatentControlWitness``, the literal ``LATENT_CTRL: SHARED_STATE_HASH=<12-hex> mask=<binary> bits=<binary>`` bytes are reconstructible exactly from the witness fields. The ``ctrl_bytes_sha256`` field binds the bytes; an auditor who re-builds the block from the witness fields will compute the same SHA-256.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/shared_state_proxy.py::build_latent_control_string`; `tests/test_shared_state_proxy_w48.py::TestLatentControl::test_build_latent_control_round_trip`. |
| **W48-L-TRIVIAL-SHARED-STATE-PASSTHROUGH** | **When the registry is configured trivially (``proxy_enabled=False``, ``pseudo_kv_enabled=False``, ``reconstruction_enabled=False``, ``branch_bias_enabled=False``, ``write_head_enabled=False``, ``latent_control_enabled=False``, W47-trivial inner), the W48 orchestrator produces the same ``final_output``, ``n_turns``, and capsule chain head as ``AutogradManifoldTeam.run`` for the same backend; every turn's ``decision_branch`` is ``W48_BRANCH_TRIVIAL_SHARED_STATE_PASSTHROUGH``.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/shared_state_proxy.py::SharedStateProxyRegistry.is_trivial`; `tests/test_shared_state_proxy_w48.py::TestTrivialPassthrough::test_trivial_w48_reduces_to_w47_team`; R-95 family `r95_trivial_shared_state_passthrough` (3/3 seeds, all seven arms). |
| **W48-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP (limitation theorem; carries forward and strengthens W43-C-COLLECTIVE-KV-POOLING and W47-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING)** | **The W48 pseudo-KV factor bank reproduces the algebraic interface of a KV cache — ``softmax((Q W_Q)·(K W_K)^T / sqrt(d_factor))·(V W_V)`` over admissible slots — at the capsule layer, with auditable byte-deterministic provenance. It does NOT transplant real KV state from a transformer's attention layers. Any claim that W48 closes ``W43-C-COLLECTIVE-KV-POOLING``, ``W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT``, ``W43-C-FULL-GRASSMANNIAN-HOMOTOPY``, ``W45-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING``, or ``W47-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING`` is over-stated.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W48-L-PROXY-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W47-L-AUTOGRAD-DISTRIBUTION-CAP)** | **When an adversary controls the pseudo-KV bank, the training distribution, AND the runtime observations, the trained W48 proxy cannot recover at the capsule layer — every channel's feature vector matches the trained "honest" distribution, every pseudo-KV slot is filled with adversarial keys / values, and the multi-head proxy attention ratifies on the adversarial cells. The R-95 ``r95_proxy_distribution_cap`` family registers mean ``downstream_protect_rate = 0.222`` across 3 seeds — the trained controller abstains on a minority of forged cells (the trained margin happens to fire on some out-of-distribution cells), but is not majority-protective. Recovery requires either (a) a stricter role-handoff signature policy, (b) native-latent evidence outside the capsule layer (``W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT``), (c) a trained adversarial-example detector that operates on a feature axis the attacker cannot trivially forge, or (d) a disjoint training set + bank the attacker did not influence.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | R-95 `r95_proxy_distribution_cap` family — `w48.mean = 0.222` across 3/3 seeds; `tests/test_r95_benchmark.py::TestH12ProxyDistributionCap`. |
| **W48-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP (limitation theorem; carries forward from W47)** | **The pure-Python autograd engine reused from W47 has per-step cost ``O(n_params × n_examples)`` — no vectorisation, no GPU. Training the W48 multi-head proxy + shared-state delta + reconstruction + branch-bias + write-head jointly on 16-32 examples for 40-200 SGD steps is approximately 1-3M scalar ops. This caps practical n_steps at a few hundred for the per-family wall-clock budget; full convergence on tight non-trivial losses (XOR, hard memory tasks) requires NumPy/JAX/PyTorch bindings.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/shared_state_proxy.py::fit_shared_state_proxy` (per-example SGD loop); `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W48-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (limitation theorem; carries forward from W47-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP)** | **The trained ``LATENT_CTRL`` packed control block, the ``SHARED_STATE_HASH`` header, and the ``BRANCH_HIST`` compressor guarantee only that the trained-controller's recommendation + shared-state fingerprint + branch-path are present in the model's context. A real LLM may or may not condition on the headers. The H13 task-correct rate is measured on the deterministic ``SharedStateAwareSyntheticBackend``; on real LLMs the saving is bounded to "the trained packed control block + shared-state header + branch-history header are in the model's context".** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W48-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W47-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING in a further-bounded direction)** | **The full direction of "train a deep, transformer-coupled controller that consumes hidden states and emits attention-mask adjustments / real KV-cache routing" remains substrate-blocked. The W48 mechanism is the strongest capsule-layer *executable proxy* we can write today; W48 *strengthens* the W47 bounding by adding shared base state + pseudo-KV factor bank + multi-head proxy attention + reconstruction + branch/cycle bias, but it does not close transformer-internal consumption.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; out of capsule-layer scope; further-bounds W47-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W48-C-REAL-KV-COUPLED-PROXY (new conjectural direction)** | **Coupling the pseudo-KV factor bank to a real LLM's KV cache through backend-side prompt caching hooks is structurally compatible with the W48 envelope chain (the pseudo-KV bank's slot CIDs are content-addressed bytes), but requires backend support beyond what the released ``LLMBackend`` protocol provides today. A future milestone may add a ``[kv-coupled]`` extra that wires the pseudo-KV bank to backend-side caches.** | **conjectural; new substrate; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W48-C-MULTI-HOST-SHARED-STATE (new conjectural direction; strengthens W47-C-LIVE-MULTI-HOST-AUTOGRAD)** | **Sharing the W48 ``SharedStateCapsule`` + pseudo-KV bank + trained params across hosts requires a host-consensus protocol on which shared-state byte payload to use. The base state's CID is already content-addressed, so the protocol's verifier is a no-op; the protocol's *agreement* is the open piece. Out of scope for W48.** | **conjectural; new substrate; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W48-R95-EMPIRICAL** | **R-95 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 14 cell families: trivial-passthrough 1.000 across all seven arms (baseline / W43 / W44 / W45 / W46 / W47 / W48); shared_state_cid_stable 1.000 on `r95_shared_state_cid_stability` (4 turns × 3 seeds); proxy_recall_cosine 0.750 on `r95_pseudo_kv_reuse` (W47 = 0.0); multi_head_diversity > 0 on `r95_multi_head_specialisation` (W47 = 0); reconstruction_l1_under_baseline 1.000 on `r95_reconstruction_objective` (W47 = 0); branch_split_acc 1.000 on `r95_branch_cycle_bias` (W47 = 0.5 random); write_gate_selectivity 0.521 on `r95_write_gate_selectivity` (W47 = 0); latent_ctrl_round_trip_ok 1.000 on `r95_latent_control_round_trip`; compressed_save_ratio 0.667 on `r95_branch_history_compression`; replay_determinism_ok 1.000 on `r95_replay_determinism`; verifier_soundness_ok 1.000 on `r95_proxy_envelope_verifier` (7 disjoint forgeries detected); task_correct_rate 1.000 on `r95_shared_state_aware_backend` (W47 = 0); sdk_byte_identity_preserved 1.000 on `r95_proxy_falsifier`. Limitation `r95_proxy_distribution_cap`: W48 mean = 0.222 — the W48-L-PROXY-DISTRIBUTION-CAP limitation reproduces (not majority-protective).** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 14 families)** | `coordpy/r95_benchmark.py::run_all_families`; `tests/test_r95_benchmark.py::TestH*` (H1..H14). |

## Multi-block cross-bank coordination — multi-block stacked transformer-proxy + role-conditioned multi-bank pseudo-KV + learned eviction policy + retention head + dictionary codebook compression + content-addressed shared-latent capsule per turn + cramming witness (W49-T-MULTI-BLOCK-DEPTH-EXPRESSIVITY, W49-T-MULTI-BANK-CAUSAL-INTERFERENCE-BOUND, W49-T-LEARNED-EVICTION-SELECTIVITY, W49-T-RETENTION-HEAD-CORRECTNESS, W49-T-DICTIONARY-COMPRESSION-RATE, W49-T-SHARED-LATENT-CHAIN-WALK, W49-T-CRAMMING-WITNESS-SOUNDNESS, W49-T-MULTI-BLOCK-TRAIN-DETERMINISM, W49-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS, W49-T-LONG-HORIZON-RETENTION, W49-T-AGGRESSIVE-COMPRESSION-RECOVERY, W49-L-TRIVIAL-MULTI-BLOCK-PASSTHROUGH, W49-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP, W49-L-MULTI-BLOCK-DISTRIBUTION-CAP, W49-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP, W49-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP, W49-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING, W49-C-CROSS-MODEL-LATENT-TRANSFER) — post-W48 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W49-T-MULTI-BLOCK-DEPTH-EXPRESSIVITY** | **Under the bounded-feature assumption and the three-way nonlinear composition regime (R-96 H2: ``label = sign(sph * cau * hyp)``), an ``L_p = 2`` multi-block proxy transformer strictly separates the composition that a single block (``L_p = 1``, the W48 regime) cannot. R-96 empirical: mean accuracy ``L_p = 2 = 0.833``, ``L_p = 1 = 0.542``, ``Δ = +0.292`` across 3/3 seeds. Each block has its own trainable ``(W_Q, W_K, W_V, W_O, W_FFN1, b_FFN1, W_FFN2, b_FFN2, residual_scale)`` and runs in sequence with residual connections.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::MultiBlockProxyStack`; `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::family_multi_block_depth`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH2MultiBlockDepth`. |
| **W49-T-MULTI-BANK-CAUSAL-INTERFERENCE-BOUND** | **For any pair of roles ``(r_a, r_b)`` with ``r_a ≠ r_b`` and any admissible turn ``t`` and any forged slot ``s`` written into ``r_a``'s pseudo-KV bank at turn ``t-1``, the W49 read from ``r_b``'s bank at turn ``t`` is unperturbed by ``s``: L2 distance to the un-forged-read baseline is exactly 0. The proof is by inspection: ``MultiBankPseudoKV`` returns disjoint per-role banks and ``_bank_read`` queries only the role's own bank. R-96 empirical: 3/3 seeds report perturbation = 0.000.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::MultiBankPseudoKV.get_or_init_role_bank`; `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::family_cross_bank_interference`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH8CrossBankInterference`. |
| **W49-T-LEARNED-EVICTION-SELECTIVITY** | **Under a tight bank capacity with a single high-write-gate signal slot and many low-write-gate noise slots that partly overlap with the signal direction, the trained eviction policy retains the signal slot under bank overflow at recall cosine = 0.859 across 3 seeds, while plain FIFO drops the signal at recall cosine = 0.000. ``Δ = +0.859``.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::EvictionPolicy.evict_index`; `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::family_learned_eviction`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH4LearnedEviction`. |
| **W49-T-RETENTION-HEAD-CORRECTNESS** | **The trained retention head answers the binary "was this fact stored?" question at accuracy 1.000 across 3/3 seeds on the synthetic regime, vs the W48 baseline (no retention head, returns 0.5 = chance). The head is a two-layer tanh-then-sigmoid stack trained jointly with the rest of the W49 stack via BCE on per-example retention labels.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::RetentionHead`; `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::family_retention_head`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH5RetentionHead`. |
| **W49-T-DICTIONARY-COMPRESSION-RATE** | **The W49 packed ``LATENT_CTRL_V2`` control block (dictionary code + shared-latent header) saves 25% of the visible-token cost vs the W48 ``LATENT_CTRL`` block on the H6 R-96 cell, while round-tripping bijectively through the ``LatentControlV2Witness`` CID. The dictionary codebook is trained jointly via soft-assignment cross-entropy on a K-prototype index target. R-96 empirical: w49_ctrl_tokens = 3, w48_ctrl_tokens = 4, savings_ratio = 0.250 across 3/3 seeds.** | **proved + empirical** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::DictionaryCodebook`; `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::family_dictionary_compression`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH6DictionaryCompression`. |
| **W49-T-SHARED-LATENT-CHAIN-WALK** | **Given a ``MultiBlockProxyTeam.run`` envelope chain, an auditor can recover every prior turn's ``SharedLatentCapsule.cid()`` by walking the ``shared_latent_parent_cid`` field of each envelope in turn order; no external state required. The shared-latent capsule at turn ``t`` is the projection of the multi-block output of turn ``t-1`` (via ``SharedLatentProjector``); content-addressed. R-96 empirical: chain_walk_ok = 1.000 across 3/3 seeds; latent_evolves_ok = 1.000 (all 4 turns produce distinct latent CIDs).** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::SharedLatentCapsule`, `SharedLatentProjector`; `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::family_shared_latent_capsule`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH7SharedLatentCapsule`. |
| **W49-T-CRAMMING-WITNESS-SOUNDNESS** | **The per-turn ``CrammingWitness.structured_bits`` field equals ``int(dictionary_code_bits) + int(len(emit_mask)) + int(len(bits_payload))`` exactly; the ``bits_per_visible_token`` field equals ``structured_bits / (visible_ctrl_tokens + visible_latent_header_tokens)`` rounded to 12 decimals. Bound under the witness CID; tamper-evident under SHA-256.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::CrammingWitness`, `build_cramming_witness`; `tests/test_multi_block_proxy_w49.py::TestCrammingWitness`. |
| **W49-T-MULTI-BLOCK-TRAIN-DETERMINISM** | **For any deterministic training set, any seed, and any optimiser config, two independent runs of ``fit_multi_block_proxy`` produce byte-identical ``MultiBlockProxyParams.cid()`` and byte-identical ``MultiBlockTrainingTraceWitness.cid()``. Two independent runs of ``MultiBlockProxyTeam.run`` with the same trained params produce byte-identical ``final_output``, root CID, every ``multi_block_outer_cid``, every per-role and shared ``multi_bank_head_cid``, the trained-params CID, training-trace CID, and the shared-latent capsule chain. Carries forward W47/W48 determinism via the reused W47 pure-Python autograd engine.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::family_replay_determinism`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH9ReplayDeterminism`; `tests/test_multi_block_proxy_w49.py::TestFitMultiBlockProxy::test_fit_replay_determinism`. |
| **W49-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W49 verifier: ``verify_multi_block_proxy_handoff`` enumerates 22 disjoint failure modes (``empty_w49_envelope``, ``w49_schema_version_unknown``, ``w49_schema_cid_mismatch``, ``w49_decision_branch_unknown``, ``w49_role_handoff_signature_cid_invalid``, ``w49_multi_block_params_cid_invalid``, ``w49_training_trace_cid_invalid``, ``w49_multi_block_stack_cid_invalid``, ``w49_bank_router_cid_invalid``, ``w49_bank_mix_gate_cid_invalid``, ``w49_eviction_policy_cid_invalid``, ``w49_retention_head_cid_invalid``, ``w49_dictionary_cid_invalid``, ``w49_shared_latent_projector_cid_invalid``, ``w49_shared_latent_capsule_cid_invalid``, ``w49_multi_bank_head_cid_invalid``, ``w49_latent_ctrl_v2_witness_cid_invalid``, ``w49_cramming_witness_cid_invalid``, ``w49_multi_block_forward_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w49_multi_block_witness_cid_mismatch``, ``w49_outer_cid_mismatch``, ``w49_token_accounting_invalid``) disjoint from W22..W48's 301 cumulative failure modes. **Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W49 = 323 enumerated failure modes**. R-96 empirical: detection_rate = 1.000 across 3/3 seeds on 8 disjoint forgeries.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::verify_multi_block_proxy_handoff`; `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::W49_ALL_FAILURE_MODES`; `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::family_envelope_verifier`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH10EnvelopeVerifier`. |
| **W49-T-LONG-HORIZON-RETENTION** | **On a length-12 branch path with a target fact emitted at turn 0 and 11 cluttering writes from other roles at turns 1..11, the W49 role-conditioned multi-bank read at turn 12 recovers the fact at cosine 1.000 across 3/3 seeds; the W48 single-bank baseline at the same total capacity recovers at cosine 0.732 (``Δ = +0.268``). The role-bank read is unperturbed by other-role writes by W49-T-MULTI-BANK-CAUSAL-INTERFERENCE-BOUND.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r97_benchmark.py::family_long_branch_retention`; `tests/test_r97_benchmark.py::TestH11LongBranchRetention`. |
| **W49-T-AGGRESSIVE-COMPRESSION-RECOVERY** | **Under aggressive compression (W49 emits the ``LATENT_CTRL_V2`` block with the dictionary code only and zero ``emit_mask``/``bits_payload``), the W49 control block carries 3 structured bits in 3 visible tokens (info_per_visible_token = 1.0), while a W48 aggressive equivalent (1-bit mask + 1-bit payload) carries 2 bits in 4 tokens (info_per_visible_token = 0.5). ``Δ = +0.5``.** | **proved + empirical** | `coordpy/r97_benchmark.py::family_aggressive_compression`; `tests/test_r97_benchmark.py::TestH15AggressiveCompression`. |
| **W49-L-TRIVIAL-MULTI-BLOCK-PASSTHROUGH** | **When the registry is configured trivially (``multi_block_enabled=False``, ``multi_bank_enabled=False``, ``retention_enabled=False``, ``dictionary_enabled=False``, ``shared_latent_capsule_enabled=False``, ``eviction_enabled=False``, W48-trivial inner), the W49 orchestrator produces the same ``final_output`` and ``n_turns`` as ``SharedStateProxyTeam.run`` for the same backend; every turn's ``decision_branch`` is ``W49_BRANCH_TRIVIAL_MULTI_BLOCK_PASSTHROUGH``.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::MultiBlockProxyRegistry.is_trivial`; `tests/test_multi_block_proxy_w49.py::TestTrivialPassthrough::test_trivial_w49_reduces_to_w48_team`; R-96 family `r96_trivial_multi_block_passthrough` (3/3 seeds, all three arms). |
| **W49-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP (limitation theorem; carries forward and strengthens W48-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP)** | **The W49 multi-bank pseudo-KV factor banks reproduce the algebraic interface of a per-role + shared KV cache at the capsule layer with auditable byte-deterministic provenance. They do NOT transplant real KV state from a transformer's attention layers. Any claim that W49 closes ``W43-C-COLLECTIVE-KV-POOLING``, ``W43-C-MIXED-CURVATURE-LATENT``, ``W43-C-FULL-GRASSMANNIAN-HOMOTOPY``, ``W47-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING``, ``W48-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING``, or ``W48-C-REAL-KV-COUPLED-PROXY`` is over-stated.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W49_MULTI_BLOCK_PROXY.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W49-L-MULTI-BLOCK-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (limitation theorem; strengthens W48-L-PROXY-DISTRIBUTION-CAP)** | **When an adversary controls the multi-bank pseudo-KV banks, the training distribution, AND the runtime observations, the trained W49 multi-block stack cannot recover at the capsule layer — every channel's feature vector matches the trained "honest" distribution, every per-role + shared bank is filled with adversarial keys/values, and the multi-block proxy ratifies on the adversarial cells. The R-97 ``r97_multi_block_distribution_cap`` family registers mean ``downstream_protect_rate = 0.000`` across 3 seeds — the trained controller does not abstain on forged cells matching the training distribution.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | R-97 `r97_multi_block_distribution_cap` family; `tests/test_r97_benchmark.py::TestH16MultiBlockDistributionCap`. |
| **W49-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP (carries forward from W47/W48)** | **The pure-Python autograd engine reused from W47 has per-step cost ``O(n_params × n_examples)``. The W49 multi-block stack's per-step cost is approximately ``L_p`` × W48 cost (one full block forward per ``L_p`` layer). At default ``L_p = 2`` this caps practical n_steps at ~80 on a 16-example training set for the per-family wall-clock budget; full convergence on tight non-trivial losses requires NumPy/JAX/PyTorch bindings.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/multi_block_proxy.py::fit_multi_block_proxy`. |
| **W49-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (carries forward from W48)** | **The trained ``LATENT_CTRL_V2`` packed control block + ``SHARED_LATENT_HASH`` header guarantee only that the trained-controller's recommendation + shared-latent fingerprint are present in the model's context. A real LLM may or may not condition on the headers. The H14 task-correct rate is measured on the deterministic ``MultiBlockAwareSyntheticBackend``; on real LLMs the saving is bounded to "the trained packed control block + shared-latent header are in the model's context".** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W49_MULTI_BLOCK_PROXY.md`. |
| **W49-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W48-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING in a further-bounded direction)** | **The full direction of "train a deep, transformer-coupled controller that consumes hidden states and emits attention-mask adjustments / real KV-cache routing" remains substrate-blocked. The W49 mechanism is the strongest capsule-layer *executable proxy* we can write today; W49 *strengthens* the W48 bounding by adding multi-block depth + role-conditioned multi-bank pseudo-KV + learned eviction + retention head + dictionary codebook + per-turn shared-latent capsule, but it does not close transformer-internal consumption.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; out of capsule-layer scope; further-bounds W48-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING** | `docs/RESULTS_COORDPY_W49_MULTI_BLOCK_PROXY.md` ("What was NOT done — honest scope"). |
| **W49-C-CROSS-MODEL-LATENT-TRANSFER (new conjectural direction)** | **Sharing the W49 shared-latent capsule chain across two backends with different tokenizers is structurally compatible with the envelope chain (the shared-latent capsule's CID is content-addressed bytes), but requires a tokenizer-agnostic adapter on the backend side. A future milestone may add a ``[cross-model-latent]`` extra. Out of W49 scope.** | **conjectural; new substrate; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W49_MULTI_BLOCK_PROXY.md`. |
| **W49-R96-EMPIRICAL** | **R-96 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 10 cell families: trivial-passthrough 1.000 across baseline / W48 / W49 arms; multi_block_depth 0.833 vs 0.542 (Δ +0.292) on three-way composition; multi_bank_recall 1.000 vs 0.792 (Δ +0.208); learned_eviction 0.859 vs 0.000 (Δ +0.859); retention_head 1.000 vs 0.500 (Δ +0.500); dictionary_compression 0.250 token-savings vs W48; shared_latent_capsule 1.000 (4 distinct latent CIDs, chain-walk recoverable); cross_bank_interference 0.000 (perfect isolation); replay_determinism 1.000; envelope_verifier 1.000 (8/8 forgeries detected).** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 10 families)** | `coordpy/r96_benchmark.py::run_all_families`; `tests/test_r96_benchmark.py::TestH*` (H1..H10). |
| **W49-R97-EMPIRICAL** | **R-97 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 6 cell families: long_branch_retention 1.000 vs 0.732 (Δ +0.268, length-12 path); cycle_reconstruction 0.461 vs 0.000 (Δ +0.461, multi-bank recovers cycle's first emission while FIFO single-bank overwrites); cramming_bits_ratio 5.0 vs 3.0 bits/visible-token (1.67× ratio); shared_state_vs_transcript 1.000 vs 0.000 task-correct rate (live realism anchor on ``MultiBlockAwareSyntheticBackend``); aggressive_compression 1.000 vs 0.500 info/visible-token; multi_block_distribution_cap 0.000 downstream_protect_rate (limitation `W49-L-MULTI-BLOCK-DISTRIBUTION-CAP` reproduces).** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 6 families)** | `coordpy/r97_benchmark.py::run_all_families`; `tests/test_r97_benchmark.py::TestH*` (H11..H16). |

## Cross-backend latent coordination — five orthogonal capsule-native advances over W49: cross-backend latent projector (M1) + L=4 deep proxy stack (M2) + adaptive K=16 compression with learned emit-mask (M3) + role-pair pseudo-KV transfer with adaptive eviction V2 (M4) + chain-walkable shared-latent carrier V2 + reconstruction V2 head (M5) (W50-T-CROSS-BACKEND-PROJECTOR-SOUNDNESS, W50-T-DEEP-STACK-L4-EXPRESSIVITY, W50-T-CROSS-BANK-TRANSFER-INTERFACE, W50-T-ADAPTIVE-EVICTION-V2-MONOTONICITY, W50-T-ADAPTIVE-COMPRESSION-RATE-BOUND, W50-T-RECONSTRUCTION-V2-CORRECTNESS, W50-T-W50-OUTER-CID-CHAIN, W50-T-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH-BYTE-IDENTICAL, W50-T-CRAMMING-WITNESS-V2-SOUNDNESS, W50-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS, W50-T-LONG-HORIZON-RETENTION-8TURN, W50-T-LONG-HORIZON-RETENTION-12TURN-STRETCH, W50-T-CROSS-BACKEND-FIDELITY-SYNTHETIC, W50-L-TRIVIAL-W50-PASSTHROUGH, W50-L-CROSS-BACKEND-TOKENIZER-CAP, W50-L-CROSS-BANK-COMPROMISE-CAP, W50-L-DEEP-STACK-RESIDUAL-PATHOLOGY-CAP, W50-L-RATE-FLOOR-CAP, W50-L-MULTI-BLOCK-DISTRIBUTION-CAP, W50-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP, W50-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP, W50-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP, W50-C-CROSS-TOKENIZER-LATENT-TRANSFER, W50-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING, W50-C-REAL-KV-COUPLED-PROXY, W50-C-MULTI-HOST-SHARED-STATE) — post-W49 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W50-T-CROSS-BACKEND-PROJECTOR-SOUNDNESS** | **The cross-backend encode→decode roundtrip is a deterministic fixed point at trivial parameters; the projector params CID is content-addressed and reproducible. Carries forward W43-W49 deterministic-audit conventions.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/cross_backend_alignment.py::BackendEncoder.init`, `BackendDecoder.init`; `tests/test_cross_backend_alignment_w50.py`. |
| **W50-T-DEEP-STACK-L4-EXPRESSIVITY** | **Under the bounded-feature assumption + the four-step product-amplified composition regime (R-98 H2: ``label = sign(amp · prod_signs(...))``), an ``L=4`` deep proxy stack strictly separates a composition that the W49 ``L_p=2`` stack cannot fit cleanly. R-98 empirical: mean ``acc(L=4) - acc(L=2) = +0.094`` on 3 seeds — passes the ``≥ +0.05`` honest bar under the W47 pure-Python autograd training cost cap.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack.py::DeepProxyStack`; `coordpy/r98_benchmark.py::family_deep_stack_depth_strict_gain`. |
| **W50-T-CROSS-BANK-TRANSFER-INTERFACE** | **Role-pair transfer preserves the W49 bank algebraic interface: slot keys/values remain ``factor_dim`` vectors; transfer is a learned linear projection per ordered role pair. R-98 empirical: trained recall 0.371 vs no-transfer baseline 0.078 (Δ +0.294) across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked + empirical** | `coordpy/cross_bank_transfer.py::CrossBankTransferLayer.transfer_slot`; `coordpy/r98_benchmark.py::family_cross_bank_transfer_role_pair_gain`. |
| **W50-T-ADAPTIVE-EVICTION-V2-MONOTONICITY** | **The V2 keep-score ``sigmoid(w · [age_norm, role_match, write_gate, retention_prob, transfer_signal])`` is monotone non-decreasing in ``retention_prob`` and ``write_gate``, non-increasing in ``age_norm`` and ``transfer_signal`` under the W50 hand-crafted weights ``[-0.5, 0.0, 0.5, 4.0, -2.0]``. R-98 empirical: V2 keeps signal slot 1.000 on all 3 seeds; FIFO drops it 0.000.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/cross_bank_transfer.py::AdaptiveEvictionPolicyV2`; `coordpy/r98_benchmark.py::family_adaptive_eviction_v2_vs_v1`. |
| **W50-T-ADAPTIVE-COMPRESSION-RATE-BOUND** | **Under K=16 codebook + adaptive emit-mask + emit_mask_len = bits_payload_len = 10, the trained gate achieves mean ratio 9.32 bits/visible-token across 3 seeds — strictly above the H9 8.0 bar and 1.86× the W49 declared baseline (5.0). The accounting: ``structured_bits = code_bits (4) + emit_mask_len (10) + mask_sum``; ``visible_tokens = 1 + (1 if mask_sum > 0)``.** | **proved + empirical** | `coordpy/adaptive_compression.py::compress_carrier`; `coordpy/r99_benchmark.py::family_adaptive_compression_8bits`. |
| **W50-T-RECONSTRUCTION-V2-CORRECTNESS** | **The trained reconstruction V2 head recovers turn ``t-k`` flat features at MSE 0.201 (3-seed mean at k=3) — strictly below the random-prediction baseline (MSE 0.333) and the H8 0.25 bar. Honest under the W47 pure-Python autograd training cost cap.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/shared_latent_carrier.py::ReconstructionV2Head`; `coordpy/r99_benchmark.py::family_reconstruction_v2_recovers_prior_turn`. |
| **W50-T-W50-OUTER-CID-CHAIN** | **The W50 outer-CID chain ``w47_outer → w48_proxy_outer → w49_multi_block_outer → w50_outer`` verifies end-to-end. Each link binds the prior CID by inclusion in the dataclass payload; tamper at any link changes the outer hash. R-98 empirical: every forged envelope is rejected with the corresponding enumerated failure mode.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/w50_team.py::W50HandoffEnvelope.cid`, `verify_w50_handoff`. |
| **W50-T-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH-BYTE-IDENTICAL** | **``W50Team`` with ``W50Params.build_trivial()`` produces an envelope whose internal ``w49_root_cid`` equals the W49 baseline ``MultiBlockProxyTeamResult.root_cid`` byte-for-byte. ``final_output`` matches. The W50 outer CID strictly wraps the W49 root + the empty W50 bundle.** | **proved + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/w50_team.py::W50Params.build_trivial`; `tests/test_w50_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W50-T-CRAMMING-WITNESS-V2-SOUNDNESS** | **The W50 ``CrammingWitnessV2.structured_bits`` field equals ``code_bits + emit_mask_len + mask_sum`` exactly; ``visible_tokens = 1 + (1 if mask_sum > 0 else 0)``; ``bits_per_visible_token = structured_bits / max(1, visible_tokens)``. Bound under the witness CID; tamper-evident.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/adaptive_compression.py::CrammingWitnessV2`. |
| **W50-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W50 verifier: ``verify_w50_handoff`` enumerates 20 disjoint failure modes disjoint from W22..W49's 323. **Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W50 = 343 enumerated failure modes**. R-98 empirical: detection rate 1.000 on the envelope verifier family.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/w50_team.py::W50_ENVELOPE_VERIFIER_FAILURE_MODES`. |
| **W50-T-LONG-HORIZON-RETENTION-8TURN** | **On a length-8 branch path with signal at turn 0 + 7 noise writes, the W50 retention-aware bank (V2 eviction + capacity 8) recovers the signal at cosine 1.000 across 3 seeds. W49 baseline (FIFO + capacity 3) drops to 0.023.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r99_benchmark.py::family_long_horizon_retention_8turn`. |
| **W50-T-LONG-HORIZON-RETENTION-12TURN-STRETCH** | **On a 12-turn path, W50 recovers signal at cosine 1.000 across 3 seeds — passes H7 0.70 bar with margin. Honest about drop-off: W50 doesn't claim retention beyond capacity_w50.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r99_benchmark.py::family_long_horizon_retention_12turn_stretch`. |
| **W50-T-CROSS-BACKEND-FIDELITY-SYNTHETIC** | **On the synthetic primary anchor (two synthetic backends with circular-shift gold transformation), the trained ``CrossBackendAlignmentLayer`` achieves mean alignment fidelity 0.956 across 3 seeds — passes H3 0.95 bar.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/cross_backend_alignment.py::fit_cross_backend_alignment`. |
| **W50-L-TRIVIAL-W50-PASSTHROUGH (limitation theorem)** | **Trivial W50Registry reduces to MultiBlockProxyTeam byte-for-byte.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `tests/test_w50_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W50-L-CROSS-BACKEND-TOKENIZER-CAP (sharpens W49-C-CROSS-MODEL-LATENT-TRANSFER)** | **Behavioral transfer across genuinely different tokenizers requires backend-side adapters out of W50 scope. The H11 realism anchor probe records ``anchor_status = "synthetic_only"`` when ``COORDPY_W50_OLLAMA_REACHABLE`` is unset.** | **proved-conditional limitation + carry-forward sharper than W49-C** | `coordpy/cross_backend_alignment.py::run_realism_anchor_probe`. |
| **W50-L-CROSS-BANK-COMPROMISE-CAP (new at W50)** | **Adversarial role-pair training set forgery → trained transfer cannot recover. R-98 empirical: protect rate 0.902.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/cross_bank_transfer.py::forge_cross_bank_training_set`. |
| **W50-L-DEEP-STACK-RESIDUAL-PATHOLOGY-CAP (new at W50)** | **``residual_scale = 0`` collapses L=4 stack to noise. R-98 empirical: pathology accuracy 0.472 (∼chance).** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack.py::force_residual_pathology`. |
| **W50-L-RATE-FLOOR-CAP (new at W50)** | **Target rate 16 bits/token exceeds K=16 codebook structural ceiling. R-99 empirical: rate_target_missed=True across 3 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/adaptive_compression.py::probe_rate_floor_falsifier`. |
| **W50-L-MULTI-BLOCK-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (strengthens W49-L)** | **Adversarial forgery across all W50 trainable surfaces → cannot recover. R-99 empirical: protect rate 0.877.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r99_benchmark.py::family_w50_distribution_cap`. |
| **W50-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP (carries forward W49-L)** | **W50 cross-bank transfer, adaptive eviction V2, carrier V2, reconstruction V2 all operate over capsule-layer pseudo-KV slots — do NOT transplant real KV bytes.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W50_CROSS_BACKEND_LATENT_COORDINATION.md`. |
| **W50-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP (carries forward)** | **W50 stage-wise cost = sum of per-module costs (M1: 288 steps, M2: 288, M3: 96, M4: 192, M5: 480). Capped at a few hundred steps per module on Mac wall-clock; tighter convergence requires NumPy/JAX/PyTorch.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | per-module ``fit_*`` functions. |
| **W50-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (carries forward W48/W49)** | **``LATENT_CTRL_V3`` packed control guarantees only that the controller's recommendation is in the model's context. A real LLM may or may not condition on it.** | **proved-conditional limitation + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W50_CROSS_BACKEND_LATENT_COORDINATION.md`. |
| **W50-C-CROSS-TOKENIZER-LATENT-TRANSFER (sharper than W49-C)** | **W49 conjecture sharpened: the W50 projector + carrier chain is trained and auditable; only tokenizer-level divergence remains carried forward. A future ``[cross-tokenizer-adapter]`` extra may close it.** | **conjectural; sharper bounds than W49-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W50_CROSS_BACKEND_LATENT_COORDINATION.md`. |
| **W50-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W47/W48/W49)** | **Full transformer-internal hidden-state + KV-cache coupling remains substrate-blocked. W50 further-bounds W49 by adding M1..M5 but does not close it.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; further-bounds W49-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W50_CROSS_BACKEND_LATENT_COORDINATION.md`. |
| **W50-C-REAL-KV-COUPLED-PROXY (carries forward W48-C)** | **Unchanged.** | **conjectural; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W50-C-MULTI-HOST-SHARED-STATE (carries forward W48-C)** | **Unchanged.** | **conjectural; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W50-R98-EMPIRICAL** | **R-98 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 10 cell families: trivial-passthrough 1.000 (W49 byte-identity preserved); cross_backend_alignment_synthetic w50 0.956 vs baseline 0.063 (Δ +0.893); realism_probe synthetic-only 1.000; deep_stack_depth w50 0.844 vs L=2 0.750 (Δ +0.094); residual_pathology w50 0.472 (chance) vs healthy 0.764; cross_bank_role_pair w50 0.371 vs no-transfer 0.078 (Δ +0.294); cross_bank_compromise protect 0.902; adaptive_eviction_v2 w50 1.000 vs FIFO 0.000 (Δ +1.000); envelope_verifier w50 1.000; replay_determinism 1.000.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 10 families)** | `coordpy/r98_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W50-R99-EMPIRICAL** | **R-99 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 7 cell families: long_horizon_retention_8turn w50 1.000 vs FIFO 0.023 (Δ +0.977); 12turn w50 1.000 vs FIFO 0.469 (Δ +0.531); reconstruction_v2 MSE 0.201 vs random 0.333; adaptive_compression_8bits w50 9.323 vs W49 5.000 (Δ +4.323); rate_floor_falsifier reproduces 1.000; aggressive_compression_recovery w50 1.000; w50_distribution_cap protect 0.877.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 7 families)** | `coordpy/r99_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |

## Persistent Cross-Backend Latent Coordination (W51-T-*, W51-L-*, W51-C-*) — Post-W50 research milestone

| Claim                                                  | Description                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | Status                                                                 | Anchor                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                              |
| ------------------------------------------------------ | -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **W51-T-PERSISTENT-STATE-GRU-SOUNDNESS** | **The GRU update rule ``s_t = (1 - z_t) ⊙ s_{t-1} + z_t ⊙ tanh(W_h · [s_{t-1}; x_t])`` is a deterministic fixed point at trivial parameters: when ``z_t = 0``, ``s_t = s_{t-1}`` exactly. R-100 empirical: trivial-passthrough preserves W50 outer CID byte-for-byte.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked + empirical** | `coordpy/persistent_shared_latent.py::PersistentStateCell.step_value`; `tests/test_w51_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W51-T-TRIPLE-BACKEND-TRANSITIVITY** | **Under the trained joint loss ``L = L(A→B) + L(A→C) + L(B→C) + w · L(A→B→C)``, the transitivity gap ``|fid(A→C) - fid(A→B→C)|`` is bounded. R-100 empirical: mean transitivity gap 0.087 across 3 seeds — passes the H3 ≤ 0.10 ceiling.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/cross_backend_translator.py::fit_triple_backend_translator`; `coordpy/r100_benchmark.py::family_triple_backend_transitivity_gap`. |
| **W51-T-DEEP-STACK-V2-L6-STRUCTURAL** | **The ``L=6`` deep stack V2 with branch/cycle-specialised heads achieves classifier accuracy ≥ 0.65 on a six-step composition regime and exhibits non-regression relative to W50's ``L=4`` baseline (mean delta +0.014 across 3 seeds, ≥ -0.05 cap floor). Strict gain over ``L=4`` is NOT claimed under pure-Python autograd; the V2 win comes from branch/cycle specialisation (H5: +0.056).** | **proved-conditional + empirical (non-monotonicity acknowledged)** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack_v2.py::DeepProxyStackV2`; `coordpy/r100_benchmark.py::family_deep_stack_v2_depth_strict_gain`, `family_branch_specialised_heads_gain`. |
| **W51-T-HIERARCHICAL-COMPRESSION-RATE-BOUND** | **Under the K1=32 + K2=16 hierarchical codebook + adaptive emit gate with emit_mask_len=14 and full mask emit, the achieved bits-per-visible-token ratio = 13.0 (R-101 empirical, 3 seeds × 1 sample). Capacity per (coarse, fine) pair = log2(32·16) = 9 bits — auditable structural ceiling.** | **proved + empirical** | `coordpy/hierarchical_compression.py::compress_carrier_hierarchical`; `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::family_hierarchical_compression_12bits`. |
| **W51-T-RECONSTRUCTION-V3-K5-CORRECTNESS** | **The trained two-headed reconstruction V3 (causal + branch) recovers turn ``t-5`` flat features at MSE 0.409 (3-seed mean) — passes the H13 ≤ 0.50 bar. Honest under the W47 pure-Python autograd training cost cap.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/long_horizon_retention.py::LongHorizonReconstructionV3Head`; `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::family_reconstruction_v3_recovers_t_minus_5`. |
| **W51-T-RECONSTRUCTION-V3-K8-DROPOFF** | **At k=8 (design-maximum lookback), V3 MSE = 0.462 (3-seed mean) — passes the H14 ≤ 0.60 stretch bar. Drop-off past k=8 is graceful (witness records the curve across k∈{1..16}).** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/long_horizon_retention.py::evaluate_long_horizon_mse_curve`; `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::family_reconstruction_v3_k8_stretch`. |
| **W51-T-BRANCH-CYCLE-MEMORY-PAGE-ISOLATION** | **The per-branch and per-cycle memory pages are content-addressed and disjoint across branch / cycle indices: a write to branch index b₀ produces a slot CID indexed only in ``branch_pages[b₀]``, recoverable from the page head CID. R-100 empirical: BCM recall 0.993 (vs generic 0.785; Δ +0.208) — passes H6 ≥ +0.15.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked + empirical** | `coordpy/branch_cycle_memory.py::BranchCycleMemoryHead`; `coordpy/r100_benchmark.py::family_branch_cycle_memory_gain`. |
| **W51-T-W51-OUTER-CID-CHAIN** | **The W51 outer-CID chain ``w47_outer → w48_proxy_outer → w49_multi_block_outer → w50_outer → w51_outer`` verifies end-to-end. Each link binds the prior CID by inclusion in the dataclass payload; tamper at any link changes the outer hash. R-100 empirical: every forged envelope is rejected with the corresponding enumerated failure mode (verifier score 1.000 across 3 seeds).** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/w51_team.py::W51HandoffEnvelope.cid`, `verify_w51_handoff`. |
| **W51-T-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH-BYTE-IDENTICAL** | **``W51Team`` with ``W51Params.build_trivial()`` produces an envelope whose internal ``w50_outer_cid`` equals the W50 baseline ``W50TeamResult.w50_outer_cid`` byte-for-byte. ``final_output`` matches. The W51 outer CID strictly wraps the W50 outer CID + the empty W51 bundle.** | **proved + mechanically-checked + empirical** | `coordpy/w51_team.py::W51Params.build_trivial`; `tests/test_w51_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W51-T-PERSISTENT-STATE-CHAIN-WALK** | **Chain-walk from any ``PersistentLatentState`` recovers the parent chain up to depth ``W51_DEFAULT_MAX_CHAIN_WALK_DEPTH = 16``. Each ``PersistentLatentState.cid()`` is content-addressed and includes ``parent_state_cid``; cycle detection terminates walk.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked + empirical** | `coordpy/persistent_shared_latent.py::PersistentLatentStateChain.walk_from`; `tests/test_persistent_shared_latent_w51.py`. |
| **W51-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS** | **Trust-boundary soundness of the W51 verifier: ``verify_w51_handoff`` enumerates 24 disjoint failure modes disjoint from W22..W50's 343. **Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W51 = 367 enumerated failure modes**. R-100 empirical: detection rate 1.000 on the envelope verifier family.** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/w51_team.py::W51_ENVELOPE_VERIFIER_FAILURE_MODES`. |
| **W51-T-LONG-HORIZON-RETENTION-12TURN** | **On a length-12 task with signal at turn 0 + 11 noise inputs, the trained W51 persistent state cell recovers the signal at cosine 0.707 across 3 seeds vs W50 untrained baseline -0.237 (Δ +0.945). Passes H11 ≥ 0.60 + Δ ≥ 0.20 bars.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::family_long_horizon_retention_12turn`. |
| **W51-T-LONG-HORIZON-RETENTION-16TURN-STRETCH** | **On a 16-turn path, W51 cosine 0.796 across 3 seeds — passes H12 ≥ 0.40 stretch bar. Honest about drop-off: W51 doesn't claim full recovery beyond capacity.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::family_long_horizon_retention_16turn_stretch`. |
| **W51-T-COMPRESSION-DEGRADATION-CURVE-MONOTONICITY** | **Under decreasing token budgets ``{8, 4, 2, 1}``, the achieved bits/token does not collapse to chance — minimum 6.17 across 3 seeds (R-101). Witnessed by the per-budget degradation curve in the witness payload.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/hierarchical_compression.py::probe_degradation_curve`; `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::family_compression_degradation_curve`. |
| **W51-L-TRIVIAL-W51-PASSTHROUGH (limitation theorem)** | **Trivial ``W51Registry`` reduces to ``W50Team`` byte-for-byte.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `tests/test_w51_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W51-L-CROSS-TOKENIZER-TRIPLE-CAP (sharpens W50-C-CROSS-TOKENIZER-LATENT-TRANSFER)** | **Triple-backend transitivity at the capsule layer is trained and auditable; behavioural transitivity across genuinely different tokenizers requires backend-side adapters out of W51 scope. The H7 realism anchor probe records ``anchor_status = "synthetic_only"`` when ``COORDPY_W51_OLLAMA_REACHABLE`` is unset.** | **proved-conditional limitation + carry-forward sharper than W50-C** | `coordpy/cross_backend_translator.py::run_triple_realism_anchor_probe`. |
| **W51-L-CROSS-BACKEND-TRANSLATOR-COMPROMISE-CAP (new at W51)** | **Adversarial triple-backend training set forgery → trained translator cannot recover. R-100 empirical: protect rate 0.944 across 3 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/cross_backend_translator.py::forge_triple_backend_training_set`. |
| **W51-L-DEEP-STACK-OVERDEPTH-CAP (new at W51)** | **``L=6`` does NOT strictly improve over ``L=4`` on shallow composition regimes. R-101 empirical: (acc_L6 − acc_L4) = -0.05 on a 2-step regime (3 seeds). Passes H18 ≤ +0.05 cap floor.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::family_deep_stack_v2_overdepth_cap`. |
| **W51-L-LONG-HORIZON-DROPOFF-CAP (new at W51)** | **At k > 8, V3 reconstruction MSE rises (curve probe witnesses the drop-off). Bounds the reconstruction claim.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/long_horizon_retention.py::evaluate_long_horizon_mse_curve`. |
| **W51-L-COMPRESSION-RATE-FLOOR-V2-CAP (new at W51)** | **Target rate 20 bits/token exceeds K1=32 + K2=16 hierarchical codebook structural ceiling (~9 bits/pair). R-101 empirical: rate_target_missed=True.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/hierarchical_compression.py::probe_rate_floor_v2_falsifier`. |
| **W51-L-PXBLC-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (strengthens W50-L)** | **Adversarial forgery across all W51 trainable surfaces → cannot recover. R-101 empirical: protect rate 0.771.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::family_w51_distribution_cap`. |
| **W51-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP (carries forward W50-L)** | **W51 persistent state, triple-backend translator, deep stack V2, hierarchical compression, long-horizon reconstruction V3, branch/cycle memory all operate over capsule-layer abstractions — do NOT transplant real KV bytes.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W51_PERSISTENT_LATENT_COORDINATION.md`. |
| **W51-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP (carries forward)** | **W51 stage-wise cost = sum of per-module costs. Capped at a few hundred steps per module on Mac wall-clock; tighter convergence requires NumPy/JAX/PyTorch. The H4 L=6 strict-gain claim is **not** met under this cap — see W51-T-DEEP-STACK-V2-L6-STRUCTURAL.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | per-module ``fit_*`` functions. |
| **W51-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (carries forward W48/W49/W50)** | **The ``LATENT_CTRL_V3_H`` packed hierarchical control guarantees only that the controller's recommendation is in the model's context. A real LLM may or may not condition on it.** | **proved-conditional limitation + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W51_PERSISTENT_LATENT_COORDINATION.md`. |
| **W51-C-CROSS-TOKENIZER-TRIPLE-TRANSITIVITY (sharper than W50-C)** | **W50 conjecture sharpened: capsule-layer triple-backend transitivity is now trained and auditable; only tokenizer-level transitivity remains carried forward. A future ``[cross-tokenizer-triple-adapter]`` extra may close it.** | **conjectural; sharper bounds than W50-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W51_PERSISTENT_LATENT_COORDINATION.md`. |
| **W51-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W47/W48/W49/W50)** | **Full transformer-internal hidden-state + KV-cache coupling remains substrate-blocked. W51 further-bounds W50 by adding M1..M6 but does not close it.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; further-bounds W50-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W51_PERSISTENT_LATENT_COORDINATION.md`. |
| **W51-C-REAL-KV-COUPLED-PROXY (carries forward W48-C)** | **Unchanged.** | **conjectural; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W51-C-MULTI-HOST-SHARED-STATE (carries forward W48-C)** | **Unchanged.** | **conjectural; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W51-R100-EMPIRICAL** | **R-100 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 11 cell families: trivial_w51_passthrough 1.000 (W50 byte-identity preserved); persistent_state_long_horizon_gain w51 0.707 vs w50 -0.237 (Δ +0.945); triple_backend_transitivity w51 0.887 vs unfitted 0.070; triple_backend_transitivity_gap w51 0.087 vs untrained 1.000; deep_stack_v2_depth w51 0.833 vs L4 0.819 (Δ +0.014, structural floor passed); branch_specialised_heads w51 0.833 vs shared 0.778 (Δ +0.056); branch_cycle_memory_gain w51 0.993 vs generic 0.785 (Δ +0.208); triple_backend_realism_probe synthetic-only 1.000; w51_envelope_verifier 1.000; w51_replay_determinism 1.000; cross_backend_translator_compromise_cap protect 0.944.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 11 families)** | `coordpy/r100_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W51-R101-EMPIRICAL** | **R-101 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 8 cell families: long_horizon_retention_12turn w51 0.707 vs w50 -0.237 (Δ +0.945); long_horizon_retention_16turn_stretch w51 0.796 vs w50 0.037 (Δ +0.759); reconstruction_v3_recovers_t_minus_5 w51 mse 0.409 vs w50 baseline 0.775 (Δ -0.366); reconstruction_v3_k8_stretch w51 mse 0.462 vs w50 ceiling 1.000 (Δ -0.538); hierarchical_compression_12bits w51 13.000 vs w50 12.000 (Δ +1.000); compression_degradation_curve min w51 6.167 vs w50 0.000 (Δ +6.167); w51_distribution_cap protect 0.771; deep_stack_v2_overdepth_cap (L6-L4) -0.05 (cap reproduces).** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 8 families)** | `coordpy/r101_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |

## Quantised Persistent Multi-Hop Latent Coordination (W52-T-*, W52-L-*, W52-C-*) — Post-W51 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **W52-T-PERSISTENT-V4-STACKED-SOUNDNESS** | **The two-layer stacked GRU + identity-init skip-link is a deterministic fixed point at trivial parameters and a strict improvement on V3 under mid-sequence distractor regimes. R-102 / R-103 empirical: 24-turn V4 cosine 0.995 vs trained V3 0.757 (Δ +0.238); 20-turn V4 0.995 vs V3 0.762 (Δ +0.234).** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked + empirical** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v4.py::V4StackedCell.step_value`; `coordpy/r102_benchmark.py::family_persistent_v4_long_horizon_gain`; `coordpy/r103_benchmark.py::family_long_horizon_v4_retention_20turn`. |
| **W52-T-MULTI-HOP-QUAD-TRANSITIVITY-LEN3** | **Under the trained quad-backend translator with disagreement-weighted arbitration, the chain-length-3 transitivity gap `\|fid(A→D) − fid(A→B→C→D)\|` is bounded. R-102 empirical: mean gap 0.058 across 3 seeds; transitive fidelity 0.924 ≥ 0.70 bar.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator.py::fit_multi_hop_translator`; `coordpy/r102_benchmark.py::family_multi_hop_quad_transitivity`. |
| **W52-T-DISAGREEMENT-WEIGHTED-ARBITRATION-WIN** | **Under a perturbed-edge regime (single-edge corruption + calibrated per-edge confidence), the disagreement-weighted arbitration produces strictly higher mean fidelity than naive equal-weight arbitration. R-102 empirical: weighted 0.724 vs naive 0.375 (Δ +0.348).** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator.py::MultiHopBackendTranslator.disagreement_weighted_arbitration`; `coordpy/r102_benchmark.py::family_disagreement_weighted_arbitration`. |
| **W52-T-DEEP-STACK-V3-L8-STRUCTURAL** | **The `L=8` deep stack V3 (role banks + residual gate) achieves classifier accuracy ≥ 0.55 on an eight-step composition regime and exhibits non-regression relative to W51's `L=6` V2 baseline (mean delta +0.083 across 3 seeds, ≥ -0.05 cap floor). Strict gain over `L=6` V3 is NOT claimed on shallow regimes — H21 cap reproduces.** | **proved-conditional + empirical (non-monotonicity acknowledged)** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack_v3.py::DeepProxyStackV3`; `coordpy/r102_benchmark.py::family_deep_stack_v3_depth_strict_gain`. |
| **W52-T-ROLE-GRAPH-TRANSFER-GAIN** | **The trained role-graph mixer with per-edge `(src, dst)` linear projections beats equal-weight cross-role averaging on a direction-dependent regime. R-102 empirical: role-graph 0.806 vs equal-weight 0.080 (Δ +0.727).** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/role_graph_transfer.py::RoleGraphMixer`; `coordpy/r102_benchmark.py::family_role_graph_transfer_gain`. |
| **W52-T-TRANSCRIPT-VS-SHARED-STATE-WIN** | **Under a fixed visible-token budget B=3 on a 12-dim carrier, the shared-latent arm encoded via K1×K2×K3 quantised codebook retains the target signal at strictly higher cosine than the transcript-truncation arm. R-102 empirical: shared 0.718 vs transcript 0.464 (Δ +0.253).** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/transcript_vs_shared_state.py::compare_transcript_vs_shared_state`; `coordpy/r102_benchmark.py::family_transcript_vs_shared_state`. |
| **W52-T-QUANTISED-COMPRESSION-RATE-BOUND** | **Under the K1=32 × K2=16 × K3=8 quantised codebook + adaptive budget gate with emit_mask_len=16 and full mask emit, the achieved bits-per-visible-token ratio = 15.67 (R-103 empirical, 3 seeds × 1 sample). Capacity per (coarse, fine, ultra) triple = log2(32·16·8) = 12 bits — auditable structural ceiling.** | **proved + empirical** | `coordpy/quantised_compression.py::compress_carrier_quantised`; `coordpy/r103_benchmark.py::family_quantised_compression_14bits`. |
| **W52-T-RECONSTRUCTION-V4-K8-CORRECTNESS** | **The trained three-headed reconstruction V4 (causal + branch + cycle) recovers turn `t-8` flat features at MSE 0.417 (3-seed mean) — passes the H15 ≤ 0.55 bar.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/long_horizon_retention_v4.py::LongHorizonReconstructionV4Head`; `coordpy/r103_benchmark.py::family_reconstruction_v4_recovers_t_minus_8`. |
| **W52-T-RECONSTRUCTION-V4-K12-DROPOFF** | **At k=12 (design-maximum lookback), V4 MSE = 0.369 (3-seed mean) — passes the H16 ≤ 0.70 stretch bar.** | **proved-conditional + empirical** | `coordpy/long_horizon_retention_v4.py::evaluate_long_horizon_v4_mse_curve`; `coordpy/r103_benchmark.py::family_reconstruction_v4_k12_stretch`. |
| **W52-T-BCM-V2-JOINT-PAGE-MERGE-AUDIT** | **The V2 branch/cycle memory head adds joint `(branch, cycle)` pages with content-addressed merge audit trail and importance-weighted eviction. R-103 empirical: joint recall 0.991 vs V1 0.657 (Δ +0.334).** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked + empirical** | `coordpy/branch_cycle_memory_v2.py::BranchCycleMemoryV2Head`; `coordpy/r103_benchmark.py::family_branch_cycle_memory_v2_merge_gain`. |
| **W52-T-W52-OUTER-CID-CHAIN** | **The W52 outer-CID chain `w47_outer → w48_proxy_outer → w49_multi_block_outer → w50_outer → w51_outer → w52_outer` verifies end-to-end. Each link binds the prior CID by inclusion in the dataclass payload; tamper at any link changes the outer hash. R-102 empirical: every forged envelope is rejected with the corresponding enumerated failure mode (verifier score 1.000 across 3 seeds).** | **proved by inspection + mechanically-checked** | `coordpy/w52_team.py::W52HandoffEnvelope.cid`, `verify_w52_handoff`. |
