## Persistent Mergeable Corruption-Robust Latent OS (W53-T-*, W53-L-*, W53-C-*) — Post-W52 research milestone

| Claim | Description | Status | Anchor |
| ----- | ----------- | ------ | ------ |
| **W53-T-V5-PERSISTENT-SKIP-LINK-EXPRESSIVITY (new at W53)** | **The 3-layer V5 stacked GRU with persistent skip-link applied at every step is strictly more expressive than V4's turn-0-only skip-link in the long-horizon retention setting; V5 has the V4 cell as a special case (set persistent skip projection = 0).** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v5.py::V5StackedCell.step_value`. |
| **W53-T-V5-MERGE-HEAD-SOUNDNESS (new at W53)** | **The V5 state-merge head is a per-dim sigmoid gate; merged_state = α ⊙ a + (1-α) ⊙ b is a convex combination per-dim, hence bounded by max(\|a\|, \|b\|) per dimension. Idempotent on a==b.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v5.py::V5StackedCell.merge_states_value`. |
| **W53-T-V5-CHAIN-WALK-DEPTH (new at W53)** | **R-106 H33 empirical: V5 chain walks back ≥ 16 turns under a 20-turn run.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/r106_benchmark.py::family_persistent_v5_chain_walk_depth`. |
| **W53-T-MULTI-HOP-V3-CHAIN-LEN4-FIDELITY (new at W53)** | **R-104 H3 empirical: 5-backend chain-length-4 fidelity is bounded; trained translator achieves chain_len4_fid_mean ≥ 0.7 across the synthetic suite.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v3.py::score_quint_fidelity`. |
| **W53-T-UNCERTAINTY-AWARE-ARBITRATION-SOUNDNESS (new at W53)** | **The uncertainty-aware arbiter returns a weighted mean prediction PLUS a per-dim 1-sigma std-dev; the std-dev is the c_p-weighted std of {y_p[i]}; aggregate_confidence is the mean path confidence.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v3.py::uncertainty_aware_arbitration`. |
| **W53-T-MLSC-CAPSULE-CID-STABILITY (new at W53)** | **MergeableLatentCapsule.cid() is a deterministic hash over (kind, branch_id, parent_cids, payload, confidence, fact_tags, merge_weights, turn_index); identical inputs produce identical CIDs.** | **proved by inspection + R-106 H28 empirical (replay determinism 1.0 on consistent parents)** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule.py::MergeableLatentCapsule.cid`; `coordpy/r106_benchmark.py::family_mlsc_merge_replay_determinism`. |
| **W53-T-MLSC-MERGE-WEIGHTS-SUM-TO-ONE (new at W53)** | **MergeOperator.merge produces weights that sum to 1.0 (modulo float64 epsilon ≤ 1e-6); softmax over scaled confidences guarantees this.** | **proved by inspection + verifier check** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule.py::MergeOperator.merge`; `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule.py::verify_mlsc_witness::w53_mlsc_merge_weights_dont_sum_to_one`. |
| **W53-T-MLSC-AUDIT-WALK-TO-ROOTS (new at W53)** | **MergeAuditTrail.walk_to_roots returns the deduplicated set of ROOT-kind capsule CIDs reachable from a given leaf; orphan parents are surfaced as roots-with-warning. R-104 H11 empirical: walk-to-roots correctness 1.0 on 4-root + chained merge.** | **proved by inspection + R-104 H11 empirical** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule.py::MergeAuditTrail.walk_to_roots`. |
| **W53-T-MLSC-CONSENSUS-QUORUM-K-OF-N (new at W53)** | **compute_consensus_quorum picks the largest K-clique under cosine_floor; abstains when no K-clique exists. R-104 H5 empirical: 1.0 correct (consensus on consistent + abstain on random).** | **proved by inspection + R-104 H5 empirical** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule.py::compute_consensus_quorum`. |
| **W53-T-DEEP-V4-CORRUPTION-AWARE-SOUNDNESS (new at W53)** | **DeepProxyStackV4.detect_corruption_value returns a confidence in [0,1] AND a corruption flag; the flag fires iff any per-layer L2 falls below floor or above ceiling. R-104 H6 empirical: 1.0 correct on (normal, pathological) test pair.** | **proved by inspection + R-104 H6 empirical** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack_v4.py::DeepProxyStackV4.detect_corruption_value`. |
| **W53-T-ECC-PARITY-DETECT-SINGLE-BIT (new at W53)** | **The XOR parity bit per segment detects all single-bit flips that affect any segment bit (the parity bit toggles iff exactly one segment bit toggles). R-106 H23 empirical: detect_rate 1.0 across 20 carriers × 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-106 H23 empirical** | `coordpy/ecc_codebook_v5.py::decode_with_parity_check`. |
| **W53-T-ECC-PARTIAL-CORRECTION-RECOVERS-VIA-SURVIVING-SEGMENTS (new at W53)** | **When exactly one segment is corrupted, decoding zeroes its contribution; the surviving 3 segments still carry signal. R-106 H24 empirical: correction_rate 1.0 across 20 carriers × 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-106 H24 empirical** | `coordpy/ecc_codebook_v5.py::decode_with_parity_check`. |
| **W53-T-CRC-MAJORITY-PAYLOAD-RECOVERY (new at W53)** | **3-of-3 majority repetition recovers the correct bit when ≤ 1 of the 3 reps is corrupted (per-bit error rate 3p²−2p³ vs raw p).** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier.py::CorruptionRobustCarrier.decode_with_majority`. |
| **W53-T-BMM-V3-CONSENSUS-ABSTAIN-SOUNDNESS (new at W53)** | **BranchMergeMemoryV3Head.read_consensus returns abstain=True iff no consensus has been populated for the cycle. R-106 H27 empirical: 1.0 correct abstain when K=4 and cosine_floor=0.99.** | **proved by inspection + R-106 H27 empirical** | `coordpy/branch_merge_memory_v3.py::BranchMergeMemoryV3Head.read_consensus`. |
| **W53-T-TVS-ARBITER-V2-ORACLE-CORRECTNESS (new at W53)** | **R-105 H22 empirical: TVS arbiter V2 picks the oracle-optimal arm 1.0 of the time on the heterogeneous-confidence probe.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/r105_benchmark.py::family_arbiter_strict_dominance`. |
| **W53-T-UNCERTAINTY-LAYER-CALIBRATION (new at W53)** | **R-104 H10 empirical: composite-confidence calibration_gap ≥ 0.10 across 30 separable probes × 3 seeds. High-conf strictly more accurate than low-conf.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/uncertainty_layer.py::calibration_check`; `coordpy/r104_benchmark.py::family_uncertainty_layer_calibration`. |
| **W53-T-W53-OUTER-CID-CHAIN (new at W53)** | **Every W53 envelope binds the W52 outer CID, the W53 params CID, every W53 per-turn witness bundle CID, the persistent V5 chain CID, and the MLSC audit trail CID into a single w53_outer_cid; the chain w47 → w48 → w49 → w50 → w51 → w52 → w53 is content-addressed end-to-end.** | **proved by inspection + R-104 H7 + H8 empirical** | `coordpy/w53_team.py::W53HandoffEnvelope.cid`. |
| **W53-T-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH-BYTE-IDENTICAL (new at W53)** | **trivial W53 reduces to W52 byte-for-byte. R-104 H1 empirical: passthrough_ok 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `tests/test_w53_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W53-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS (new at W53)** | **W53 envelope verifier rejects forged envelopes (29 enumerated failure modes). R-104 H7 empirical: verifier_score 1.0.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/w53_team.py::verify_w53_handoff`. |
| **W53-L-TRIVIAL-W53-PASSTHROUGH (new at W53)** | **Trivial W53 reduces to W52 byte-for-byte. Any divergence is a fatal regression.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `tests/test_w53_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W53-L-OVERDEPTH-V4-CAP (new at W53)** | **L=10 V4 does NOT strictly improve over L=8 V3 on shallow composition regimes. R-105 H20 empirical: (acc_L10 − acc_L8) ≤ +0.02 (cap reproduces).** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r105_benchmark.py::family_deep_v4_overdepth_cap`. |
| **W53-L-ECC-RATE-FLOOR-CAP (new at W53)** | **Target rate 40 bits/token exceeds K1=32 × K2=16 × K3=8 × K4=4 + parity codebook structural ceiling (~18 bits/visible-token). R-105 H21 empirical: rate_target_missed=True 1.000 across 3 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/ecc_codebook_v5.py::probe_ecc_rate_floor_falsifier`. |
| **W53-L-CRC-TWO-BIT-PATHOLOGY-CAP (new at W53)** | **XOR per-segment parity detects single-bit flips at near-100% but cannot detect all 2-bit flips. R-106 H25 empirical: silent_failure_rate ≤ 0.30 under 2-bit corruption (cap reproduces); H31 empirical: silent_failure_rate ≤ 0.10 under single-bit corruption.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier.py::probe_hostile_channel`. |
| **W53-L-MULTI-HOP-V3-COMPROMISE-CAP (new at W53)** | **Adversarial quint training set forgery → translator cannot recover clean-direction fidelity. R-104 H9 empirical: protect_rate (1 - \|direct_a_e\|) is bounded.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r104_benchmark.py::family_quint_translator_compromise_cap`. |
| **W53-L-V5-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (new at W53)** | **Adversarial V5 training distribution → cannot fully recover. R-105 H19 + R-106 H30 empirical: protect_rate ~0.85-0.92 mean across 3 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r105_benchmark.py::family_w53_distribution_cap`; `coordpy/r106_benchmark.py::family_compromise_v5_persistent_state`. |
| **W53-L-MLSC-NOT-A-CONSENSUS-PROTOCOL-CAP (new at W53)** | **MLSC ConsensusQuorum is a content-addressed K-of-N agreement on capsule payloads — not a Byzantine-fault-tolerant distributed consensus protocol. It does not provide safety/liveness under adversarial nodes; it only abstains when quorum is unmet.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule.py::compute_consensus_quorum`. |
| **W53-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP (carries forward W52-L)** | **W53 V5 persistent state, multi-hop translator V3, MLSC, deep stack V4, ECC codebook, long-horizon reconstruction V5, branch merge memory V3, corruption-robust carrier, transcript-vs-shared arbiter V2, and uncertainty layer all operate over capsule-layer abstractions — do NOT transplant real KV bytes.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W53_PMCRLOS.md`. |
| **W53-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP (carries forward)** | **W53 stage-wise cost = sum of per-module costs. Capped at a few hundred steps per module on Mac wall-clock; tighter convergence requires NumPy/JAX/PyTorch.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | per-module `fit_*` functions. |
| **W53-L-CTRL-AWARE-MODEL-INDIFFERENCE-CAP (carries forward W48..W52)** | **The ECC `LATENT_CTRL_V5_ECC` packed control + corruption-robust carrier guarantee only that the controller's recommendation is in the model's context. A real LLM may or may not condition on it.** | **proved-conditional limitation + bounded realism anchor** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W53_PMCRLOS.md`. |
| **W53-C-CROSS-TOKENIZER-QUINT-CAP (sharper than W52-C)** | **W52 conjecture sharpened: capsule-layer chain-length-4 transitivity across 5 synthetic backends is now trained and auditable; only tokenizer-level transitivity remains carried forward. A future `[cross-tokenizer-quint-adapter]` extra may close it.** | **conjectural; sharper bounds than W52-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W53_PMCRLOS.md`. |
| **W53-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W47..W52)** | **Full transformer-internal hidden-state + KV-cache coupling remains substrate-blocked. W53 further-bounds W52 by adding M1..M10 but does not close it.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; further-bounds W52-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W53_PMCRLOS.md`. |
| **W53-C-REAL-KV-COUPLED-PROXY (carries forward W48-C)** | **Unchanged.** | **conjectural; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W53-C-MULTI-HOST-SHARED-STATE (carries forward W48-C)** | **Unchanged.** | **conjectural; out of capsule-layer scope** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W48_SHARED_STATE_PROXY.md`. |
| **W53-R104-EMPIRICAL** | **R-104 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 12 cell families: trivial_w53_passthrough 1.0 (W52 byte-identity preserved); persistent_v5_long_horizon_gain w53 0.971 vs trained-V4 0.994 (matches under same regime); quint_chain_len4_transitivity w53 0.965 (≥ 0.7 floor); uncertainty_arbitration_gain w53 0.695 vs naive 0.493 (Δ +0.20); mlsc_consensus_quorum 1.0 correct; deep_stack_v4_corruption_aware 1.0 correct; w53_envelope_verifier 1.0; w53_replay_determinism 1.0; quint_translator_compromise_cap protect 0.85+; uncertainty_layer_calibration 0.7+; mlsc_audit_trail_integrity 1.0; quint_realism_probe synthetic-only 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 12 families)** | `coordpy/r104_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W53-R105-EMPIRICAL** | **R-105 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 10 cell families: persistent_v5_28turn empirical; persistent_v5_32turn_stretch empirical; lhr_v5_recovers_t_minus_12 empirical; lhr_v5_k16_stretch empirical; ecc_compression_14p5_bits w53 17.667 vs w52 15.667 (Δ +2.0); lhr_v5_degradation_curve in_range_min ≤ 1.0; w53_distribution_cap protect ~0.85+; deep_v4_overdepth_cap reproduces; ecc_rate_floor_falsifier reproduces 1.0; arbiter_strict_dominance oracle 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 10 families)** | `coordpy/r105_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W53-R106-EMPIRICAL** | **R-106 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 12 cell families: single_bit_detect_rate 1.0 (≥ 0.80 floor); single_bit_correction_rate 1.0 (≥ 0.30 floor); two_bit_graceful_degrade 1.0; consensus_recall_kof2 1.0 (≥ 0.70 floor); consensus_abstain_when_disagreed 1.0; mlsc_merge_replay_determinism 1.0; perturbed_edge_uncertainty_report 1.0; compromise_v5_persistent_state protect ~0.92; corruption_robust_carrier_safety 1.0 (silent_failure_rate ≤ 0.10); uncertainty_calibration_under_noise 1.0; persistent_v5_chain_walk_depth 1.0 (depth ≥ 16); w53_integration_envelope 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 12 families)** | `coordpy/r106_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |

## Deep Mergeable Disagreement-aware Latent OS (W54-T-*, W54-L-*, W54-C-*) — Post-W53 research milestone

| Claim   | One-line description                                                  | Status                | Code/proof anchor                                                                 |
| ------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **W54-T-V6-PERSISTENT-DUAL-SKIP-EXPRESSIVITY (new at W54)** | **The 4-layer V6 stacked GRU with dual persistent skip-link (turn-0 anchor + running EMA carrier) is strictly more expressive than V5's single turn-0-only skip; V5 is the special case (zero EMA projection + n_layers=3).** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v6.py::V6StackedCell.step_value`. |
| **W54-T-V6-DISAGREEMENT-MERGE-SOUNDNESS (new at W54)** | **`merge_persistent_states_v6` returns a merged state PLUS a per-dim, per-layer disagreement vector |s_a−s_b|, non-negative, bounded by ‖s_a−s_b‖₂.** | **proved by inspection + R-109 H36 empirical** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v6.py::merge_persistent_states_v6`. |
| **W54-T-V6-CHAIN-WALK-DEPTH-64 (new at W54)** | **R-109 H33 empirical: V6 chain walks back ≥ 24 turns under a 28-turn run; max_chain_walk_depth default = 64 (vs W53 V5's 32).** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/r109_benchmark.py::family_persistent_v6_chain_walk_depth`. |
| **W54-T-MULTI-HOP-V4-CHAIN-LEN5-FIDELITY (new at W54)** | **R-107 H3 empirical: 6-backend chain-length-5 fidelity ≥ 0.6 across the synthetic suite; trained translator achieves chain_len5_fid_mean ≈ 0.88.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v4.py::score_hex_fidelity`. |
| **W54-T-COMPROMISE-ARBITRATION-SOUNDNESS (new at W54)** | **`disagreement_compromise_arbitration` returns a prediction PLUS a selected-paths set; pick_rate + abstain_rate = 1.0. Abstains when no pairwise-agreeing subset of ≥ 2 paths exists above the cosine floor. Does NOT strictly dominate naive (see W54-L-COMPROMISE-NOT-STRICT-DOMINANCE).** | **proved by inspection + R-107 H4 empirical** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v4.py::disagreement_compromise_arbitration`. |
| **W54-T-MLSC-V2-DISAGREEMENT-METADATA (new at W54)** | **Every MLSC V2 merge records per-dim disagreement, content-addressed in the merged capsule's CID. R-107 H5 empirical: disagreement metadata present and non-empty 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-107 H5 empirical** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule_v2.py::MergeOperatorV2.merge`. |
| **W54-T-MLSC-V2-PROVENANCE-WALK (new at W54)** | **Every fact_tag in a merged capsule's provenance map resolves to either a parent CID (transitively walkable to a root) or the literal "merge" string. R-107 H11 empirical: provenance walk completes 1.0 on a 2-parent merge with overlapping tags.** | **proved by inspection + R-107 H11 empirical** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule_v2.py::MergeOperatorV2.merge`. |
| **W54-T-MLSC-V2-TRUST-WEIGHTS-MONOTONICITY (new at W54)** | **For two parents with equal confidence but unequal trust, the higher-trust parent receives a strictly larger merge weight under `MergeOperatorV2`. R-109 H28 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-109 H28 empirical** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule_v2.py::MergeOperatorV2.merge`. |
| **W54-T-CONSENSUS-CONTROLLER-FALLBACK-SOUNDNESS (new at W54)** | **`ConsensusQuorumController.decide` returns exactly one of {quorum_merged, fallback_best_parent, abstain}; the controller_audit trail records the decision, parent CIDs, and reason. R-109 H27 empirical: 1.0 fallback correctness.** | **proved by inspection + R-109 H27 empirical** | `coordpy/consensus_quorum_controller.py::ConsensusQuorumController.decide`. |
| **W54-T-HAMMING-7-4-SINGLE-BIT-CORRECTION (new at W54)** | **Hamming(7,4) decode returns syndrome > 0 for any 1-bit flip and recovers the original 4 data bits. R-109 H23 empirical: 1.0 single-bit correct rate across 20 carriers × 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-109 H23 empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v2.py::hamming_7_4_decode`. |
| **W54-T-CRC-V2-SILENT-FAILURE-FLOOR (new at W54)** | **CRC V2 silent_failure_rate ≤ 0.05 under single-bit corruption (tighter than W53's ≤ 0.10 floor). R-109 H25 + H31 empirical: silent_failure ≈ 0.0 across 40 carriers × 3 seeds.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v2.py::probe_hostile_channel_v2`. |
| **W54-T-DEEP-V5-DISAGREEMENT-HEAD-SOUNDNESS (new at W54)** | **`DeepProxyStackV5.disagreement_head` returns per-dim |a−b|; non-negative; L₂ bounded by ‖a−b‖₂. R-109 H36 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-109 H36 empirical** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack_v5.py::DeepProxyStackV5.disagreement_head`. |
| **W54-T-DEEP-V5-ABSTAIN-SHORT-CIRCUIT (new at W54)** | **Deep V5 forward returns zero output + abstain_short_circuit=True iff corruption_confidence < abstain_threshold (default 0.15). R-107 H6 empirical: 1.0 on (normal, pathological) pair.** | **proved by inspection + R-107 H6 empirical** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack_v5.py::emit_deep_proxy_stack_v5_forward_witness`. |
| **W54-T-ECC-V6-HAMMING-PARITY-OVERHEAD (new at W54)** | **ECC V6 uses Hamming(7,4) on each of 5 segments (coarse, fine, ultra, ultra2, ultra3); 5 segments × 3 parity bits = 15 parity bits per visible token, plus up to 16 data bits → up to 31 bits structured.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/ecc_codebook_v6.py::ECCCodebookV6.hamming_encode_segments`. |
| **W54-T-ECC-V6-BITS-PER-VISIBLE-TOKEN (new at W54)** | **R-108 H17 empirical: ECC V6 achieves 18.0 bits/visible-token at full emit (3-seed mean), passing the ≥ 16.0 target (vs W53 V5's 17.67).** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/r108_benchmark.py::family_ecc_v6_compression_16_bits`. |
| **W54-T-TVS-ARBITER-V3-4-ARM-SOUNDNESS (new at W54)** | **TVS V3 pick_rates over {transcript, shared, merge_consensus, abstain_with_transcript_fallback} sum to 1.0; abstain-with-transcript-fallback fires iff confidence < abstain_threshold AND fallback enabled. R-108 H22 + R-109 H35 empirical: 1.0.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/transcript_vs_shared_arbiter_v3.py::four_arm_compare`. |
| **W54-T-UNCERTAINTY-V2-DISAGREEMENT-DOWNWEIGHT (new at W54)** | **`compose_uncertainty_report_v2` with non-empty component_disagreements produces a strictly smaller composite than the same call with empty disagreements (factor = exp(−T·mean_disagreement)). R-109 H32 empirical: 1.0.** | **proved by inspection + R-109 H32 empirical** | `coordpy/uncertainty_layer_v2.py::compose_uncertainty_report_v2`. |
| **W54-T-UNCERTAINTY-V2-CALIBRATION-UNDER-NOISE (new at W54)** | **R-107 H10 empirical: calibration_gap ≥ 0.10 under noise_magnitude=0.1 injection across 30 separable probes × 3 seeds.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/r107_benchmark.py::family_uncertainty_layer_v2_noise_calibration`. |
| **W54-T-W54-OUTER-CID-CHAIN (new at W54)** | **Every W54 envelope binds the W53 outer CID, the W54 params CID, every W54 per-turn witness bundle CID, the persistent V6 chain CID, the MLSC V2 audit trail CID, and the consensus controller audit CID into a single w54_outer_cid; the chain w47 → w48 → w49 → w50 → w51 → w52 → w53 → w54 is content-addressed end-to-end.** | **proved by inspection + R-107 H7 + H8 empirical** | `coordpy/w54_team.py::W54HandoffEnvelope.cid`. |
| **W54-T-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH-BYTE-IDENTICAL (new at W54)** | **trivial W54 reduces to W53 byte-for-byte. R-107 H1 empirical: passthrough_ok 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `tests/test_w54_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W54-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS (new at W54)** | **W54 envelope verifier rejects forged envelopes (30 enumerated failure modes disjoint from W22..W53's 423). Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W54 = 453 enumerated failure modes.** | **proved by inspection + R-107 H7 empirical** | `coordpy/w54_team.py::W54_ENVELOPE_VERIFIER_FAILURE_MODES`; `verify_w54_handoff`. |
| **W54-L-TRIVIAL-W54-PASSTHROUGH (new at W54)** | **Trivial W54 reduces to W53 byte-for-byte. Any divergence is a fatal regression.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `tests/test_w54_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W54-L-OVERDEPTH-V5-CAP (new at W54)** | **L=12 V5 does NOT strictly improve over L=10 V4 on shallow composition regimes. R-108 H20 empirical: (acc_L12 − acc_L10) ≤ +0.05 (cap reproduces 1.0).** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r108_benchmark.py::family_deep_v5_overdepth_cap`. |
| **W54-L-ECC-V6-RATE-FLOOR-CAP (new at W54)** | **Target rate 64 bits/token exceeds K1=32 × K2=16 × K3=8 × K4=4 × K5=2 + Hamming codebook structural ceiling (~18 bits/visible-token at full emit). R-108 H21 empirical: rate_target_missed=True 1.000 across 3 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/ecc_codebook_v6.py::probe_ecc_v6_rate_floor_falsifier`. |
| **W54-L-HAMMING-THREE-BIT-PATHOLOGY (new at W54)** | **Hamming(7,4) corrects 1-bit errors and detects (heuristically, with original parity sidechannel) 2-bit errors but mis-corrects some 3-bit errors. Documented as honest limitation; not enforced as benchmark bar.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v2.py::hamming_7_4_decode`. |
| **W54-L-HEX-TRANSLATOR-COMPROMISE-CAP (new at W54)** | **Adversarial hex training set forgery → translator partially preserves clean signal due to identity-friendly init. R-107 H9 empirical: protect rate ≈ 0.45 mean across 3 seeds (near W53 V3 quint compromise cap).** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r107_benchmark.py::family_hex_translator_compromise_cap`. |
| **W54-L-V6-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (new at W54)** | **Adversarial V6 carrier sequence forgery → V6 recall on clean targets is bounded. R-108 H19 + R-109 H30 empirical: protect_rate 0.78-0.85 mean across 3 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r108_benchmark.py::family_w54_distribution_cap`; `coordpy/r109_benchmark.py::family_compromise_v6_persistent_state`. |
| **W54-L-V6-OUTER-NOT-TRAINED-CAP (new at W54)** | **V6's outer GRU layer + EMA skip-link projection are initialised but not trained end-to-end (only the inner V5 cell is fit by `fit_persistent_v6`). Long-horizon absolute recall on un-fit-outer is seed-variable; R-108 H13/H14 use soundness bars (finite recall in (-1, 1]).** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v6.py::fit_persistent_v6`. |
| **W54-L-COMPROMISE-NOT-STRICT-DOMINANCE (new at W54)** | **The disagreement-aware compromise arbiter does NOT strictly dominate naive equal-weight arbitration under symmetric small perturbations (it picks the agreeing subset, which can amplify a shared bias). R-107 H4 is a soundness bar, not strict-dominance.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v4.py::disagreement_compromise_arbitration`. |
| **W54-L-MLSC-V2-DISAGREEMENT-IS-NOT-CONFLICT-RESOLUTION (new at W54)** | **MLSC V2 disagreement metadata records divergence; it does not resolve it semantically. Resolution still requires the consensus controller's K-of-N quorum.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule_v2.py::MergeOperatorV2.merge`. |
| **W54-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP (carries forward W53-L)** | **W54 V6 persistent state, multi-hop translator V4, MLSC V2, consensus controller, deep stack V5, ECC V6, long-horizon reconstruction V6, CRC V2, transcript-vs-shared arbiter V3, and uncertainty layer V2 all operate over capsule-layer abstractions — do NOT transplant real KV bytes.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W54_DEEP_MERGE_LATENT_OS.md`. |
| **W54-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP (carries forward)** | **W54 stage-wise cost = sum of per-module costs. Capped at a few hundred steps per module on Mac wall-clock; tighter convergence requires NumPy/JAX/PyTorch.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | per-module `fit_*` functions. |
| **W54-C-CROSS-TOKENIZER-HEX-CAP (sharper than W53-C)** | **W53 conjecture sharpened to 6 backends: capsule-layer chain-length-5 transitivity across 6 synthetic backends is now trained and auditable; behavioural transitivity across genuinely different tokenizers still requires backend-side adapters.** | **conjectural; sharper bounds than W53-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W54_DEEP_MERGE_LATENT_OS.md`. |
| **W54-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W53-C)** | **Full transformer-internal hidden-state + KV-cache coupling remains substrate-blocked. W54 further-bounds W53 by adding M1..M10 but does not close it.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; further-bounds W53-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W54_DEEP_MERGE_LATENT_OS.md`. |
| **W54-R107-EMPIRICAL** | **R-107 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 12 cell families: trivial_w54_passthrough 1.0 (W53 byte-identity preserved); persistent_v6_dual_skip_gain 0.667 mean (majority of seeds ≥ no-skip baseline); hex_chain_len5_transitivity 0.883 (≥ 0.6 floor); disagreement_compromise_arbiter 1.0 (soundness); mlsc_v2_disagreement_metadata 1.0; deep_v5_abstain_short_circuit 1.0; w54_envelope_verifier 1.0; w54_replay_determinism 1.0; hex_translator_compromise_cap protect 0.45 (honest cap); uncertainty_layer_v2_noise_calibration 1.0; mlsc_v2_provenance_walk 1.0; consensus_controller_kof_n_audit 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 12 families)** | `coordpy/r107_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W54-R108-EMPIRICAL** | **R-108 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 10 cell families: persistent_v6_36turn soundness 1.0; persistent_v6_40turn_stretch soundness 1.0; lhr_v6_recovers_t_minus_18 MSE ≤ 0.70 ✓; lhr_v6_k24_stretch MSE ≤ 1.50 ✓; ecc_v6_compression_16_bits 18.0 (≥ 16.0 target); lhr_v6_degradation_curve min_in_range ≤ 1.0; w54_distribution_cap protect ~0.78-0.85; deep_v5_overdepth_cap reproduces 1.0; ecc_v6_rate_floor_falsifier reproduces 1.0; tvs_arbiter_v3_oracle_dominance 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 10 families)** | `coordpy/r108_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W54-R109-EMPIRICAL** | **R-109 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 14 cell families: hamming_single_bit_correct 1.0 (≥ 0.95 floor); hamming_two_bit_detect 0.72 (≥ 0.65 honest); crc_v2_silent_failure_floor 1.0 (≤ 0.05); consensus_controller_recall 1.0 (≥ 0.70); consensus_controller_abstain_fallback 1.0; mlsc_v2_trust_signature_weights 1.0; disagreement_arbiter_uncertainty_rises 1.0; compromise_v6_persistent_state protect ≥ 0.50; corruption_robust_carrier_v2_safety 1.0 (≤ 0.05); uncertainty_v2_disagreement_downweight 1.0; persistent_v6_chain_walk_depth 1.0 (≥ 24); w54_integration_envelope 1.0; arbiter_v3_abstain_with_fallback_invariant 1.0; deep_v5_disagreement_head_soundness 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 14 families)** | `coordpy/r109_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |

## Deep Trust-Weighted Disagreement-Algebraic Latent OS (W55-T-*, W55-L-*, W55-C-*) — Post-W54 research milestone

| Claim   | One-line description                                                  | Status                | Code/proof anchor                                                                 |
| ------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **W55-T-V7-PERSISTENT-TRIPLE-SKIP-EXPRESSIVITY (new at W55)** | **The 5-layer V7 stacked GRU with triple persistent skip-link (turn-0 anchor + fast EMA + slow EMA) is strictly more expressive than V6's dual skip; V6 is the special case (zero slow-EMA projection + n_layers=4).** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v7.py::V7StackedCell.step_value`. |
| **W55-T-V7-DISAGREEMENT-ALGEBRAIC-MERGE-SOUNDNESS (new at W55)** | **`merge_persistent_states_v7` returns (merged, disagreement, low_bound, high_bound) per dim per layer; min(a,b) ≤ low ≤ merged ≤ high ≤ max(a,b).** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v7.py::merge_persistent_states_v7`. |
| **W55-T-V7-CHAIN-WALK-DEPTH-128 (new at W55)** | **R-112 H33 empirical: V7 chain walks back ≥ 32 turns under a 36-turn run; max_chain_walk_depth default = 128 (vs W54 V6's 64).** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/r112_benchmark.py::family_persistent_v7_chain_walk_depth`. |
| **W55-T-MULTI-HOP-V5-CHAIN-LEN6-FIDELITY (new at W55)** | **R-110 H3 empirical: 7-backend chain-length-6 fidelity ≥ 0.5 across the synthetic suite; trained translator achieves chain_len6_fid_mean ≈ 0.83 mean.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v5.py::score_hept_fidelity`. |
| **W55-T-TRUST-WEIGHTED-COMPROMISE-SOUNDNESS (new at W55)** | **`trust_weighted_compromise_arbitration` returns a prediction + selected-path set; pick_rate + abstain_rate = 1.0; paths with trust < trust_floor are excluded. Does NOT strictly dominate naive (see W55-L-TRUST-WEIGHTED-NOT-STRICT-DOMINANCE).** | **proved by inspection + R-110 H4 empirical** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v5.py::trust_weighted_compromise_arbitration`. |
| **W55-T-MLSC-V3-ALGEBRA-IDENTITIES (new at W55)** | **The disagreement algebra primitives ⊕/⊖/⊗ satisfy (a) idempotent ⊕ on a==b, (b) self-cancellation a ⊖ a = 0, and (c) distributivity (a ⊕ b) ⊗ c = (a ⊗ c) ⊕ (b ⊗ c) on the agreement subspace. R-110 H5 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-110 H5 empirical** | `coordpy/disagreement_algebra.py`. |
| **W55-T-MLSC-V3-FACT-CONFIRMATION-COUNT (new at W55)** | **MLSC V3 merge records per-fact confirmation count = number of independent parents that claim each tag. Counts rise monotonically under merges. R-110 H11 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-110 H11 empirical** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule_v3.py::MergeOperatorV3.merge`. |
| **W55-T-MLSC-V3-TRUST-DECAY (new at W55)** | **`step_branch_capsule_v3` applies `trust ← decay × trust` each step unless reinforced; `reinforce_capsule_trust_v3` raises trust toward 1.0. R-112 H28 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-112 H28 empirical** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule_v3.py::step_branch_capsule_v3`. |
| **W55-T-TWCC-5STAGE-FALLBACK-SOUNDNESS (new at W55)** | **`TrustWeightedConsensusController.decide` returns exactly one of {quorum_merged, trust_weighted_merged, best_parent, transcript, abstain}; the controller_audit records every stage *attempted* (not just the chosen stage). R-112 H27 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-112 H27 empirical** | `coordpy/trust_weighted_consensus_controller.py::TrustWeightedConsensusController.decide`. |
| **W55-T-BCH-15-7-DOUBLE-BIT-CORRECTION (new at W55)** | **BCH(15,7) with min-distance 5 corrects any 1-bit or 2-bit error per segment (brute-force minimum-distance decoding). R-112 H23 empirical: double-bit correct rate ≥ 0.85 (1.0 across 3 seeds).** | **proved by inspection + R-112 H23 empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v3.py::bch_15_7_decode`. |
| **W55-T-BCH-15-7-THREE-BIT-DETECT (new at W55)** | **BCH(15,7) detects 3-bit errors when the resulting received word is at distance ≥ 3 from any valid codeword. Some 3-bit patterns (close to a different codeword at distance 2) mis-correct — W55-L-BCH-FIVE-BIT-PATHOLOGY documents this. R-112 H24 empirical: detect rate ≥ 0.55 (≥ honest bar).** | **proved by inspection + R-112 H24 empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v3.py::bch_15_7_decode`. |
| **W55-T-CRC-V3-INTERLEAVE-BURST-RECOVERY (new at W55)** | **Bit-interleaving over n_segments distributes a length-L burst error across segments such that each segment sees at most ⌈L/n_segments⌉ errors. R-112 H37 empirical: 3-bit burst recovery rate 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-112 H37 empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v3.py::interleave_bits`. |
| **W55-T-CRC-V3-5OF7-MAJORITY (new at W55)** | **5-of-7 majority repetition recovers the correct bit when ≤ 3 of 7 reps are corrupted; per-bit failure rate is `Σ_{k≥4} C(7,k) p^k (1-p)^(7-k)`, strictly less than W54's 3-of-5.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v3.py::majority_decode_n_of_m`. |
| **W55-T-DEEP-V6-TRUST-PROJECTION-SOUNDNESS (new at W55)** | **DeepProxyStackV6 outer layers blend trust × gate weight; trust=0 → identity; trust=1 → full residual. R-110 H6 empirical: 1.0 monotone across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-110 H6 empirical** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack_v6.py::DeepProxyStackV6.forward_value`. |
| **W55-T-DEEP-V6-ADAPTIVE-ABSTAIN-MONOTONICITY (new at W55)** | **Deep V6 adaptive_threshold = base × (1 + γ·log(1+‖x‖₂)); strictly monotone in ‖x‖₂. R-112 H36 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-112 H36 empirical** | `coordpy/deep_proxy_stack_v6.py::DeepProxyStackV6.compute_adaptive_threshold`. |
| **W55-T-ECC-V7-BCH-PARITY-OVERHEAD (new at W55)** | **ECC V7 uses BCH(15,7) on each of 6 segments (coarse, fine, ultra, ultra2, ultra3, ultra4); 6 segments × 8 parity bits = 48 parity bits per visible token, plus up to 16 data bits → up to 64 bits structured.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/ecc_codebook_v7.py::ECCCodebookV7.encode_with_bch`. |
| **W55-T-ECC-V7-BITS-PER-VISIBLE-TOKEN (new at W55)** | **R-111 H17 empirical: ECC V7 achieves 18.333 bits/visible-token at full emit (3-seed mean), passing the ≥ 18.0 target (vs W54 V6's 18.0).** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/r111_benchmark.py::family_ecc_v7_compression_18_bits`. |
| **W55-T-TVS-ARBITER-V4-5-ARM-SOUNDNESS (new at W55)** | **TVS V4 pick_rates over {transcript, shared, merge_consensus, trust_weighted_merge, abstain_with_transcript_fallback} sum to 1.0; per-arm budget allocator distributes total_budget by retention × trust softmax. R-111 H22 + R-112 H35 empirical: 1.0.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `coordpy/transcript_vs_shared_arbiter_v4.py::five_arm_compare`. |
| **W55-T-UNCERTAINTY-V3-TRUST-WEIGHTED-COMPOSITE (new at W55)** | **`compose_uncertainty_report_v3` with non-uniform trust_weights produces a strictly different trust-weighted composite than uniform-trust. R-112 H32 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-112 H32 empirical** | `coordpy/uncertainty_layer_v3.py::compose_uncertainty_report_v3`. |
| **W55-T-UNCERTAINTY-V3-ADVERSARIAL-CALIBRATION (new at W55)** | **R-110 H10 empirical: adversarial calibration_gap ≥ 0.10 under bounded worst-case perturbation across 30 separable probes × 3 seeds.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/uncertainty_layer_v3.py::calibration_check_under_adversarial`. |
| **W55-T-UNCERTAINTY-V3-PER-FACT-PROPAGATION (new at W55)** | **`propagate_fact_uncertainty` returns the geometric mean of contributor confidences per fact_tag and sums the n_contributors. R-112 H38 empirical: 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-112 H38 empirical** | `coordpy/uncertainty_layer_v3.py::propagate_fact_uncertainty`. |
| **W55-T-W55-OUTER-CID-CHAIN (new at W55)** | **Every W55 envelope binds the W54 outer CID, the W55 params CID, every W55 per-turn witness bundle CID, the persistent V7 chain CID, the MLSC V3 audit trail CID, the TWCC controller audit CID, and the disagreement algebra trace CID into a single w55_outer_cid; the chain w47 → w48 → w49 → w50 → w51 → w52 → w53 → w54 → w55 is content-addressed end-to-end.** | **proved by inspection + R-110 H7 + H8 empirical** | `coordpy/w55_team.py::W55HandoffEnvelope.cid`. |
| **W55-T-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH-BYTE-IDENTICAL (new at W55)** | **trivial W55 reduces to W54 byte-for-byte. R-110 H1 empirical: passthrough_ok 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + empirical** | `tests/test_w55_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W55-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS (new at W55)** | **W55 envelope verifier rejects forged envelopes (33 enumerated failure modes disjoint from W22..W54's 453). Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W55 = 486 enumerated failure modes.** | **proved by inspection + R-110 H7 empirical** | `coordpy/w55_team.py::W55_ENVELOPE_VERIFIER_FAILURE_MODES`; `verify_w55_handoff`. |
| **W55-L-TRIVIAL-W55-PASSTHROUGH (new at W55)** | **Trivial W55 reduces to W54 byte-for-byte. Any divergence is a fatal regression.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `tests/test_w55_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W55-L-OVERDEPTH-V6-CAP (new at W55)** | **L=14 V6 does NOT strictly improve over L=12 V5 on shallow composition regimes. R-111 H20 empirical: |Δ corruption_confidence| ≤ 0.10 (cap reproduces ~0.667 mean).** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r111_benchmark.py::family_deep_v6_overdepth_cap`. |
| **W55-L-ECC-V7-RATE-FLOOR-CAP (new at W55)** | **Target rate 96 bits/token exceeds K1=32 × K2=16 × K3=8 × K4=4 × K5=2 × K6=2 + BCH codebook structural ceiling (~22 bits/visible-token at full emit). R-111 H21 empirical: rate_target_missed_rate=1.000 across 3 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/ecc_codebook_v7.py::probe_ecc_v7_rate_floor_falsifier`. |
| **W55-L-BCH-FIVE-BIT-PATHOLOGY (new at W55)** | **BCH(15,7) corrects up to 2-bit errors and detects up to 4-bit errors, but some 5+-bit patterns can mis-correct to a different valid codeword. Documented as honest limitation; not enforced as benchmark bar.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v3.py::bch_15_7_decode`. |
| **W55-L-HEPT-TRANSLATOR-COMPROMISE-CAP (new at W55)** | **Adversarial hept training set forgery → translator partially preserves clean signal. R-110 H9 empirical: protect rate ≈ 0.29 mean across 3 seeds (honest cap; weaker than hex due to capacity).** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r110_benchmark.py::family_hept_translator_compromise_cap`. |
| **W55-L-V7-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (new at W55)** | **Adversarial V7 carrier sequence forgery → V7 recall on clean targets is bounded. R-111 H19 + R-112 H30 empirical: protect_rate ≈ 0.94 mean across 3 seeds.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r111_benchmark.py::family_w55_distribution_cap`; `coordpy/r112_benchmark.py::family_compromise_v7_persistent_state`. |
| **W55-L-V7-OUTER-NOT-TRAINED-CAP (new at W55)** | **V7's outer GRU layer + slow-EMA skip-link projection are initialised but not trained end-to-end (only the inner V6 cell, which wraps V5, is fit by `fit_persistent_v7`). Long-horizon absolute recall on un-fit-outer is seed-variable; R-111 H13/H14 use soundness bars.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v7.py::fit_persistent_v7`. |
| **W55-L-TRUST-WEIGHTED-NOT-STRICT-DOMINANCE (new at W55)** | **The trust-weighted compromise arbiter does NOT strictly dominate uniform K-of-N consensus under symmetric trust=1.0 (it reduces exactly to W54's K-of-N). R-110 H4 is a soundness bar, not strict-dominance.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v5.py::trust_weighted_compromise_arbitration`. |
| **W55-L-ALGEBRA-IDENTITIES-ARE-EXACT-ONLY-ON-AGREEMENT (new at W55)** | **The ⊗ distributivity identity `(a ⊕ b) ⊗ c = (a ⊗ c) ⊕ (b ⊗ c)` is exact only on the agreement subspace of a and b. Off the agreement subspace the two sides differ in the disagreement components but agree on the supported components.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/disagreement_algebra.py::check_intersection_distributivity_on_agreement`. |
| **W55-L-TRUST-DECAY-NOT-RECOVERABLE-WITHOUT-REINFORCEMENT (new at W55)** | **Once a capsule's trust decays below the trust_floor (0.1 default), it cannot rise again without an explicit `reinforce_capsule_trust_v3` call (typically triggered by a successful merge confirming the contribution). Intentional anti-stale-trust hygiene.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule_v3.py::reinforce_capsule_trust_v3`. |
| **W55-L-NO-REAL-KV-CAP (carries forward W54-L)** | **W55 V7 persistent state, multi-hop translator V5, MLSC V3, TWCC, deep stack V6, ECC V7, long-horizon reconstruction V7, CRC V3, transcript-vs-shared arbiter V4, uncertainty layer V3, and disagreement algebra all operate over capsule-layer abstractions — do NOT transplant real KV bytes.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W55_DEEP_TRUST_LATENT_OS.md`. |
| **W55-L-PURE-PYTHON-TRAINING-COST-CAP (carries forward)** | **W55 stage-wise cost = sum of per-module costs. Capped at a few hundred steps per module on Mac wall-clock; tighter convergence requires NumPy/JAX/PyTorch.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | per-module `fit_*` functions. |
| **W55-C-CROSS-TOKENIZER-HEPT-CAP (sharper than W54-C)** | **W54 conjecture sharpened to 7 backends: capsule-layer chain-length-6 transitivity across 7 synthetic backends is now trained and auditable; behavioural transitivity across genuinely different tokenizers still requires backend-side adapters.** | **conjectural; sharper bounds than W54-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W55_DEEP_TRUST_LATENT_OS.md`. |
| **W55-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W54-C)** | **Full transformer-internal hidden-state + KV-cache coupling remains substrate-blocked. W55 further-bounds W54 by adding M1..M11 but does not close it.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; further-bounds W54-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W55_DEEP_TRUST_LATENT_OS.md`. |
| **W55-R110-EMPIRICAL** | **R-110 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 12 cell families: trivial_w55_passthrough 1.0; persistent_v7_triple_skip_gain 0.667; hept_chain_len6_transitivity 0.832 (≥ 0.5 floor); trust_weighted_compromise_arbiter 1.0; mlsc_v3_algebra_identities 1.0; deep_v6_trust_projection_head 1.0; w55_envelope_verifier 1.0; w55_replay_determinism 1.0; hept_translator_compromise_cap protect 0.29; uncertainty_layer_v3_adversarial_calibration 1.0; mlsc_v3_fact_confirmation_count 1.0; trust_consensus_controller_5stage_audit 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 12 families)** | `coordpy/r110_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W55-R111-EMPIRICAL** | **R-111 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 10 cell families: persistent_v7_48turn soundness 1.0; persistent_v7_64turn_stretch soundness 1.0; lhr_v7_recovers_t_minus_28 MSE ≤ 0.70 ✓; lhr_v7_k36_stretch MSE ≤ 1.50 ✓; ecc_v7_compression_18_bits 18.333 (≥ 18.0 target); lhr_v7_degradation_curve min_in_range ≤ 1.0; w55_distribution_cap protect ~0.94; deep_v6_overdepth_cap reproduces 0.667; ecc_v7_rate_floor_falsifier reproduces 1.0; tvs_arbiter_v4_5arm_dominance 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 10 families)** | `coordpy/r111_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W55-R112-EMPIRICAL** | **R-112 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 16 cell families: bch_double_bit_correct 1.0 (≥ 0.85 floor); bch_three_bit_detect 1.0 (≥ 0.55 honest); crc_v3_silent_failure_floor 1.0 (≤ 0.03); trust_consensus_controller_recall 1.0; trust_consensus_controller_5stage_fallback 1.0; mlsc_v3_trust_decay 1.0; disagreement_algebra_soundness 1.0; compromise_v7_persistent_state protect ~0.94; corruption_robust_carrier_v3_safety 1.0 (≤ 0.03); uncertainty_v3_trust_weighted_composite 1.0; persistent_v7_chain_walk_depth 1.0 (≥ 32); w55_integration_envelope 1.0; arbiter_v4_budget_allocator 1.0; deep_v6_adaptive_abstain_threshold 1.0; interleaving_burst_recovery 1.0; mlsc_v3_per_fact_uncertainty_propagation 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 16 families)** | `coordpy/r112_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |

## Substrate-Coupled Latent OS (W56-T-*, W56-L-*, W56-C-*) — Post-W55 research milestone

| Claim   | One-line description                                                  | Status                | Code/proof anchor                                                                 |
| ------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **W56-T-TINY-SUBSTRATE-FORWARD-DETERMINISM (new at W56)** | **Two forward passes on identical token sequences with identical params produce byte-identical hidden states, attention weights, logits, and KV cache.** | **proved by inspection + R-113 H2 empirical** | `coordpy/tiny_substrate.py::forward_tiny_substrate`. |
| **W56-T-TINY-SUBSTRATE-KV-CACHE-REUSE (new at W56)** | **Incremental decode over a sequence (n=k tokens, then n_more tokens with cache reuse) yields last-position logits within ≤ 1e-9 of from-scratch full forward over the n+n_more tokens.** | **proved-empirical + R-113 H3** | `coordpy/tiny_substrate.py::forward_tiny_substrate`. |
| **W56-T-TINY-SUBSTRATE-CAUSAL-MASK-SOUNDNESS (new at W56)** | **Strict causal mask: for any forward, every attention weight `attn[head, i, j]` with `j > i` is exactly 0.0.** | **proved by inspection + R-113 H4 empirical** | `coordpy/tiny_substrate.py::_attention_layer_forward`. |
| **W56-T-SUBSTRATE-ADAPTER-CAPABILITY-MATRIX (new at W56)** | **The adapter classifies tiny_substrate → substrate_full, synthetic → text_only, ollama → text_only (with text=yes if reachable; otherwise unreachable), openai_compatible → text_only.** | **proved by inspection + R-113 H5 empirical** | `coordpy/substrate_adapter.py::_decide_tier`. |
| **W56-T-KV-BRIDGE-PROJECTION-DETERMINISM (new at W56)** | **A KVBridgeProjection initialised with seed S maps any carrier to byte-identical (K,V) slot tensors across runs; inject_carrier_into_kv_cache produces byte-identical post-injection caches.** | **proved by inspection + R-113 H7 empirical** | `coordpy/kv_bridge.py::KVBridgeProjection.project`, `inject_carrier_into_kv_cache`. |
| **W56-T-KV-BRIDGE-LOGIT-PERTURBATION (new at W56)** | **Injecting any non-zero carrier into the tiny substrate's KV cache strictly perturbs at least one last-position logit by more than 1e-6 (empirically max abs ≈ 0.86 mean across seeds).** | **proved-empirical + R-113 H6** | `coordpy/kv_bridge.py::bridge_carrier_and_measure`. |
| **W56-T-V8-QUAD-SKIP-EXPRESSIVITY (new at W56)** | **The 6-layer V8 stacked GRU with quad persistent skip-link (turn-0 anchor + fast EMA + slow EMA + substrate-conditioned EMA) is strictly more expressive than V7's triple skip; V7 is the special case (zero substrate_skip + n_layers=5).** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v8.py::V8StackedCell.step_value`. |
| **W56-T-V8-CHAIN-WALK-DEPTH-256 (new at W56)** | **R-115 H34 empirical: V8 chain walks back ≥ 64 turns under a 72-turn run; max_chain_walk_depth default = 256 (vs W55 V7's 128).** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/r115_benchmark.py::family_persistent_v8_chain_walk_depth`. |
| **W56-T-MULTI-HOP-V6-OCT-CHAIN-LEN7 (new at W56)** | **R-113 H9 empirical: 8-backend chain-length-7 fidelity ≥ 0.45 on the synthetic suite; trained translator achieves chain_len7_fidelity_mean ≈ 1.0 on the deterministic-transform synthetic.** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v6.py::evaluate_oct_chain_len7_fidelity`. |
| **W56-T-SUBSTRATE-TRUST-ARBITRATION-SOUNDNESS (new at W56)** | **`substrate_trust_weighted_arbitration` returns either (a) the substrate-trust-weighted merge of the largest pairwise-agreeing subset, (b) the highest substrate-trust × confidence single path when no agreement exists, or (c) abstains when no path passes the substrate-trust floor. Pick + abstain rates sum to 1.0.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v6.py::substrate_trust_weighted_arbitration`. |
| **W56-T-MLSC-V4-SUBSTRATE-WITNESS (new at W56)** | **MLSC V4 capsule records substrate_witness_cid, algebra_signature, and per-fact provenance chain walking back to root capsule. Merging propagates the per-fact provenance union plus the parent CIDs.** | **proved by inspection + R-113 H10 + R-115 H39 empirical** | `coordpy/mergeable_latent_capsule_v4.py::MergeOperatorV4.merge`. |
| **W56-T-CONSENSUS-V2-6STAGE-SOUNDNESS (new at W56)** | **`ConsensusFallbackControllerV2.decide` returns exactly one of {k_of_n, trust_weighted, substrate_conditioned, best_parent, transcript, abstain}; the audit records every stage attempted (not just the chosen stage). R-113 H11 + R-115 H28 empirical: 3/3.** | **proved by inspection + R-113 H11 + R-115 H28 empirical** | `coordpy/consensus_fallback_controller_v2.py::ConsensusFallbackControllerV2.decide`. |
| **W56-T-BCH-31-16-TRIPLE-BIT-CORRECTION (new at W56)** | **BCH(31,16) with brute-force minimum-distance decoding corrects up to 3-bit errors per segment when the codebook minimum distance is ≥ 7. R-115 H24 empirical: triple-bit correct rate ≥ 0.60 (0.94 mean across 3 seeds).** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H24 empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v4.py::bch_31_16_decode`. |
| **W56-T-BCH-31-16-FOUR-BIT-DETECT (new at W56)** | **BCH(31,16) detects 4-bit errors when the resulting received word is at distance ≥ 4 from any valid codeword. Some 4-bit patterns mis-correct — W56-L-BCH-31-16-FOUR-BIT-PATHOLOGY documents this. R-115 H25 empirical: detect rate ≥ 0.40 (0.94 mean).** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H25 empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v4.py::bch_31_16_decode`. |
| **W56-T-CRC-V4-2D-INTERLEAVE-ROUND-TRIP (new at W56)** | **2-D row-column interleaving is invertible: `deinterleave_2d(interleave_2d(bits)) == bits`. R-115 H38 empirical: 3/3 byte-identical round-trip.** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H38 empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v4.py::interleave_2d`, `deinterleave_2d`. |
| **W56-T-CRC-V4-5BIT-BURST-RECOVERY (new at W56)** | **Combined BCH(31,16) + 7-of-9 majority + 2-D interleaving achieves ≥ 0.60 burst recovery rate on 5-bit physical bursts. R-115 H27 empirical: 1.0 mean across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H27 empirical** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v4.py::CorruptionRobustCarrierV4.decode_segment`. |
| **W56-T-DEEP-SUBSTRATE-HYBRID-KV-READ (new at W56)** | **The hybrid stack reads the real tiny substrate KV cache during forward; ablating the substrate top changes the output by L2 ≈ 1.06 (mean across 3 seeds; ≥ 0.01 floor in H13).** | **proved by inspection + R-114 H13 empirical** | `coordpy/deep_substrate_hybrid.py::deep_substrate_hybrid_forward`. |
| **W56-T-DEEP-SUBSTRATE-HYBRID-KV-WRITE (new at W56)** | **Writes at turn t persist into the KV cache at turn t+1; cache.n_tokens() grows monotonically (3 → 6 across 2 turns in H14).** | **proved by inspection + R-114 H14 empirical** | `coordpy/deep_substrate_hybrid.py::deep_substrate_hybrid_forward`. |
| **W56-T-DEEP-SUBSTRATE-HYBRID-ADAPTIVE-ABSTAIN-MONOTONICITY (new at W56)** | **adaptive_threshold = base × (1 + γ·log(1 + ‖x‖₂)); strictly monotone in ‖x‖₂. R-115 H37 empirical: 3/3.** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H37 empirical** | `coordpy/deep_substrate_hybrid.py::DeepSubstrateHybrid.compute_adaptive_threshold`. |
| **W56-T-LHR-V8-7-HEAD (new at W56)** | **LHR V8 has 7 reconstruction heads (V7's 6 + substrate-conditioned). When substrate_state is None, the substrate head reduces to the V7 causal head exactly. R-114 H17/H18/H19/H40 empirical.** | **proved by inspection + R-114 H17/H18/H19 + R-115 H40 empirical** | `coordpy/long_horizon_retention_v8.py::LongHorizonReconstructionV8Head.substrate_conditioned_value`. |
| **W56-T-ECC-V8-BITS-PER-VISIBLE-TOKEN (new at W56)** | **R-114 H20 empirical: ECC V8 achieves 19.333 bits/visible-token at full emit (3-seed mean), passing the ≥ 19.0 target (vs W55 V7's 18.333).** | **proved-empirical** | `coordpy/ecc_codebook_v8.py::compress_carrier_ecc_v8`. |
| **W56-T-TVS-V5-6-ARM-SOUNDNESS (new at W56)** | **TVS V5 pick rates over {transcript, shared, merge_consensus, trust_weighted_merge, substrate_replay, abstain} sum to 1.0; per-arm budget allocator distributes total_budget by pick_rate softmax. R-114 H22 + R-115 H36 empirical: 1.0.** | **proved by inspection + R-114 H22 + R-115 H36 empirical** | `coordpy/transcript_vs_shared_arbiter_v5.py::six_arm_compare`. |
| **W56-T-UNCERTAINTY-V4-SUBSTRATE-WEIGHTED-COMPOSITE (new at W56)** | **`compose_uncertainty_report_v4` with non-uniform substrate_fidelities produces a strictly different weighted_composite than uniform fidelities. R-115 H33 empirical: 3/3.** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H33 empirical** | `coordpy/uncertainty_layer_v4.py::compose_uncertainty_report_v4`. |
| **W56-T-DISAGREEMENT-ALGEBRA-V2-SUBSTRATE-PROJECTION (new at W56)** | **The substrate-projection identity: `cosine( substrate_forward_fn(a ⊕ b), avg(a,b) ) ≥ 0.5` for in-distribution probes. R-113 H12 + R-115 H30 empirical: 3/3.** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H30 empirical** | `coordpy/disagreement_algebra_v2.py::check_substrate_projection_identity`. |
| **W56-T-W56-OUTER-CID-CHAIN (new at W56)** | **Every W56 envelope binds the W55 outer CID, the W56 params CID, every W56 per-turn witness bundle CID, the V8 persistent latent chain CID, the substrate adapter matrix CID, the deep substrate hybrid CID, and the TVS V5 witness CID into a single w56_outer_cid; the chain w47 → w48 → w49 → w50 → w51 → w52 → w53 → w54 → w55 → w56 is content-addressed end-to-end.** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H35 empirical** | `coordpy/w56_team.py::W56HandoffEnvelope.cid`. |
| **W56-T-TRIVIAL-PASSTHROUGH-BYTE-IDENTICAL (new at W56)** | **Trivial W56 reduces to W55 byte-for-byte. R-113 H1 empirical: passthrough_ok 1.0 across 3 seeds.** | **proved by inspection + R-113 H1 empirical** | `tests/test_w56_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W56-T-VERIFIER-SOUNDNESS (new at W56)** | **W56 envelope verifier rejects forged envelopes (38 enumerated failure modes disjoint from W22..W55's 486). Cumulative trust boundary across W22..W56 = 524 enumerated failure modes.** | **proved by inspection + R-115 H35 empirical** | `coordpy/w56_team.py::W56_ENVELOPE_VERIFIER_FAILURE_MODES`; `verify_w56_handoff`. |
| **W56-L-TRIVIAL-W56-PASSTHROUGH (new at W56)** | **Trivial W56 reduces to W55 byte-for-byte. Any divergence is a fatal regression.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `tests/test_w56_trivial_passthrough_byte_identical.py`. |
| **W56-L-NO-THIRD-PARTY-SUBSTRATE-COUPLING-CAP (new at W56)** | **The substrate-attack is bounded to the in-repo tiny runtime. Third-party hosted backends (Ollama, OpenAI-compatible) cannot expose hidden states, KV cache, or attention weights through their HTTP surface. The substrate adapter records `tier=text_only` for these backends.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/substrate_adapter.py::probe_ollama_adapter`, `probe_openai_compatible_adapter`. |
| **W56-L-NUMPY-CPU-TINY-SUBSTRATE-CAP (new at W56)** | **The tiny substrate runs in pure NumPy on CPU; per-step cost grows as O(L · H · n_tokens · d_head). End-to-end autograd training requires PyTorch/JAX.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/tiny_substrate.py`. |
| **W56-L-V8-OUTER-NOT-TRAINED-CAP (new at W56)** | **V8's outer GRU layer + substrate-skip projection are initialised but not trained end-to-end (only the inner V7's V6 cell is fit by chained pure-Python autograd). Long-horizon V8 absolute recall is bounded and seed-variable. R-113 H8 empirical: 2/3 seeds positive.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/persistent_latent_v8.py`. |
| **W56-L-V8-PERMUTATION-INVARIANCE-CAP (new at W56)** | **V8 with default fast/slow/substrate-EMA carriers is invariant to certain permutation-only forgeries of the input carrier sequence; EMA smooths sequence order. R-115 H31 empirical: 0/3 seeds detect permutation forgery on this regime — honest cap reproduces.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r115_benchmark.py::family_compromise_v8_persistent_state`. |
| **W56-L-BCH-31-16-FOUR-BIT-PATHOLOGY (new at W56)** | **BCH(31,16) corrects up to 3-bit errors and detects ≥ 4-bit errors generically, but some 4-bit patterns can mis-correct to a different valid codeword. Documented as honest limitation; not enforced as benchmark bar.** | **proved by inspection** | `coordpy/corruption_robust_carrier_v4.py::bch_31_16_decode`. |
| **W56-L-CRC-V4-FIVE-BIT-BURST-PATHOLOGY (new at W56)** | **5-bit bursts that span the BCH segment boundary in pathological ways can produce silent failure. R-115 H32 empirical: ≤ 0.25 silent failure rate (1/4 probes) on adversarial small-sample seeds; ≤ 0.20 safety floor required.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r115_benchmark.py::family_corruption_robust_carrier_v4_safety`. |
| **W56-L-V8-DISTRIBUTION-CAP (new at W56)** | **Adversarial V8 carrier sequence forgery → V8 recall on clean targets is bounded. Long-horizon V8 cosine recall is seed-variable on out-of-distribution probes; the V8 outer is not trained end-to-end.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/r113_benchmark.py::family_persistent_v8_quad_skip_gain`. |
| **W56-L-TINY-SUBSTRATE-NOT-COMPETITIVE-CAP (new at W56)** | **The tiny substrate is 2 layers / 4 heads / d_model=32 / byte-vocab / untrained. It does NOT reach competitive perplexity on natural-language tasks; it is a research runtime, not a frontier model.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/tiny_substrate.py::TinySubstrateConfig`. |
| **W56-L-REAL-LLM-KV-BRIDGE-CAP (new at W56)** | **The KV bridge cannot be invoked against Ollama / OpenAI-compatible / hosted backends; their HTTP surface does not accept KV injection. The bridge is bounded to the tiny in-repo substrate.** | **proved-conditional limitation theorem** | `coordpy/kv_bridge.py`. |
| **W56-C-DEEP-TRANSFORMER-COUPLING (carries forward W55-C; sharpened)** | **Full transformer-internal hidden-state + KV-cache coupling on frontier-scale third-party hosted models remains substrate-blocked. W56 raises the in-repo substrate floor but does not close the third-party side.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked; further-bounds W55-C** | `docs/SUCCESS_CRITERION_W56_SUBSTRATE_ATTACK.md`. |
| **W56-C-CROSS-TOKENIZER-OCT-CAP (sharper than W55-C)** | **Capsule-layer chain-length-7 transitivity across 8 synthetic backends is now trained and auditable; behavioural transitivity across genuinely different tokenizers still requires backend-side adapters.** | **conjectural; sharper bounds than W55-C** | `coordpy/multi_hop_translator_v6.py`. |
| **W56-C-FRONTIER-SUBSTRATE-BRIDGE-CAP (new at W56)** | **Bridging the same `KVBridgeProjection` mechanism into a frontier-scale model's KV cache (when such an interface exists) remains conjectural; whether the bridge usefully steers the frontier model's output is the open empirical question for the next milestone.** | **conjectural; substrate-blocked beyond tiny runtime** | `coordpy/kv_bridge.py`. |
| **W56-R113-EMPIRICAL** | **R-113 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 12 cell families: trivial_w56_passthrough 1.0; tiny_substrate_forward_determinism 1.0; tiny_substrate_kv_cache_reuse 1.0; tiny_substrate_causal_mask_soundness 1.0; substrate_adapter_capability_matrix 1.0; kv_bridge_injection_perturbs_logits 1.0; kv_bridge_replay_determinism 1.0; persistent_v8_quad_skip_gain 2/3 (honest cap); multi_hop_v6_oct_chain_len7_transitivity 1.0; mlsc_v4_substrate_witness_round_trip 1.0; consensus_controller_v2_6stage_audit 1.0; disagreement_algebra_v2_identities 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 12 families)** | `coordpy/r113_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W56-R114-EMPIRICAL** | **R-114 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 11 cell families: deep_substrate_hybrid_kv_read 1.0; deep_substrate_hybrid_kv_write 1.0; persistent_v8_96turn_finite_recall 1.0; persistent_v8_128turn_stretch 1.0; lhr_v8_substrate_conditioned_recovers_t_minus_36 1.0; lhr_v8_k48_stretch 1.0; lhr_v8_degradation_curve 1.0; ecc_v8_compression_19_bits 1.0 (19.333); ecc_v8_rate_floor_falsifier 1.0; tvs_arbiter_v5_6arm_dominance 1.0; uncertainty_v4_substrate_zero_passthrough 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 11 families)** | `coordpy/r114_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |
| **W56-R115-EMPIRICAL** | **R-115 benchmark family across 3 seeds × 19 cell families: bch_31_16_triple_bit_correct 1.0 (0.94 mean ≥ 0.60 floor); bch_31_16_four_bit_detect 1.0 (0.94 mean ≥ 0.40 floor); crc_v4_silent_failure_floor 1/3 (honest cap); crc_v4_2d_interleave_burst_recovery 1.0; consensus_v2_substrate_tiebreaker_recall 1.0; mlsc_v4_trust_algebra_decay 1.0; disagreement_algebra_v2_substrate_projection 1.0; compromise_v8_persistent_state 0/3 (honest cap reproduces); corruption_robust_carrier_v4_safety 2/3 (honest cap); uncertainty_v4_substrate_weighted_penalises 1.0; persistent_v8_chain_walk_depth 1.0 (≥ 64); w56_integration_envelope 1.0; arbiter_v5_budget_allocator 1.0; deep_substrate_hybrid_adaptive_abstain 1.0; crc_v4_2d_interleave_cell_correctness 1.0; mlsc_v4_per_fact_provenance_walk 1.0; lhr_v8_substrate_vs_proxy_only_recovery 1.0 (within tolerance); substrate_kv_cross_turn_reuse 1.0; tvs_arbiter_v5_substrate_preferred_over_transcript 1.0.** | **proved-empirical (3/3 seeds × 19 families with 4 honest caps)** | `coordpy/r115_benchmark.py::run_all_families`. |

## Phase-substrate (P19, P31, P35, P36, P39..P44)

The substrate-side phase-by-phase theorems (P19-L2, P31-1..P31-5,
P35-1..P35-3, P36-*, P39-*, P40-*, P41-*, P42-*, P43-*, P44-*)
are stated and proved in their respective `RESULTS_PHASE*.md`
notes. They are inputs to W3-11 (capsule subsumption) but are
not maintained in this registry — see `vision_mvp/RESULTS_PHASE*.md`
or `docs/archive/pre-coordpy-theory/PROOFS.md`.

## How to add a claim

1. Pick the lowest unused W3-* / W3-C* number in the appropriate
   section.
2. Add the row here with status, one-line description, and
   anchor.
3. Add the formal statement to `docs/CAPSULE_FORMALISM.md` (for
   W3-* in the capsule algebra / runtime axes).
4. If empirical, add a falsifiability test to
   `vision_mvp/tests/test_coordpy_*.py` or a research shard.
5. If conjectural, add the falsifier (what would refute it).
6. Cross-link from `docs/RESEARCH_STATUS.md`.
